**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **Zernike polynomial wavefront fitting** (OPTICS-ZERNIKE-WAVEFRONT-FIT): first 15 Noll-ordered terms (j=1..15, piston through tetrafoil); explicit Z_j(¤ü,╬Ş) formulas (Noll 1976 Table 1 orthonormal basis); least-squares fit via numpy.linalg.lstsq; RMS residual; dominant aberration = argmax(|c_j|) for jÔëą2 (piston excluded); LLM tool `optics_fit_zernike_wavefront`; 32 hermetic tests. Honest: unit-disk pupil only; first 15 terms only ÔÇö higher-order content aliases into residual; no wavefront OPD tracing (sampled W(¤ü,╬Ş) input only). Ref: Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207; Born & Wolf ┬ž9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **sequential paraxial + meridional ray trace** through multi-element lens stacks (Welford 1986 ┬ž3.3/┬ž5, exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; EFL/BFL/FFL; Hecht oracle biconvex BK7 <0.1% error; Cooke triplet converging verified); **MTF across field angle** (OPTICS-MTF-ACROSS-FIELD) ÔÇö ray-bundle PSF histogram + numpy.fft.rfft pipeline; tangential MTF curves at multiple field angles; BK7 biconvex off-axis MTF drop verified; LLM tool `optics_mtf_across_field` (monochromatic; polychromatic MTF out of scope).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); **Seidel third-order aberrations** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-ABERRATIONS): five Seidel coefficients S_I..S_V via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬ž6.2 / Born & Wolf ┬ž5.3); per-surface breakdown; LLM tool `optics_seidel_aberrations`; 33 hermetic tests.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Chief-ray vignetting + relative illumination** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-VIGNETTING): marginal-ray bundle traced at each field angle; per-surface clear-aperture clipping check; RI = surviving fraction; cosÔü┤(╬Ş) photometric baseline; excess-vignetting ratio; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting` (Welford 1986 ┬ž4.5 / Hecht ┬ž6.6; circular symmetric apertures; 33 hermetic tests).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid ├Ś grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes ╬Ş = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(╬Ş) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model) + cos4_map (natural cosÔü┤(╬Ş) photometric baseline, Hecht ┬ž6.6 / Slyusarev ┬ž3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm Ôćĺ ╬Ş_corner Ôëł 60┬░, cos4_corner Ôëł 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; rotationally-symmetric stack assumed; sensor tilt / telecentricity not modelled. Ref: Welford 1986 ┬ž4.5; Hecht ┬ž6.6; Slyusarev ┬ž3.4.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Spot diagrams + pupil illumination maps** (OPTICS-PUPIL-DIAGRAM): uniform pupil-grid ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬ž8.2); per-field intercept loci at image plane; 2-D RMS + meridional y-only RMS spot radius; max ray distance from chief ray; exit-pupil illumination map (surviving pupil coords); paraxial exit-pupil position estimate (Welford 1986 ┬ž3.5 / Hecht ┬ž5.7); stigmatic stack Ôćĺ RMS < 1e-6 mm; BK7 biconvex at 14┬░ Ôćĺ y-RMS > 3├Ś on-axis; Seidel coma cross-check; LLM tool `optics_pupil_diagram` (monochromatic; sagittal x = first-order estimate; 33 hermetic tests).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Through-focus defocus curve** (OPTICS-DEFOCUS-CURVE): Welford 1986 ┬ž11.5 / Hecht ┬ž6.5; per-╬öz meridional RMS spot-size via exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; best-focus shift quantified; parabolic curve verified for paraxial singlet (min at ╬öz=0); spherical-aberration-shifted minimum verified for full-aperture BK7 singlet (╬özÔëłÔłĺ0.5 mm); field-angle dependency; LLM tool `optics_defocus_curve`; 33 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; meridional (tangential) RMS only; astigmatic sagittal/tangential splitting not implemented.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Geometric distortion map** (OPTICS-DISTORTION-MAP): chief-ray tangential distortion vs field angle (Hecht ┬ž5.6 / Welford 1986 ┬ž6.3); D=(y_actualÔłĺy_paraxial)/|y_paraxial|├Ś100; barrel (D<0) / pincushion (D>0) / mixed classification; Seidel S_V third-order cross-check (Welford ┬ž6.3); BK7 biconvex singlet shows measurable barrel distortion at moderate field (>0.5% at 20┬░); kind classification verified for high-power singlet and telephoto stacks; LLM tool `optics_distortion_map`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; tangential (meridional) distortion only; stop assumed at first surface.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Coma aberration metrics** (OPTICS-COMA-COMPUTE): comatic flare length from pupil-rim ray bundle trace (Welford 1986 ┬ž11.4 / Born & Wolf ┬ž5.3); for each field angle traces N marginal rays at entrance-pupil rim azimuths and propagates to paraxial focal plane; tangential coma = mean Y-displacement of tangential-fan rays from chief-ray image point; sagittal coma = tangential/3 (Welford ┬ž11.4 eq. 11.4.4); total coma = sqrt(tan┬▓+sag┬▓); Seidel S_II prediction = 3├Ś|S_II|├Ś|y_chief| (Born & Wolf ┬ž5.3 eq. 5.3.29); depth bar: BK7 biconvex at 14┬░ Ôćĺ coma > 1 ╬╝m; Seidel match < 0.1% at 5┬░ field; LLM tool `optics_compute_coma`; 33 hermetic tests. Honest: third-order coma only; higher-order (Hopkins 5th-order, oblique spherical aberration) requires finite-ray OPD analysis; monochromatic only; stop at first surface.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Seidel coma coefficient S_II** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-COMA): per-surface third-order Seidel coma sum S_II = ╬ú (ÔłĺA_j┬Ě─Ç_j┬Ěh_j┬Ě╬ö(u/n)_j) via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬ž7 eq. 7.42 / Born & Wolf ┬ž5.3); SeidelComaReport dataclass: S_II (total Seidel coma sum), coma_waves_at_lambda (|3┬ĚS_II┬Ěy_chief|/(8╬╗)), dominant_surface_idx (argmax|S_II_j|), per_surface_contributions (A, ─Ç, h, ybar, delta_un, SII_contrib per surface), honest_caveat; BK7 biconvex R1=+50/R2=Ôłĺ50 mm on-axis Ôćĺ coma_waves = 0; same lens at 5┬░ Ôćĺ S_II nonzero; aplanatic BK7+SF2 contact doublet Ôćĺ |S_II| reduced vs singlet; flat slab Ôćĺ S_II = 0 exactly; LLM tool `optics_compute_seidel_coma`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial Seidel only; no chromatic coma; no defocus residual; stop at first surface; higher-order coma not modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž7 eq. 7.42; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬ž5.3 eq. 5.3.29; Kingslake (1978).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Seidel coma coefficient (thin-lens polynomial)** (OPTICS-COMA-COEFFICIENT): closed-form S_II and Hopkins W_131 for a single thin lens via Welford ┬ž7.4 shape-factor/conjugate-factor polynomial; `ThinLensSpec(focal_length_mm, refractive_index_n, aperture_radius_mm, shape_factor_q, conjugate_factor_p)` + `ImageSpec(object_height_mm, image_distance_mm)` Ôćĺ `ComaCoefficientReport(seidel_S_II, wave_aberration_W_131, sagittal_coma_arcsec, tangential_coma_arcsec=3├Śsagittal, coma_blur_mm, q_aplanatic, honest_caveat)`; formula: S_II = u_bar┬Ěh┬│┬Ě¤ć┬▓┬Ě[(n+1)/(2n(nÔłĺ1))┬Ěq + (Ôłĺ(2n+1)/(2n))┬Ě(p+2)] where q=(RÔéü+RÔéé)/(RÔéüÔłĺRÔéé) and p=(uÔÇ▓+u)/(uÔÇ▓Ôłĺu); numerically verified vs two-surface paraxial trace across qÔłł{Ôłĺ1,Ôłĺ0.5,0,0.5,1} and pÔłł{Ôłĺ1,0,1} for nÔłł{1.4,1.5,1.5168,1.6,1.7,1.8} (all within 1e-10 relative); aplanatic shape q=(2n+1)(nÔłĺ1)(p+2)/(n+1) gives S_II=0 exactly; BK7 (n=1.5168, p=Ôłĺ1): q_aplanaticÔëł0.8283; angular coma = S_II/(8┬ĚF#┬Ěv)├Ś206265 arcsec; W_131=ÔłĺS_II (Hopkins sign convention, Born & Wolf ┬ž5.5.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_coma_coefficient`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: third-order Seidel only ÔÇö fifth-order Schwarzschild coma and higher-order Hopkins terms NOT included; single thin lens in air; stop coincident with lens; monochromatic only. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž7.4; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬ž5.3 eq. 5.3.29 + ┬ž5.5.3; Smith MOE (2008) ┬ž4.3.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected. **Longitudinal chromatic aberration** (OPTICS-CHROMATIC-FOCUS): Sellmeier dispersion n(╬╗) = sqrt(1 + ╬ú B_i ╬╗┬▓/(╬╗┬▓ÔłĺC_i)) for BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10 (Schott catalog 2023); per-wavelength BFL via ABCD thin-lens stack; LCA_FC = BFL(486nm)ÔłĺBFL(656nm); Abbe V-number (singlet); BK7 VÔëł64.2 verified; achromat LCA < 0.1 mm verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_chromatic_focus`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial thin-lens LCA only; chromatic lateral aberration not computed.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Abbe number + partial dispersion** (OPTICS-ABBE-NUMBER-COMPUTE): V_d = (n_d Ôłĺ 1) / (n_F Ôłĺ n_C) from Sellmeier Fraunhofer lines d/F/C (Hecht ┬ž6.3 / ISO 10110); secondary spectrum partial dispersion P_{F,g} = (n_g Ôłĺ n_F) / (n_F Ôłĺ n_C) for g-line (435.84 nm); six glasses BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10 (Schott 2023); BK7 V_d = 64.17, F2 = 36.37, SF6 = 25.43, K5 = 59.45, BK10 = 66.95 ÔÇö all within 0.1% of catalog; SF11 = 25.37 (catalog 25.76, 1.5% gap documented ÔÇö Sellmeier fit vs direct spectrophotometric measurement, Schott TIE-29 ┬ž3.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_abbe_number`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: catalog nominal/melt-mean coefficients; melt-to-melt V_d variation ┬▒0.3ÔÇô0.5% (Schott TIE-31).
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid ├Ś grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes ╬Ş = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(╬Ş) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model: all 1.0 with no CA, drops with finite CAs) + cos4_map (natural cosÔü┤(╬Ş) photometric baseline, Hecht ┬ž6.6 / Slyusarev ┬ž3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm Ôćĺ ╬Ş_corner Ôëł 60┬░, cos4_corner Ôëł 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; rotationally-symmetric stack assumed; sensor tilt / telecentricity not modelled. Ref: Welford 1986 ┬ž4.5; Hecht ┬ž6.6; Slyusarev ┬ž3.4.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Entrance pupil position + size** (OPTICS-ENTRANCE-PUPIL-POS): paraxial reverse-trace of a marginal ray from the aperture stop through the front sub-stack (Welford 1986 ┬ž4.4 / Hecht ┬ž6.6); position_z_mm from first surface vertex; D-element transverse magnification; converging front Ôćĺ real pupil (positive z); diverging front Ôćĺ virtual pupil (negative z); LLM tool `optics_compute_entrance_pupil`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; exit pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Exit pupil position + size** (OPTICS-EXIT-PUPIL-POS): paraxial two-ray forward trace from the aperture stop through the rear sub-stack (Welford 1986 ┬ž4.4 / Hecht ┬ž6.6); position_z_mm from last surface vertex; radius from stop-edge ray height at exit pupil plane; thin-lens identity (stop at last surface Ôćĺ EP at z=0, m=1); BK7 biconvex Ôćĺ virtual exit pupil (zÔëłÔłĺ3.41 mm, Welford ┬ž4.4 oracle); afocal telescope (f_obj=100 mm, f_eye=25 mm) Ôćĺ Ramsden disk at z=31.25 mm, radius=1.25 mm, m=0.25=1/M_telescope (Hecht ┬ž6.6 oracle); LLM tool `optics_compute_exit_pupil`; 43 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; entrance pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Diffraction-limited MTF for circular aperture** (OPTICS-MTF-DIFFRACTION-LIMITED): closed-form on-axis MTF(╬Ż) = (2/¤Ç)[arccos(╬Ż/╬ŻÔéÇ) Ôłĺ (╬Ż/╬ŻÔéÇ)┬ĚÔłÜ(1Ôłĺ(╬Ż/╬ŻÔéÇ)┬▓)] for ╬Ż ÔëĄ ╬ŻÔéÇ, 0 otherwise; cutoff ╬ŻÔéÇ = 1/(╬╗┬ĚF#) (Goodman "Introduction to Fourier Optics" ┬ž6.4 eq. 6-49; Hecht "Optics" 5e ┬ž11.3.3); oracle: ╬╗=550nm, F/4 Ôćĺ ╬ŻÔéÇ=454.5 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0, MTF(╬ŻÔéÇ/2)Ôëł0.391 ÔÇö all validated to < 0.1%; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: diffraction-limited theoretical upper bound only ÔÇö no aberrations (Seidel S_IÔÇôS_V), no defocus, no wavefront error, no sensor MTF; monochromatic only (polychromatic = ÔłźW(╬╗)┬ĚMTF(╬╗)d╬╗, not implemented); on-axis only; circular aperture only.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Pixel aperture MTF + Nyquist limit** (OPTICS-PIXEL-MTF): `PixelSensorSpec(pixel_pitch_um, fill_factor=1.0)` Ôćĺ `PixelMtfReport(nyquist_freq_cyc_per_mm, mtf_curve, mtf_at_nyquist, mtf_at_50_percent_nyquist, honest_caveat)`; pixel aperture MTF = |sinc(¤Ç┬Ěa┬Ě╬Ż)| where a = pitch┬Ěfill_factor (Boreman "MTF in Optical and Electro-Optical Systems" ┬ž3.4; Hecht ┬ž11.3); Nyquist limit ╬Ż_N = 1/(2┬Ěp) caps detectable spatial frequency; oracle (p=1.5╬╝m, ff=1.0): ╬Ż_N=333.33 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0 exactly, MTF(╬Ż_N)=2/¤ÇÔëł0.6366 ÔÇö all validated to < 1e-6; fill_factor < 1 Ôćĺ narrower aperture Ôćĺ slower sinc roll-off Ôćĺ MTF at Nyquist > 2/¤Ç (verified: ff=0.5 Ôćĺ MTF(╬Ż_N)Ôëł0.900); `combine_mtf_curves(optical, pixel)` for incoherent cascade MTF_system = MTF_optical ├Ś MTF_pixel (Boreman ┬ž2.1); LLM tool `optics_compute_pixel_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: PIXEL APERTURE SINC ONLY ÔÇö NOT modelled: silicon carrier-diffusion MTF (lateral minority-carrier spread vs. depth, Boreman ┬ž3.4); inter-pixel electrical/optical crosstalk; anti-aliasing filter MTF; Bayer CFA demosaicing resolution loss; charge-transfer inefficiency (CCD); non-square pixels; 2-D MTF = product of independent 1-D sincs for square pixel. Ref: Boreman (2001) ┬ž3.4, ┬ž2.1; Hecht (2017) ┬ž11.3; Holst & Lomheim (2007) ┬ž5.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/pixel_mtf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Petzval field curvature** (OPTICS-PETZVAL-CURVATURE-COMPUTE): Petzval sum P = ╬ú (n_after Ôłĺ n_before) / (n_before ┬Ě n_after ┬Ě R_i) (Hecht ┬ž6.3.2 / Born & Wolf ┬ž4.5); Petzval radius R_P = 1/P; flat-field score 1/(1+|P|┬Ě100); BK7 biconvex oracle (R1=+50, R2=Ôłĺ50, n=1.5168): P Ôëł 0.01363 mmÔü╗┬╣, R_P Ôëł 73.4 mm (within 1%); flat-field condition ╬ú¤ć/n = 0 Ôćĺ P = 0 verified; plano surfaces (|R|=1e18) contribute 0; stop-shift invariance; per-surface breakdown with is_plano flag; LLM tool `optics_compute_petzval_curvature`; 26 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial (third-order) only; does NOT include astigmatism (S_III term); P=0 guarantees flat Petzval sphere but not zero field curvature in the presence of astigmatism (Hecht ┬ž6.3.2); thick-lens pupil-shift corrections not modelled.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Spot diagram + encircled energy** (OPTICS-SPOT-DIAGRAM): fan-of-rays trace through sequential lens system; ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) ├Ś ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) Cartesian pupil grid over unit disk (Welford 1986 ┬ž8.2); exact meridional y-intercept via Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect (Welford ┬ž5.2-5.3); first-order sagittal x estimate (Hecht ┬ž5.7); `SpotDiagramResult` dataclass: image_points_xy (list[(float,float)], mm), rms_radius_mm (Welford ┬ž8.2 RMS), encircled_80pct_radius_mm (geometric EE80 radius, Hecht ┬ž6.3), centroid_xy, svg_diagram (SVG with RMS/EE80/Airy-disk rings + centroid marker + scale bar), honest_caveat; weak-lens paraxial singlet on-axis Ôćĺ near-zero y-spread; BK7 biconvex singlet at 10┬░ Ôćĺ rms > on-axis (coma verified; Hecht ┬ž6.3 / Welford ┬ž6); EE80 Ôëą RMS monotonically; LLM tool `optics_compute_spot_diagram` (monochromatic only; sagittal x = first-order estimate; no chromatic dispersion; single wavelength; stop at first surface; 24 hermetic tests). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬ž6.3, ┬ž10.2; Welford (1986) ┬ž5.2-5.3, ┬ž6, ┬ž8.2.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Piston/tip/tilt/defocus wavefront alignment analysis** (OPTICS-WAVEFRONT-PISTON-TIP-TILT): extracts ZÔéü (piston), ZÔéé (tip), ZÔéâ (tilt), ZÔéä (defocus) Noll-ordered Zernike alignment components from a sampled wavefront W(¤ü,╬Ş); reports each in waves at a given wavelength via W_nm / wavelength_nm conversion; reuses fit_zernike_wavefront (4-term least-squares, numpy.linalg.lstsq, Noll 1976 orthonormal basis); `PistonTipTiltReport` dataclass (piston_waves, tip_waves, tilt_waves, defocus_waves, residual_rms_waves, dominant_misalignment, honest_caveat); dominant = argmax(|c_j|) for j=1..4 with "none" below 0.001 wave threshold; LLM tool `optics_analyze_wavefront_alignment`; 45 hermetic tests (pure piston 10nm @ ╬╗=632.8nm Ôćĺ 0.01580 waves verified; pure tip/tilt/defocus; combined misalignment; higher-order residual; error-path). Honest: circular unit-disk pupil only (¤ü Ôłł [0,1]; no obscuration or elliptical aperture); alignment analysis only ÔÇö corrects rigid-body misalignment (piston = axial OPD offset, tip/tilt = wavefront tilt, defocus = longitudinal focus); does NOT correct higher-order aberrations (coma, astigmatism, spherical, etc.); use optics_fit_zernike_wavefront for full 15-term decomposition. Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬ž11.3; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬ž9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992) Applied Optics and Optical Engineering XI ch.1; Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207.

**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Sagitta arrow chart** (OPTICS-SAGITTA-ARROW-CHART): conic + even-power aspheric surface sagitta z(r) sampled across the clear aperture; standard ISO 10110-12 ┬ž6.2 / Welford ┬ž3.3 formula z = c┬Ěr┬▓/(1+ÔłÜ(1Ôłĺ(1+k)c┬▓r┬▓)) + ╬úaßÁó┬Ěr^(2i+4); SVG chart with horizontal axis = radius (mm), vertical = sagitta (mm), arrow markers at every 5th sample showing local slope dz/dr; `AsphericSurfaceSpec` dataclass (radius_mm, conic_k, aspheric_coeffs, clear_aperture_radius_mm); `SagittaArrowChartResult` (sagitta_samples, max_sagitta_mm, conic_only_sagitta_mm, aspheric_contribution_mm, svg_chart, honest_caveat); sphere R=50 r=10 oracle zÔëł1.0102 verified < 1e-6; paraboloid k=Ôłĺ1 z=r┬▓/(2R) exact; hemisphere z=R at edge; domain-violation guard (radicand Ôëą 0 + fp-epsilon clamp); LLM tool `optics_compute_sagitta_arrow_chart`; 28 hermetic tests. Honest: standard conic + even-power polynomial asphere ONLY; no Zernike / freeform / XY-polynomial / Q-polynomial / off-axis / tilted surface support; arrow markers show dz/dr (slope), not surface normal; ISO 10110-12:2019. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž3.3; ISO 10110-12:2019.

**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Vignetting fraction check** (OPTICS-VIGNETTING-CHECK): computes the fraction of entrance-pupil area occluded by clear-aperture limits at a given field angle; `LensClearApertureSpec` dataclass (surfaces: list of {clear_aperture_radius_mm, axial_position_mm}); `VignettingReport` dataclass (field_angle_deg, vignetting_pct, limiting_surface_idx, effective_pupil_area_pct, honest_caveat); `compute_vignetting(spec, field_angle_deg, marginal_ray_at_stop_mm=10.0)` ÔÇö paraxial chief-ray displacement ╬ö_j = z_j┬Ětan(╬Ş); effective pupil area = exact two-circle intersection area (Weisstein formula) of entrance-pupil disk (radius R) with per-surface CA disk (radius r_j, centred at ╬ö_j); vignetting_pct = (1 Ôłĺ A_eff/A_full)├Ś100; limiting_surface_idx = argmin of per-surface intersection areas; on-axis (field=0┬░) Ôćĺ vignetting=0 verified; wide-angle (30┬░) with tight CA Ôćĺ significant clipping verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting_check`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial chief-ray displacement only (no exact ray trace through glass); circular, rotationally-symmetric CAs only; diffraction-induced vignetting NOT modelled; chromatic pupil walk NOT modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž3.7; Hecht (2017) ┬ž5.7.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Telecentricity check** (OPTICS-TELECENTRICITY): `compute_telecentricity(lens_system_dict, field_height_mm=10.0, focus_shift_mm=0.5)` Ôćĺ `TelecentricityReport(chief_ray_angle_object_deg, chief_ray_angle_image_deg, object_telecentric, image_telecentric, both_telecentric, max_magnification_variation_pct, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray trace via Welford nu-form (`nÔÇ▓uÔÇ▓ = nu Ôłĺ hc(nÔÇ▓Ôłĺn)`); chief-ray solved by superposition: Ray A (H, 0) + ╬▒┬ĚRay B (object-dist, 1) at first surface, ╬▒ = Ôłĺh_A_stop/h_B_stop forces h=0 at aperture stop; object-space telecentric Ôćö |angle_obj| < 0.5┬░; image-space telecentric Ôćö |angle_img| < 0.5┬░; magnification variation across ┬▒focus_shift_mm computed from u_last of marginal field ray relative to Lagrange-invariant reference magnification; oracle: single-lens (f=100 mm, stop at front focal plane from 5 m object) Ôćĺ object_telecentric=True, image_telecentric=False; doubly-telecentric relay (two equal lenses, stop at shared focal plane) Ôćĺ both_telecentric=True; LLM tool `optics_compute_telecentricity`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: PARAXIAL (first-order) ONLY ÔÇö chief ray forced through h=0 at stop surface; aspheric surface terms do not affect first-order angle; stop modelled as thin plane; infinite-conjugate objects approximated by large finite distance; magnification variation uses thin-lens paraxial formula (nu-form). Telecentric threshold: |angle| < 0.5┬░ (conventional machine-vision). Ref: Welford "Aberrations of Optical Systems" (1986) ┬ž3, ┬ž4.4; Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬ž5.4; Hecht "Optics" ┬ž6.6. `kerf-cad-core/optics/telecentricity_check.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Depth-of-field + hyperfocal distance** (OPTICS-FOCAL-DISTANCE-DEPTH): `LensFocusSpec(focal_length_mm, f_number, focus_distance_mm, circle_of_confusion_mm=0.03)` Ôćĺ `DepthOfFieldReport(hyperfocal_distance_mm, near_limit_mm, far_limit_mm, depth_of_field_mm, behind_focus_fraction, infinity_focus_at_hyperfocal, honest_caveat)`; standard photographic thin-lens DoF formulae (Greenleaf "Photographic Optics" ┬ž3 / Hecht "Optics" ┬ž6.4): H = f┬▓/(N┬Ěc) + f; D_near = D┬Ě(HÔłĺf)/(H+DÔłĺ2f); D_far = D┬Ě(HÔłĺf)/(HÔłĺD) [Ôł× when D Ôëą H]; oracle 50mm f/2.8 @ 5 m c=0.03 mm Ôćĺ H Ôëł 29811.9 mm (Ôëł29.81 m); near Ôëł 4286 mm; far Ôëł 5993 mm; DoF Ôëł 1707 mm ÔÇö all verified to < 0.01%; at focus=H: D_near = H/2 exactly, D_far = Ôł× verified; D Ôëą H Ôćĺ DoF infinite; larger f/# Ôćĺ wider DoF; LLM tool `optics_compute_depth_of_field`; 25 hermetic tests. Default CoC 0.03 mm = 35mm full-frame standard (Greenleaf ┬ž3 / 1/1400 diagonal). HONEST: geometric thin-lens model only ÔÇö does NOT add diffraction-limited Airy-disk blur to geometric CoC; at small apertures (f/# Ôë│ f/16 for visible light) Airy disk 1.22┬Ě╬╗┬ĚN approaches 0.03 mm CoC, so geometric DoF is slightly optimistic; for combined blur circle use c_eff = sqrt(c_geom┬▓ + c_airy┬▓). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬ž6.4; Greenleaf (1950) ┬ž3; Kingslake (1978) ┬ž4.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Working f-number (finite-conjugate)** (OPTICS-FNO-WORKING): `FnoWorkingSpec(nominal_f_number, magnification)` Ôćĺ `FnoWorkingReport(nominal_f_number, working_f_number, exposure_loss_stops, image_irradiance_factor, honest_caveat)`; thin-lens working f-number formula N_w = N┬Ě(1+|m|) (Hecht "Optics" ┬ž6.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬ž4.5); magnification convention m = Ôłĺs_i/s_o (negative for real inverted images); oracle f/4 at 1:1 macro (m=Ôłĺ1) Ôćĺ N_w=8.0, loss=2.0 stops exactly; f/2.8 at 1:2 (m=Ôłĺ0.5) Ôćĺ N_w=4.2, lossÔëł1.17 stops; image irradiance factor = (N/N_w)┬▓ = 1/(1+|m|)┬▓; exposure_loss_stops = 2┬ĚlogÔéé(1+|m|); m=0 (infinity focus) Ôćĺ N_w=N, loss=0, factor=1.0 (no penalty); absolute value of m used so positive (virtual-image) magnifications are handled; LLM tool `optics_compute_working_fno`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: thin-lens (symmetric-pupil) approximation ONLY ÔÇö real asymmetric lenses (retrofocus, telephoto, macro with floating elements) have pupil magnification p = D_exit/D_entrance Ôëá 1; exact formula N_w = (1/p)┬ĚN┬Ě(1+|m|/p) (Smith MOE ┬ž4.5) can differ by 0.5ÔÇô1 stop for extreme retrofocus designs; pupil-position measurement requires an aperture-stop trace not in scope here. Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬ž6.4; Smith (2008) ┬ž4.5; Ray (2002) ┬ž2. `kerf-cad-core/optics/fno_working.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Iris (aperture stop) diameter map** (OPTICS-IRIS-DIAMETER-MAP): `IrisMapSpec(lens_system_dict, target_f_number, target_efl_mm=None)` Ôćĺ `IrisDiameterReport(iris_diameter_mm, effective_f_number, efl_mm, surface_clearance_check, clipped, honest_caveat)`; paraxial formula D = EFL/f# (Welford "Aberrations" ┬ž3.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬ž6); EFL computed via canonical marginal-ray trace (h=1, u=0) or supplied via `target_efl_mm`; marginal ray h=D/2 at stop (u=0) traced forward through surfaces after the stop and backward through a reversed sub-system for surfaces before the stop; per-surface clearance_ratio = CA_radius / |h| (>1 = clears; <1 = clips); clipping flag when h > 0.95 ├Ś CA_radius; oracle: EFL=50 mm, f/4 Ôćĺ D=12.5 mm exactly; f/1.4 fast lens Ôćĺ DÔëł35.7 mm; stop_surface_index configurable; LLM tool `optics_compute_iris_diameter_map`; 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: paraxial (first-order) marginal-ray trace only ÔÇö aspheric higher-order sag terms ignored; D=EFL/f# is infinity-conjugate formula only (finite-conjugate requires working f-number N_w=N┬Ě(1+|m|), Smith MOE ┬ž4.5); clear apertures are caller-supplied; production design requires exact skew-ray analysis (Zemax OpticStudio / CODE V / Welford ┬ž5). Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž3.4; Smith (2008) ┬ž6; Hecht (2017) ┬ž6.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/iris_diameter_map.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Airy-disk diffraction-limited PSF** (OPTICS-DIFFRACTION-PSF): `DiffractionPSFSpec(wavelength_nm, aperture_diameter_mm, focal_length_mm)` Ôćĺ `DiffractionPSFReport(airy_disk_radius_um, rayleigh_resolution_um, fwhm_um, psf_profile, honest_caveat)`; radial intensity I(r) = [2┬ĚJÔéü(x)/x]┬▓ where x = ¤Ç┬ĚD┬Ěr/(╬╗┬Ěf) (Hecht "Optics" 5e ┬ž10.2, eq. 10.22; Born & Wolf "Principles of Optics" 7e ┬ž8.5.2, eq. 8.41); Airy disk radius r_Airy = 1.22┬Ě╬╗┬ĚF# (first zero of JÔéü, Born & Wolf ┬ž8.5.2); Rayleigh resolution criterion ╬ör = r_Airy (Hecht ┬ž10.2.7, eq. 10.28); FWHM Ôëł 1.03┬Ě╬╗┬ĚF# (Hecht eq. 10.59); uses scipy.special.j1 when available with pure-Python ascending-series fallback (Abramowitz & Stegun ┬ž9.1.10); oracle ╬╗=550nm, D=10mm, f=50mm (F#=5): r_Airy=3.355 ╬╝m, FWHM=2.833 ╬╝m, I(0)=1.0, I(r_Airy)Ôëł0 ÔÇö all validated to <1e-6; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_psf`; 32 hermetic tests. HONEST: SCALAR DIFFRACTION ONLY ÔÇö no vector/polarisation effects (Richards-Wolf high-NA integral, Born & Wolf ┬ž8.7); circular aperture only (non-circular/annular not modelled); aberration-free (Airy pattern = diffraction-limited ideal; Seidel/Zernike wavefront error Ôćĺ Strehl < 1 not modelled); monochromatic (polychromatic PSF = ÔłźW(╬╗)┬ĚI(r,╬╗)d╬╗ not implemented); on-axis and paraxial (NA = D/(2f) Ôë¬ 1 assumed). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬ž10.2; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬ž8.5; Goodman (2005) ┬ž4.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/diffraction_psf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Singlet lens glass volume and weight** (OPTICS-LENS-VOLUME): `SingletLensSpec(radius_R1_mm, radius_R2_mm, center_thickness_mm, clear_aperture_radius_mm, glass_density_g_cm3=2.51)` Ôćĺ `LensVolumeReport(volume_mm3, weight_g, edge_thickness_mm, sag1_mm, sag2_mm, lens_form, honest_caveat)`; sag h = |R| Ôłĺ ÔłÜ(|R|┬▓ Ôłĺ r┬▓) (Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬ž13.3 eq. 13.6 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging and Aberrations" ┬ž1.2); cap volume V_cap = ¤Ç┬Ěh┬▓┬Ě(3|R|Ôłĺh)/3 (Smith ┬ž13.3 eq. 13.7); lens volume V = ¤Ç┬Ěr┬▓┬Ět_c ┬▒ V_cap1 ┬▒ V_cap2 with sign from Cartesian-sign surface convention (convex Ôćĺ subtract, concave Ôćĺ add); oracle: BK7 plano-convex R1=+100 mm, R2=Ôł×, ct=5 mm, CA_r=12.5 mm, ¤ü=2.51 g/cm┬│ Ôćĺ sag1=0.7843 mm, V=2261.6 mm┬│, weight=5.677 g (analytically verified); biconvex symmetric V = cylinder Ôłĺ 2┬Ěcap (both surfaces subtract); biconcave V = cylinder + 2┬Ěcap (both surfaces add; edge > center thickness); meniscus R1=+100/R2=+200 classified correctly; lens_form Ôłł {biconvex, biconcave, plano_convex, plano_concave, meniscus, plano_plano}; LLM tool `optics_compute_lens_volume`; 35 hermetic tests. HONEST: SPHERICAL SURFACES ONLY ÔÇö aspheric sag h=Rc┬Ěr┬▓/(1+ÔłÜ(1Ôłĺ(1+k)c┬▓r┬▓))+╬ú A_i┬Ěr^(2i) requires numerical integration (out of scope); no anti-reflection coating thickness (AR layers 100ÔÇô500 nm, negligible mass); homogeneous density assumed (GRIN / melt-gradient glass differs ÔëĄ0.3%, Schott TIE-31 ┬ž3); clear_aperture_radius Ôëá physical blank radius ÔÇö blank is always larger, giving higher actual weight. Ref: Smith (2008) ┬ž13.3; Mahajan (2011) ┬ž1.2; Schott TIE-31 (2023). `kerf-cad-core/optics/lens_volume.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Paraxial chief-ray height trace** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-HEIGHT): `trace_chief_ray(lens_system_dict, field_angle_deg, stop_surface_idx)` Ôćĺ `ChiefRayHeightReport(per_surface_heights, image_height_mm, magnification, stop_surface_idx, chief_ray_at_stop_mm, object_angle_deg, image_angle_deg, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray (principal ray from off-axis object through stop centre) traced via nu-form superposition (Welford "Aberrations" ┬ž3 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging" ┬ž2): two auxiliary rays (Ray A: object height H, slope 0; Ray B: height obj_dist, slope 1) solve h_stop=0 Ôćĺ u_obj=Ôłĺh_A_stop/h_B_stop; oracle: f=50mm plano-convex thin lens, ╬Ş=5┬░ Ôćĺ image_height=f┬Ětan(5┬░)=4.374mm (verified to <1e-3mm); chief-ray height at stop = 0 exactly; image-space telecentric condition (stop at front focal plane Ôćĺ u_img=0) verified; per-surface {surface_idx, ray_height_mm, ray_angle_deg}; LLM tool `optics_trace_chief_ray`; 30 hermetic tests. HONEST: PARAXIAL ONLY ÔÇö first-order heights differ from exact at large field/fast optics; APERTURE STOP POSITION MUST BE SUPPLIED (no auto-detect); rotationally symmetric systems only; image height = f┬Ětan(╬Ş) (no distortion correction). Ref: Welford (1986) ┬ž3, ┬ž3.7; Mahajan (2011) ┬ž2; Smith (2008) ┬ž5. `kerf-cad-core/optics/chief_ray_height.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** Ôťů ÔÇö **Schmidt corrector plate aspheric profile** (OPTICS-SCHMIDT-CORRECTOR-PLATE): `SchmidtSpec(primary_radius_R_mm, aperture_diameter_D_mm, glass_index_n=1.5168, neutral_zone_factor_kappa=1.5)` Ôćĺ `SchmidtReport(aspheric_profile, max_sag_mm, neutral_zone_radius_mm, schwarzschild_constant_k, honest_caveat)`; classical Schmidt (1932) corrector sag z(r) = r┬▓┬Ě(r┬▓Ôłĺ2┬Ě¤ü_n┬▓)/[8┬Ě(nÔłĺ1)┬ĚR┬│] where ¤ü_n = (D/2)/ÔłÜ╬║ is the neutral zone radius (Born & Wolf ┬ž6.3); kappa=1.5 places neutral zone at rÔëł0.8165┬ĚD/2 (classic Schmidt optimum that minimises peak-to-valley sag); max_sag = |z(¤ü_n)| = ¤ü_nÔü┤/[8┬Ě(nÔłĺ1)┬ĚR┬│]; neutral-zone slope check (dz/dr=0 at r=¤ü_n); Schwarzschild constant k=Ôłĺ1 (paraboloid equivalent); oracle: 200mm f/2 BK7 corrector Ôćĺ neutral zone 81.65mm, max_sagÔëł0.168mm; sag scales as (nÔłĺ1)Ôü╗┬╣ verified; LLM tool `optics_design_schmidt_corrector`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: classical Schmidt (1932) ONLY ÔÇö modern SchmidtÔÇôCassegrain and SchmidtÔÇôNewtonian designs add a secondary mirror, field-flattener, and refined aspherics for a flat corrected field; these are NOT modelled; monochromatic (chromatic residual is second-order, Wilkins 1950, not computed); on-axis only (off-axis coma requires corrector at exact centre-of-curvature position); field curvature R_PetzvalÔëłÔłĺR/2 not corrected; thin-plate approximation. Ref: Schmidt (1932) Zentralzeitung f├╝r Optik und Mechanik 52, 25-26; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬ž6.3; Rutten & van Venrooij "Telescope Optics" (1988) ┬ž6.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/schmidt_corrector.py`.

**Implicit geometry** Ôťů ÔÇö F-rep CSG (union/intersect/subtract/blend/shell) + domain warps (twist/taper/wave) in `kerf_cad_core.frep.csg`.

**Materials + LCA** Ôťů ÔÇö Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty). **Embodied-carbon DB (ICE v3 lookups)** Ôťů ÔÇö `kerf_lca.database` module with 30-material `MATERIAL_DATABASE` (steel, aluminium, copper, composites, concrete, timber, plastics, elastomers, glass, ceramics); `lca_lookup_material` + `lca_compute_embodied_carbon` LLM tools; EN 15978 Module D EoL credits. Data: ICE v3.0, Hammond & Jones, University of Bath, 2019 ÔÇö NOT Ecoinvent (license-restricted).
**Materials + LCA** Ôťů ÔÇö Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty); EoL circularity (EN 15978 Module D + Ellen MacArthur MCI) Ôťů.

**Compare matrices** Ôťů ÔÇö feature-matrix YAML for 14 reference CADs: Fusion 360, SolidWorks, Onshape, FreeCAD, Rhino, KiCad, CATIA, Creo, NX, Inventor, AutoCAD, Altium, Revit, Blender ÔÇö 741 grounded rows total.

**Security hardening** Ôťů ÔÇö `/run-topo` auth gate; NFP `grid_step` clamped; PVT `n_mc` clamped; Yosys module-name injection blocked; shared `_guard_*` helpers extracted across 68 files (Ôłĺ2009/+129 lines net).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-CROSS-CURVE** Ôťů ÔÇö walk a parametric path on the Catmull-Clark subdivision-surface limit and intersect with a planar cut to produce a cross-section curve: `walk_subd_limit_cross_plane(cage_mesh, plane_point, plane_normal, num_walk_samples=400)` returns `CrossCurveResult(points, face_indices_crossed, num_intersections, honest_caveat)`; samples a uniform (u,v) grid on each cage face using the Stam (1998) closed-form limit-position evaluator (`stam_limit_position` ÔÇö bi-cubic B-spline for regular valence-4 patches, eigenstructure for extraordinary vertices); sign changes in signed plane distance are detected between adjacent grid samples (u-adjacent + v-adjacent separately); each crossing refined by 5 bisection iterations (positional error Ôëł cell_size/32 Ôëł face_size/32); honest caveats: discrete sample walk (coarse grid can miss sub-cell features), 5-iter bisection (not sub-pixel), boundary edge duplicates possible, extraordinary vertices use Stam eigenstructure approximation; LLM tool `subd_walk_limit_cross_plane`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (cube XY/XZ/diagonal cuts, parallel planes Ôćĺ empty, flat patch, grid cage, extraordinary vertex cage, degenerate cage, non-unit normal, sample-count monotonicity) ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_walk_cross_curve.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH ┬ž3ÔÇô4; Schaefer-Warren (2004).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-ALONG-EDGES** Ôťů ÔÇö sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface curve corresponding to a chain of cage edges: `walk_along_cage_edges(cage, vertex_sequence, samples_per_edge=8)` returns `SubDEdgeWalk(points, arc_length)`; boundary edges Ôćĺ limit = cage (crease rule); creased interior edges Ôćĺ limit on sharp crease curve; smooth interior edges Ôćĺ smooth arc through CC limit positions; intermediate points via index-tracked CC subdivision (k = ceil(log2(spe)) levels, max 6) + per-vertex limit stencil; honest ValueError for non-adjacent vertices or out-of-range indices; LLM tool `subd_walk_edge_chain`; 14 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_walk.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-RING-FROM-EDGE** Ôťů ÔÇö edge ring traversal on Catmull-Clark quad cages: `compute_edge_ring(cage, start_edge)` returns `EdgeRingResult(edge_indices, is_closed, is_degenerate, transition_face_indices)`; follows opposite edges across each quad face (Maya/Blender Bridge pattern); closed on cube (4-ring) and torus (ring length = opposite-axis count); open at mesh boundary; honest degenerate flag at non-quad faces; start_edge accepts `(v0, v1)` pair or integer edge index; LLM tool `subd_compute_edge_ring`; 25 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_ring.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-LOOP-SELECT** Ôťů ÔÇö directional edge-loop walk on a quad cage mesh: `select_edge_loop(cage_mesh, start_edge_idx, max_steps=1000)` returns `EdgeLoopResult(edge_indices, vertex_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_vertex_valences, honest_caveat)`; walks the opposite-edge chain (Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni 2013 ┬ž3.2 'skip-2' rule): at each step crosses the current quad face to its opposite edge; terminates at irregular vertex (valenceÔëá4), boundary edge, non-quad face, or loop closure; oracles: 4├Ś4 torus (all valence-4) Ôćĺ closed loops length 4; 6├Ś8 torus Ôćĺ lengths {6, 8}; cube (all valence-3) Ôćĺ terminates at first irregular vertex, valence=3 reported; cylinder axial-interior edge Ôćĺ closed ring length nu; mixed tri/quad Ôćĺ terminates; ValueError on out-of-range start_edge_idx; honest caveats: quads only, no tris; assumes manifold mesh; boundary vertices treated as irregular; traversal direction fixed by first adjacent face winding; LLM tool `subd_select_edge_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 25 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬ž3.2; L├ęvy-Liu (2010) SIGGRAPH ┬ž4.

**SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** Ôťů ÔÇö walk a face loop on a quad cage mesh by hopping through opposite-edge adjacent quads: `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0, max_steps=1000)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; dual of the edge-loop walk ÔÇö tracks faces rather than edges, useful for ring-cut planning and subdivision sweep selection; `walk_direction` 0/1 selects which opposite-edge pair to traverse: dir=0 crosses (v0,v1)Ôćö(v2,v3) edges, dir=1 crosses (v1,v2)Ôćö(v3,v0) edges; on a regular torus the two directions produce orthogonal face rings; terminates at non-quad face, boundary edge, or loop closure; oracles: 4├Ś4 torus dir=0 Ôćĺ closed ring length 4; 4├Ś6 torus dir=0Ôćĺlength 4, dir=1Ôćĺlength 6; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 Ôćĺ circumferential closed ring length 12; cube Ôćĺ closed 4-ring; mixed tri/quad Ôćĺ terminated; single-quad cage Ôćĺ terminated; non-quad start face Ôćĺ immediate termination; ValueError on out-of-range start_face_idx or walk_direction not in {0,1}; honest caveats: quads only ÔÇö non-quad face terminates immediately; boundary edges terminate walk; walk_direction relative to start face winding; one-directional (no back-propagation); manifold mesh assumed; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬ž3.2; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬ž3.2.

**SUBD-CAGE-SUBDIVIDE-EDGE** Ôťů ÔÇö localized single-edge refinement on a SubD control cage (not a full Catmull-Clark pass): `subdivide_edge(cage, edge_index, position_t=0.5, split_strategy='quad') -> SubdivideEdgeResult`; inserts midpoint vertex v_m = lerp(v_a, v_b, t) on the target edge; each of the 1ÔÇô2 adjacent faces split into face_a [p0, v_m, p_{n-1}] (triangle) + face_b [v_m, p1, ..., p_{n-1}] (quad for n=4); cube oracle: V=8Ôćĺ9, F=6Ôćĺ8, E=12Ôćĺ15, Euler 9Ôłĺ15+8=2 Ôťô; boundary-edge split: 1 adjacent face only; invalid edge_index Ôćĺ ValueError; position_t clamp [1e-9, 1Ôłĺ1e-9]; honest flag `has_non_quad_input` for non-quad input faces; sharpness/bevel-weight not preserved across edge-index remapping; LLM tool `subd_subdivide_edge`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 24 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_subdivide_edge.py`. Ref: Catmull & Clark 1978; Stam 1998 ┬ž4 local refinement; Maya polySplit API.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** Ôťů ÔÇö collapse a SubD cage edge (merge two endpoints into one vertex) while maintaining mesh validity; used for mesh decimation and cage simplification: `collapse_edge(cage: SubdCage, v_keep, v_remove, midpoint=True) -> EdgeCollapseResult`; `EdgeCollapseResult(new_cage: SubdCage, num_vertices_removed, num_faces_removed, collapsed_position_xyz_mm, degenerate_faces_removed, became_invalid, honest_caveat)`; midpoint=True (default): v_new = (V[v_keep] + V[v_remove]) / 2; midpoint=False: v_new = V[v_keep]; all face refs to v_remove rewritten to v_keep; degenerate faces (containing both endpoints Ôćĺ repeated vertex) removed; vertex list compacted; adjacency check ÔÇö if v_keep and v_remove do not share a face (not a valid edge), became_invalid=True and input cage returned unchanged; cube oracle: collapse top-front edge (v_keep=4, v_remove=5) Ôćĺ 7 verts, 2 degenerate faces removed Ôťô; pyramid base edge: 5Ôćĺ4 verts, Ôëą1 degenerate face Ôťô; non-adjacent pair Ôćĺ became_invalid=True, cage unchanged Ôťô; midpoint position oracle Ôťô; endpoint position (midpoint=False) oracle Ôťô; all face indices valid post-collapse Ôťô; v_keep/v_remove out-of-range Ôćĺ ValueError Ôťô; honest caveats: TOPOLOGY ONLY ÔÇö no QEM cost function (Garland-Heckbert 1997); caller chooses which edge to collapse; midpoint placement can deviate from CC limit surface; crease annotations not preserved; all indices invalidated; non-manifold edges handled conservatively; LLM tool `subd_collapse_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in `plugin.py _TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1993) Mesh Optimization; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬ž3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM ┬ž3; Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬ž4.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-FLIP** Ôťů ÔÇö topological edge flip for two adjacent triangles sharing an edge: `flip_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx) -> EdgeFlipResult`; finds the two triangles T1=(v_a, v_b, v_c) and T2=(v_a, v_b, v_d) sharing edge (v_a, v_b); replaces them with T1'=(v_a, v_c, v_d) and T2'=(v_b, v_d, v_c) connecting the opposite vertices; winding order of T1 is preserved in both output triangles; vertex list unchanged (no vertices added or removed); face count unchanged (2 in Ôćĺ 2 out); canonical oracle: triangles ABC+BCD (share BC) Ôćĺ flip gives {A,B,D}+{A,C,D} (share AD); new shared edge is AD, old shared edge BC no longer present Ôťô; double flip restores original topology (flip is its own inverse) Ôťô; only non-incident faces unchanged Ôťô; out-of-range edge_idx Ôćĺ ValueError; boundary edge (1 incident face) Ôćĺ ValueError; non-manifold edge (> 2 incident faces) Ôćĺ ValueError; quad or n-gon face Ôćĺ ValueError; honest caveats: TOPOLOGICAL FLIP ONLY ÔÇö no Delaunay in-circle test; callers must test in-circle criterion themselves if Delaunay quality is required; triangles only (quad faces raise ValueError); no crease/UV/colour attribute preservation on flipped edge; vertex positions unchanged; LLM tool `subd_flip_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_flip.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬ž3; Edelsbrunner (2001) Geometry and Topology for Mesh Generation ┬ž2; de Berg et al. (2008) Computational Geometry ┬ž9.3.

**SUBD-CAGE-AREA** Ôťů ÔÇö compute total surface area of a subdivision control cage (control polygon) and estimate the asymptotic Catmull-Clark limit-surface area: `compute_cage_area(cage) -> CageAreaReport`; `SubdCage(vertices_xyz_mm, faces)` accepts tris, quads, and n-gons; triangle area = 0.5┬Ě|cross(v1-v0, v2-v0)|; quad area = 0.5┬Ě|cross(d1, d2)| (diagonal cross-product, exact for planar quads); n-gon area = centroid fan triangulation (exact for planar n-gons); limit-surface estimate = cage_area ├Ś 0.94 (empirical Catmull-Clark shrinkage ratio); `CageAreaReport` fields: `total_cage_area_mm2`, `estimated_limit_surface_area_mm2`, `per_face_areas`, `min_face_area_mm2`, `max_face_area_mm2`, `degenerate_face_indices`, `num_quads`, `num_tris`, `num_ngons`, `honest_caveat`; unit cube oracle: 6 mm┬▓ cage, 5.64 mm┬▓ estimate Ôťô; degenerate triangle (collinear) flagged Ôťô; pyramid (1 quad + 4 tris) area oracle Ôťô; pentagon n-gon area = exact formula within 1e-9 Ôťô; hexagon n-gon Ôťô; area scales by k┬▓ on vertex rescaling Ôťô; limit estimate = cage ├Ś 0.94 exactly Ôťô; LLM tool `subd_compute_cage_area`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 23 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/cage_area.py`. HONEST: LIMIT-SURFACE AREA IS AN EMPIRICAL ESTIMATE ONLY ÔÇö exact value requires Stam (1998) eigenanalysis at each extraordinary vertex or GL integration over Stam B-spline patches; empirical 0.92ÔÇô0.95 range applies to typical organic closed all-quad cages; error vs exact limit area can exceed 5% for cages with many extraordinary vertices or high non-planarity; non-planar quad/n-gon face areas are first-order approximations only. Refs: Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH ┬ž2; Warren-Weimer (2001) ┬ž5; Zorin-Schr├Âder (2000) SIGGRAPH Course ┬ž3.

**SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** Ôťů ÔÇö merge a list of N cage vertices (by index) into their centroid, updating all adjacent face indices and removing degenerate faces: `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices) -> VertexMergeResult`; computes v_c = mean of all named vertex positions; replaces every face reference to any named vertex with v_c; faces containing Ôëą 2 named vertices become degenerate (repeated vertex) and are removed; vertex list compacted (net -(|S|-1) vertices); special cases: empty or single-vertex list Ôćĺ no-op; duplicate indices Ôćĺ deduplicated; non-adjacent vertices (no shared edge) Ôćĺ no faces removed, vertex count drops by |S|-1; cube oracle: merge all 4 corners of isolated quad Ôćĺ 3 verts removed, 1 face removed, 0 faces survive; 2-vertex merge on plane Ôćĺ equivalent to edge_collapse (same vertex count, same faces removed, centroid=midpoint); 3-vertex centroid oracle Ôťô; all face indices valid post-merge Ôťô; out-of-range index Ôćĺ ValueError; honest caveats: centroid placement only ÔÇö NO quadric error metric (Garland-Heckbert 1997 ┬ž3); CC limit surface shape changes; crease annotations on incident edges not preserved; vertex/face indices invalidated after merge; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬ž3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM ┬ž3.

**SUBD-LIMIT-CRITICAL-POINTS** Ôťů ÔÇö discrete Morse critical points (Ôłçf = 0) on Catmull-Clark SubD limit surfaces: `find_critical_points(cage, scalar_field, sample_density=4) -> CriticalPointsReport`; classifies interior vertices using lower/upper link under Simulation-of-Simplicity total order (Edelsbrunner-M├╝cke 1990) ÔÇö minima (LkÔü╗ empty), maxima (LkÔü║ empty), saddles (#components(LkÔü╗) + #components(LkÔü║) > 2); Morse-Euler verification #max Ôłĺ #sad + #min = ¤ç(VÔłĺE+F); scalar fields: height_z/height_x/height_y/radius; oracle depth bar: sphere from cube cage Ôćĺ 1 max + 1 min + 0 sad (¤ç=2, Euler passes); torus (axis along Y, Morse generic) Ôćĺ 1 max + 1 min + 2 sad (¤ç=0); flat/tilted-plane open mesh Ôćĺ 0 critical points; honest caveat: Bott-Samelson degenerate fields (axis-symmetric height on upright torus) not handled ÔÇö euler_check flags violations; LLM tool `subd_find_critical_points`; 16 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_critical_points.py` (Edelsbrunner-Harer 2010 ┬ž1).

**BREP-SHELL-WALL-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö post-shell wall-thickness verification against manufacturing process requirements: `check_shell_walls(body, process, material) -> ShellWallReport`; injection moulding spec from Menges 2001 ┬ž3.3 Table 3.3 (t_min/t_max per material, flow-length correction +0.5 mm/100 mm); sheet metal from Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž5 (constant-wall + ┬ž5.4 bend-radius multiplier); FDM/SLA/SLS/DLP/MJF nozzle-diameter minimum wall; per-face `FaceWallResult` with violation text; `violations_thin`/`violations_thick` lists; honest caveat: static rule-based only, no CFD or mould-fill simulation; LLM tool `brep_check_shell_walls`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (2mm ABS Ôćĺ pass; 0.5mm ABS Ôćĺ thin; 0.5mm FDM Ôćĺ pass; 0.2mm FDM Ôćĺ thin; 6mm ABS Ôćĺ thick; Menges Table 3.3 oracle for PP/PC/LCP/PVC/POM/PEEK; flow-length correction; sheet-metal Al; SLA; nozzle override) ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/shell_wall_check.py`.

### Core platform

- **Auth + projects + files + chat (CRUD)** Ôťů ÔÇö Postgres, JWT, Google OAuth.
- **Plugin monorepo (`packages/kerf-*`)** Ôťů ÔÇö `kerf-core` app factory + entry-point loader; ~25 plugin packages; 864+ tests.
- **Single-binary build + brew/curl install** Ôťů ÔÇö embedded Vite SPA (~32 MB).
- **Auth-optional local mode** Ôťů ÔÇö `POST /auth/bootstrap-local` singleton user.
- **Cloud: workshop sharing, billing, LLM pricing, free/paid buckets + wallet** Ôťů ÔÇö USD-display, credits at cost, BYO-key plumbing.
- **Cloud: git (commits/branches/merge/GitHub sync) + git Storer** Ôťů.
- **Large-file git handling** Ôťů ÔÇö pointer kind, Phase 1.
- **Diff-based + compressed revisions** Ôťů ÔÇö 82├Ś shrink.
- **Workspaces (orgs), activity timeline, avatars/CDN, collapsible chat** Ôťů.
- **E2E Playwright + per-plugin pytest suites** Ôťů.
- **Billing-ledger schema on fresh databases** Ôťů.

### Scripting / SDK

- **`.script.py` via `kerf-sdk`** Ôťů ÔÇö `/v1/rpc` JSON-RPC over the LLM tool registry; API tokens; PyPI publish.
- **SDKs: Python ┬Ě TypeScript ┬Ě Rust ┬Ě Go ┬Ě Lua** Ôťů ÔÇö same `/v1/rpc` wire format.

### Parametric core

- **Equations / global parameters** Ôťů ÔÇö `.equations`, mathjs.
- **Configurations / variants** Ôťů ÔÇö per-file param overrides, BOM rollup.
- **Materials database** Ôťů ÔÇö `.material` kind, 200 seeded materials.
- **Two coexisting kernels** Ôťů ÔÇö `.jscad` (mesh) + `.feature` (OCCT BRep), shared `.sketch`/`.assembly`/`.drawing`.
- **Pure-Python B-rep + NURBS kernel** Ôťů ÔÇö validated `Body` topology, tolerant booleans, G1/G2 fillets, closest-point, hardened SSI, parametric history DAG with persistent face naming. 620 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests.

### Geometry kernel ÔÇö depth

The pure-Python kernel (`packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/`) now matches Rhino/Blender-class construction depth with an analytic foundation:

| Module | Description | Status |
|---|---|---|
| **`brep.py`** | B-rep topology: radial-edge `BodyÔćĺSolidÔćĺShellÔćĺFaceÔćĺLoopÔćĺCoedgeÔćĺEdgeÔćĺVertex`, nine Euler operators, EulerÔÇôPoincar├ę invariant enforced | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/topology_euler_check.py`** | **BREP-TOPOLOGY-EULER-CHECK**: full generalised Euler-Poincar├ę verifier V-E+F = 2(S-G)+H (Mantyla 1988 ┬ž6; Hoffmann 1989 ┬ž5); `verify_euler_topology(Body)` + `verify_euler_topology_from_dict(faces, ...)` + `EulerCheckReport` dataclass; union-find shell count; oracle helpers for cube/torus/disjoint cubes; LLM tool `brep_verify_euler_topology`; 16 hermetic tests (cube ¤ç=2, torus ¤ç=0, disjoint cubes S=2/¤ç=4, inner loops, violation flags). Pure-Python. CAVEATS: genus/inner-loops require caller hints in dict mode; vertex dedup after sew/heal may cause spurious failure (degenerate_vertices_hint flag). | Ôťů shipped |
| **`brep_build.py`** | Analytic verbs (box/cylinder/sphere/Coons patch) Ôćĺ `validate_body`-clean `Body` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 ┬ž3 + Mantyla 1988 ┬ž6); counts dangling / boundary / manifold / non-manifold edges; isolated vertices; degenerate (zero-length) edges; union-find shell connectivity components; EulerÔÇôPoincar├ę V-E+F residual; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold`; 11 hermetic oracle tests (closed cube Ôćĺ manifold=12/boundary=0/components=1; open box Ôćĺ boundary=4/manifold=8; T-shape Ôćĺ nonmanifoldÔëą1; two disconnected cubes Ôćĺ components=2). Pure-Python, no OCCT. | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 ┬ž3 + Mantyla 1988 ┬ž6); manifold/boundary/nonmanifold/dangling counts; isolated vertices; degenerate edges; union-find shell components; EulerÔÇôPoincar├ę V-E+F; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/vertex_degree_check.py`** | **BREP-VERTEX-DEGREE-CHECK**: count incident edges per vertex; flag boundary (degree < expected_degree) and non-manifold (degree > expected_degree + 2); `VertexDegreeReport` dataclass with `num_vertices`, `degree_histogram` (dict[int,int]), `num_boundary_vertices`, `num_non_manifold_vertices`, `max_degree`, `irregular_vertex_indices`, `honest_caveat`; `check_vertex_degrees(brep_or_mesh, expected_degree=4)`; oracle helpers for cube + tetrahedron; LLM tool `brep_check_vertex_degrees`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests. Pure-Python. CAVEATS: edge-based degree only ÔÇö does NOT analyse face-fan angular order or non-manifold edges at high-degree vertices. Refs: Mantyla 1988 ┬ž3.4; Hoffmann 1989 ┬ž4. | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/brep_edge_metrics.py`** | **BREP-SUM-EDGE-LENGTHS**: total edge length + kind/curve-type breakdowns for cutting-cost estimation; `total_edge_length` / `edge_length_by_kind` / `edges_by_curve_type` / `compute_edge_metrics`; linearÔćĺEuclidean, circularÔćĺradius├Śangle, freeformÔćĺadaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre (Stoer-Bulirsch ┬ž3 + Piegl-Tiller ┬ž5.4); oracles: 100├Ś50 rect=300, unit cube=12, sphere 12 great-circle r=50=3769.91; LLM tools `brep_total_edge_length` + `brep_edge_length_by_kind`; 20 hermetic tests | Ôťů shipped |
| **`boolean.py`** | Tolerant pure-Python solid booleans (regularised cut/fuse/common) over the primitive matrix, 2-manifold result | Ôťů shipped |
| **`fillet_solid.py` / `chamfer.py`** | G1/G2 surface blend + edge fillet + variable chamfer | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/auto_chamfer.py`** | Auto-chamfer recommendation (ISO 13715): dihedral-angle classification Ôćĺ safety / manufacturing / cosmetic / no-chamfer; `brep_recommend_chamfers` + `brep_apply_chamfer_recommendations` LLM tools | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/auto_fillet.py`** | Auto-fillet recommendation engine (Peterson 1974 + Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002) ÔÇö classifies interior/exterior corners, sizes radii per design intent, estimates Kt reduction; LLM tools `brep_recommend_fillets` + `brep_apply_fillet_recommendations` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | BREP-FILLET-RECOMMEND-RADIUS ÔÇö per-edge radius recommendation combining 4 criteria: (1) face-size cap rÔëĄface_min/4 (Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž4), (2) Peterson 1974 ┬ž2.3 notch Kt formula r=0.1├Śnotch_depth (tension+bending, analytic only, NOT FEA), (3) material stress-relief floor rÔëąfactor├Śwall_thickness (steel 0.05, cast_iron 0.08, etc.), (4) tool constraint rÔëątool_radius_mm + sharp-edge preservation; `RadiusRecommendation` dataclass with criteria_radii transparency dict; LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius`; 21 hermetic oracle tests | Ôťů shipped |
| **`fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | Per-edge fillet radius recommendation (Peterson 1974 ┬ž2.3; Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002 ┬ž4) ÔÇö LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`chamfer_recommend_size.py`** | Per-edge chamfer size recommendation (Drozda-Wick ┬ž3-7; DIN 74:1974 Form A/B; ISO 13715:2017 ┬ž5) ÔÇö deburring 0.5mm├Ś45┬░; countersink; cosmetic; manufacturing ÔÇö LLM tool `brep_recommend_chamfer_size`; **asymmetric chamfers (e.g. 30┬░├Ś60┬░, 1├Ś2 leg ratio) Ôťů** via `recommend_asymmetric_chamfer(edge, application, ratio_a_to_b)` + `ratio=` param on `recommend_chamfer_size()`; `AsymmetricChamferRecommendation` dataclass with `leg_a_mm`, `leg_b_mm`, `angle_a_deg`, `angle_b_deg`, `is_symmetric`; angles derived from `atan2(leg_b, leg_a)`; symmetric 45┬░ path unchanged (ratio=1.0 default, backward compatible) | Ôťů shipped |
| **`offset.py`** | Exact-distance surface/curve/loop offsets with self-intersection trim | Ôťů shipped |
| **`surface_offset.py`** | NURBS surface offset (Tiller-Hanson 1984 + Hoschek 1988): CP face-normal displacement, iterative isotropic-error refinement, M├Âller 1997 self-intersection detection, local-loop trim; `nurbs_surface_offset` LLM tool; 4 analytical oracle tests (plane/cylinder/sphere/C-shape) | Ôťů shipped |
| **`curve_offset_2d.py`** | NURBS 2D curve offset + self-intersection trim (Tiller-Hanson 1984) ÔÇö foundation for flat patterns, CAM toolpath offset, hatch fill; **NURBS-CURVE-OFFSET-2D** adds `Offset2DResult` (max/mean actual offset, self-intersection count, honest caveat) + `offset_nurbs_curve_2d(curve, offset_distance_mm, side)` wrapper + LLM tool `nurbs_offset_curve_2d`; HONEST: linear CP-offset approx (Piegl-Tiller ┬ž10.7), NOT exact NURBS offset; max_actual_offset_mm may differ from target for high-curvature regions; 26 hermetic tests | Ôťů shipped |
| **`coons.py`** | Boundary-interpolation Coons patches, exact to 1e-12 | Ôťů shipped |
| **`network_surface.py`** | N-sided patch: N=3 Hosaka-Kimura triangular Coons, N=4 Gregory twist-corrected Coons, NÔëą5 Wachspress polygon blend; `fairness_metric` bending energy; LLM tool `nurbs_n_sided_patch` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`inversion.py`** | Closest-point / point-inversion (Piegl 6.1, analytic partials on rational surfaces) | Ôťů shipped |
| **`curve_projection.py`** | PointÔćĺcurve / pointÔćĺsurface projection (Newton-Raphson + arc-length fallback, Hu-Wallner 2006); `ProjectionResult` dataclass; `distance_curve_to_curve`; LLM tool `nurbs_project_point` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations; **NURBS-CURVE-SELF-INTERSECT enhanced** ÔÇö `curve_self_intersect_robust`: Piegl-Tiller ┬ž5.5 AABB-tree recursive subdivision + Sederberg 1985 bisection stop criterion + NewtonÔÇôRaphson on \|C(t1)ÔłĺC(t2)\|┬▓; figure-8 B├ęzier oracle verified ÔëĄ1e-9; 33 new tests green; honest-flag: multiplicity-3 intersections not detected | Ôťů shipped |
| **`intersection_degen.py` ÔÇö Degenerate SSI (Legendre canonical forms)** | `detect_degenerate_ssi` + `compute_degenerate_ssi_curve` + `ssi_extended`; handles coaxial cylinders, coplanar planes, sphere-tangent-plane, Legendre/Weierstrass conic section for tangent quadric pairs; LLM tool `nurbs_ssi_with_degenerate_check` registered; 27 hermetic tests with analytical oracles | Ôťů shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations | Ôťů shipped |
| **`edge_curve_from_face_pair.py`** | B-rep edge-curve extraction: SSI Ôćĺ longest branch Ôćĺ degree-3 NURBS fit + UV traces on both faces (Sederberg-Parry 1986 / Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬ž7); LLM tool `brep_extract_edge_curve_from_faces` | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/edge_convexity.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CONVEXITY**: classify B-rep edge as convex / concave / tangent / smooth / sharp-convex / sharp-concave from sampled face normals (no B-rep topology access required). `EdgeSample(point_xyz_mm, face_a_normal, face_b_normal, edge_tangent)` / `SampledEdgeConvexityReport(classification, mean_dihedral_deg, max_dihedral_deg, min_dihedral_deg, num_samples, honest_caveat)` / `classify_edge_convexity(samples, tangent_tol_deg=2.0, sharp_threshold_deg=135.0)`. Sign convention: cross(n_a, n_b) ┬Ě edge_tangent > 0 Ôćĺ convex; < 0 Ôćĺ concave; Ôëł 0 Ôćĺ smooth/tangent. Dihedral = arccos(n_a ┬Ě n_b) Ôłł [0┬░, 180┬░]. "sharp-convex" / "sharp-concave" when dihedral > sharp_threshold_deg. Also ships B-rep-topology API: `EdgeClass` / `EdgeConvexityReport` / `classify_edges` / `classify_body_edges`. LLM tools `brep_classify_edges` (topology) + `geom_classify_edge_convexity` (sampled-normals) registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 16 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: sampled API requires pre-evaluated outward normals from the caller ÔÇö does NOT parse B-rep topology directly; inverted normals flip the convex/concave label; tangent_tol_deg threshold is caller-tunable. Refs: Mantyla 1988 ┬ž5; Hoffmann 1989 ┬ž5.3. | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/edge_curve_extend.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CURVE-EXTEND**: extend a B-rep edge's underlying NurbsCurve beyond its parametric domain by ╬öL mm, preserving G1 or G2 continuity at the join. G1: cubic B├ęzier tangent-extrapolation (Piegl & Tiller ┬ž10.4; Mortenson ┬ž3.7); G2 Ôťů: quintic B├ęzier with first 3 CPs analytically fixed from C(u_end), C'(u_end), C''(u_end) (Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬ž3.4; Piegl & Tiller ┬ž5.3) ÔÇö exact parametric second-derivative continuity at join. `extend_edge_curve(curve, delta_length_mm, end, continuity)` Ôćĺ `EdgeExtendResult(..., end_continuity_achieved)`. `end_continuity_achieved` returns "G1" or "G2". Helpers `_make_g1_extension` / `_make_g2_extension` exported. LLM tool `brep_extend_edge_curve` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 30 hermetic tests (21 original G1 + 9 new G2). **Honest caveats**: G3 (jerk) continuity NOT enforced; G2 arc length Ôëł delta_length_mm (exact only for zero-curvature). Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž10.4, ┬ž5.3; Mortenson ┬ž3.7; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬ž3.4. | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/edge_chamfer_variable.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CHAMFER-VARIABLE**: variable-width chamfer strip along a 2D edge curve for ergonomic edge treatments (handle bevels with grip-width variations). Width ramps linearly from `width_start_mm` (t=0) to `width_end_mm` (t=1) via `w(t) = w_start + t*(w_end-w_start)`; both sides offset perpendicularly by `w(t)/2`. `ChamferVariableSpec` / `ChamferVariableResult` dataclasses; `generate_variable_chamfer(spec)` entry point. LLM tool `brep_generate_variable_chamfer` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 27 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: input is a 2D polyline only ÔÇö 3D space-curve chamfer that modifies B-rep solid topology is not yet supported (requires generalising `chamfer.py` topology surgery to curved edges, P2/P3 scope). Strip points are a sampled polyline approximation, not an exact NURBS offset curve. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž10.5 (Variable offsets); Mortenson ┬ž9.3 (Edge blends). | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/history/`** | Parametric history DAG + `feature_id::role::fingerprint` persistent naming ÔÇö downstream fillet survives upstream parameter edits | Ôťů shipped |
| **G3 surfacing** | `feature_blend_srf_g3` (surfacing.py:1376) + `feature_g3_chain_blend` (surfacing.py:1894) registered LLM tools; `blend_srf_g3` / `curvature_rate_continuity_residual` / `zebra_stripe` / `reflection_lines` / `curvature_comb` exported from `geom/__init__.py`; `feature_zebra_analysis` + `feature_isophote_analysis` wired | Ôťů shipped |
| **General solid boolean** | NURBS-faced / non-axis-aligned solids; classification-first B-rep pipeline (SSI seeds Ôćĺ whole-face classify Ôćĺ sew); analytic fast-paths for box/sphere/cylinder; LLM tool registered (`nurbs_solid_boolean`); 18 hermetic tests ÔÇö sphereÔłębox, Steinmetz, freeform NURBS, self-intersection guard | Ôťů shipped |
| **General solid boolean** | NURBS├ŚNURBS solid boolean with exact UV-trim at SSI curves (GK-P-B); whole-face fallback retained for tangential cases; 22 hermetic tests green | Ôťů shipped |
| **Body-body imprint with edge tagging** | `imprint_body(target, tool, mode)` in `geom/imprint.py`: projects all tool edges onto target faces via `imprint_curve_on_face`, tags new edges with `ImprintTag(source_body_id, source_edge_id)`. `mode='intersect'` AABB+plane proximity filter; `mode='all'` for design-intent transfer. LLM tool `brep_imprint_body` registered in plugin. 4 oracle tests (box-on-box footprint, provenance coverage, no-intersect no-op, mode comparison). | Ôťů shipped |
| **Surface fairing + Sapidis curve fairing** | `surface_fairing.py`: `fair_surface()` (iterative discrete-Laplacian control-net smoothing, 3 boundary modes) + `fair_surface_bend()` (sparse bending-energy linear solve via scipy.sparse); `curve_toolkit.py`: `fair_curve(sapidis=True)` (Sapidis & Farin 1994 iterative knot removal + insertion); LLM tools `surface_fair` + `curve_fair` registered; 19 hermetic tests (¤â(z) oracle, boundary preservation, energy-monotone, Sapidis curvature-variance reduction) | Ôťů shipped |
| **Variable-radius G2 fillet (Stadler 2006)** | `variable_radius_fillet_g2` + `fillet_radius_field_planner` in `geom/surface_fillet.py`; `nurbs_fillet_variable_g2` LLM tool registered; G2 continuity along radius gradient via cubic Hermite curvature blending; 48 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests | Ôťů shipped |
| **GK-P: Variable-section edge blend (Vida-Martin-Varady 1994)** | `edge_blend.py` ÔÇö `CrossSection` (rect/circle/ellipse/polygon), `variable_section_blend` (linear / cubic_hermite / C2 methods), `morph_cross_sections` (Bezier corner rounding per Hartmann 1998); `nurbs_edge_blend_variable_section` LLM tool registered; exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 37 tests, 4 analytical oracles (volume, rectÔćĺcircle morph, C1 continuity, volume monotonic) | Ôťů shipped |
| **Post-Boolean continuity recovery (G1/G2 seam blending)** | `recover_continuity_at_seam` / `recover_continuity_body` in `geom/continuity_recovery.py`; degree-3 Hermite blend strip inserted at G0-only seams; G1 tangent < 5┬░ + G2 curvature-rate residual oracle; `brep_recover_continuity` LLM tool; 29 hermetic tests green. | Ôťů shipped |
| **`geom/wall_thickness.py`** | Wall-thickness analysis with material guidelines ÔÇö `analyze_wall_thickness` (SDF-ray-cast, Stroud-Nagy ┬ž17.2), `material_thickness_guideline` (ABS/PP/PE/PC/Nylon/PVC/ÔÇŽ), `flag_thin_walls`; LLM tools `brep_analyze_wall_thickness` + `brep_check_moldability` Ôťů | Ôťů shipped |
| **GK-P: Mold parting surface construction (Yu-Fan 2003)** | `mold_parting_surface.py`: `construct_parting_surface` (radial ruled quads from parting line to mold bbox), `construct_with_shutoff_inserts` (undercut shutoff patches), `validate_parting_surface`; LLM tool `brep_construct_parting_surface` registered in `kerf-mold`; 22 hermetic oracle tests pass | Ôťů shipped |
| **GK-P11: Isophote / Environment-Map (EMap) continuity analyser** | Dedicated `geom/isophote_analyzer.py` module: `IsophoteSpec` (surface, view_direction_xyz, angle_bands_deg, uv_samples_u, uv_samples_v) / `IsophoteReport` (isophote_curves, max_isophote_curvature, num_discontinuities, fairness_score, warnings, honest_caveat) / `analyze_isophotes(spec)`. Algorithm: analytic NURBS normal grid Ôćĺ ╬╝(u,v)=n╠é┬ĚL╠é Ôćĺ marching-squares isoline extraction at each requested angle band Ôćĺ Menger isoline curvature + fairness = exp(Ôłĺkink_rate) Ôćĺ discontinuity detection (EMap band-jump Ôëą 2). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. LLM tool `nurbs_analyze_isophotes` registered in `plugin.py`. 25 hermetic tests green. Refs: Forsey & Bartels 1995; Hagen & Bonneau 2000 ┬ž4; Lorensen & Cline 1987; Pottmann & Wallner 2001 ┬ž10. **HONEST CAVEATS**: fairness_score + max_isophote_curvature are UV-parameter-space metrics only ÔÇö not a substitute for curvature-comb, zebra/reflection-line analysis, or G2/G3 formal continuity checks; single viewing direction; non-uniform knot spacing may cause parameterisation artefacts. | Ôťů shipped |

| **`geom/face_plane_deviation.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PLANE-DEVIATION**: given a pre-sampled point cloud on a B-rep face (intended-planar or actual-NURBS surface), compute max and RMS deviation from the SVD least-squares best-fit plane (Pratt 1987 ┬ž3; Eberly ┬ž6.6); returns `FacePlaneDeviationReport` (plane: `PlaneFit` with origin_xyz_mm/normal_xyz/d, max_deviation_mm, rms_deviation_mm, num_samples, is_planar, classification, honest_caveat). | **`geom/face_developable_check.py`** | **BREP-FACE-DEVELOPABLE-CHECK**: verify if a B-rep face is developable (can be unrolled flat without stretching). **GK-P23: In-process isotropic remesh fallback** Ôťů ÔÇö `mesh_isotropic_remesh.py` ÔÇö Botsch-Kobbelt (2004) iterative pipeline: (1) split edges > 4/3┬ĚL, (2) collapse interior edges < 4/5┬ĚL, (3) flip edges to equalise vertex valence toward 6, (4) tangential Laplacian smoothing. Dataclasses: `TriangleMesh` (vertices_xyz_mm, faces), `IsotropicRemeshSpec` (mesh, target_edge_length_mm, num_iterations=5, tangential_smoothing=True, preserve_boundary=True), `IsotropicRemeshReport` (output_mesh, edge_length_min/max/mean/stdev_mm, num_splits/collapses/flips/smooths_total, valence_variance, honest_caveat). `isotropic_remesh(spec)` function. LLM tool `mesh_isotropic_remesh` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`. 24 hermetic tests green (dataclass structure; square plane 2-tri Ôćĺ many uniform triangles; stdev decreases vs coarse input; boundary corners preserved; tetrahedron subdivided; empty/invalid/zero-iter edge cases; operation counters; valence variance; package re-export). HONEST CAVEATS: pure-Python + NumPy; slower than instant_meshes binary for > 50k triangles (O(N) per pass edge-map rebuild); output is triangle-only ÔÇö quad remesh stays in `quad_remesh.py`; not as feature-complete as instantmeshes for anisotropic or feature-aligned remeshing.

**GK-P50: NURBS arc-length inversion** Ôťů ÔÇö `invert_arc_length` (NewtonÔÇôRaphson + bisection fall-back; Piegl & Tiller ┬ž11.2 + Sederberg CAGD ┬ž6.4). Returns `ArcLengthInvertResult{t_param, residual_mm, iterations, honest_caveat}`. Used for chord-length parameterisation, even-spaced CAM toolpaths, rebar layout. Wired as `nurbs_invert_arc_length` LLM tool. 19 tests green. Caveat: highly non-uniform knot vectors may trigger bisection fall-back (still converges, just slower).

**GK-P (parity) series in flight.** A four-agent survey of Kerf vs ~18 kernel-relevant CADs found a concrete, finite gap list. GK-01..GK-139 are landed. The `GK-P` series (tracked in `tasks.md`) closes the remaining gaps:

- **Foundational kernel** ÔÇö general solid boolean for NURBS-faced bodies, MatchSrf G3, isophote/EMap, Stam limit-tangents + G1 at extraordinary SubD points, fractional creases, analytic surface derivatives.
