- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, LSCM UV unwrap.
- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement Ôťů, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, LSCM UV unwrap.
- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, LSCM UV unwrap. Stam-exact limit curvature evaluation Ôťů.
- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, LSCM UV unwrap. **Geodesic distance via heat method (Crane et al. 2013) Ôťů** ÔÇö cotangent Laplacian + Poisson solve; `subd_geodesic_distance` LLM tool wired (GK-P49).
- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, UV unwrap LSCM + ARAP + mesh atlas Ôťů.
- **SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement, SDF CSG + marching-cubes, sculpt brush engine, isotropic remesh, surface-snap retopo, LSCM UV unwrap; **harmonic cage coords Ôťů** (Joshi 2007).
- **NURBS surface optimal reparametrization (LSCM + ARAP)** Ôťů ÔÇö GK-P50: `reparametrize_lscm` / `reparametrize_arap` / `distortion_metric` / `reparam_compare`; LLM tool `nurbs_reparametrize_optimal`; 21 hermetic tests green.
- **SUBD-CAGE-RING-FROM-EDGE** Ôťů ÔÇö `compute_edge_ring(cage, start_edge)` returns `EdgeRingResult(edge_indices, is_closed, is_degenerate, transition_face_indices)`; follows opposite edges across quad faces (Maya/Blender Bridge ring); cube Ôćĺ 4-ring closed; torus Ôćĺ correct U/V ring lengths; open at boundary; degenerate flag for non-quad faces; LLM tool `subd_compute_edge_ring`; 25 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_ring.py`.
- **SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-LOOP-SELECT** Ôťů ÔÇö `select_edge_loop(cage_mesh, start_edge_idx)` returns `EdgeLoopResult(edge_indices, vertex_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_vertex_valences, honest_caveat)`; opposite-edge chain walk (Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni 2013 ┬ž3.2); torus Ôćĺ closed loops; cube (valence-3) Ôćĺ terminates; cylinder axial edge Ôćĺ closed ring; LLM tool `subd_select_edge_loop`; 25 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_loop_select.py`.
- **SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** Ôťů ÔÇö `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; face-dual of edge-loop walk: hops through opposite-edge adjacent quads; walk_direction 0/1 gives orthogonal rings on regular tori; 4├Ś6 torus dir=0Ôćĺring 4, dir=1Ôćĺring 6; cube Ôćĺ closed 4-ring; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 Ôćĺ closed ring 12; mixed tri/quad Ôćĺ terminated; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; honest: quads only ÔÇö non-quad terminates; 20 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) ┬ž3.2; Hoppe (1996) ┬ž3.2.
- **SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** Ôťů ÔÇö `collapse_edge(cage: SubdCage, v_keep, v_remove, midpoint=True)` Ôćĺ `EdgeCollapseResult(new_cage, num_vertices_removed, num_faces_removed, collapsed_position_xyz_mm, degenerate_faces_removed, became_invalid, honest_caveat)`; topology only ÔÇö no QEM (caller chooses edge); midpoint or endpoint placement; non-adjacent pair Ôćĺ became_invalid=True; cube Ôćĺ 7 verts, 2 faces removed Ôťô; midpoint/endpoint position oracles Ôťô; 14 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1993); Hoppe (1996) ┬ž3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) ┬ž3; Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) ┬ž4.
- **SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** Ôťů ÔÇö `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices)` merges N cage vertices into centroid v_c; degenerate faces removed; 2-vertex merge Ôëí edge collapse; 4-corner merge on isolated quad collapses it entirely; non-adjacent merge Ôćĺ no faces removed; empty/single list Ôćĺ no-op; duplicates deduplicated; 3-vertex centroid oracle Ôťô; all face indices valid; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; honest: centroid only ÔÇö no QEM (Garland-Heckbert 1997); 20 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) ┬ž3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) ┬ž3.
- **SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-FLIP** Ôťů ÔÇö `flip_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx)` returns `EdgeFlipResult(new_cage_faces, num_edges_flipped, flipped_edge_indices, honest_caveat)`; topological flip of shared edge (v_a,v_b) in two adjacent triangles Ôćĺ T1'=(v_a,v_c,v_d) + T2'=(v_b,v_d,v_c); ABC+BCD flip Ôćĺ {A,B,D}+{A,C,D} Ôťô; double flip restores original topology Ôťô; boundary edge Ôćĺ ValueError; non-manifold edge Ôćĺ ValueError; quad face Ôćĺ ValueError; LLM tool `subd_flip_edge`; honest: topological only ÔÇö NO Delaunay in-circle test; triangles only; 14 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_flip.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) ┬ž3; Edelsbrunner (2001) ┬ž2.
- **SUBD-CAGE-AREA** Ôťů ÔÇö `compute_cage_area(cage)` returns `CageAreaReport(total_cage_area_mm2, estimated_limit_surface_area_mm2, per_face_areas, min_face_area_mm2, max_face_area_mm2, degenerate_face_indices, num_quads, num_tris, num_ngons, honest_caveat)`; unit cube Ôćĺ 6 mm┬▓ cage, 5.64 mm┬▓ limit estimate Ôťô; degenerate triangle flagged Ôťô; pyramid 1 quad+4 tris area oracle Ôťô; pentagon n-gon exact Ôťô; hexagon n-gon Ôťô; area scales k┬▓ Ôťô; LLM tool `subd_compute_cage_area`; 23 tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/cage_area.py`. HONEST: limit-surface estimate is empirical ├Ś0.94 ÔÇö NOT exact eigenanalysis; error can exceed 5% for extraordinary-vertex-heavy cages. Refs: Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD ┬ž10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH ┬ž2; Zorin-Schr├Âder (2000) ┬ž3.
- **SUBD-CAGE-DUAL-MESH** Ôťů ÔÇö `compute_dual_mesh(cage_mesh)` returns `DualMeshResult(dual_vertices, dual_faces, num_irregular_dual_faces, honest_caveat)`; dual vertices = one face centroid per primal face; dual faces = CCW-ordered ring of neighboring face centroids per primal vertex (atan2 angular sort on tangent plane); cube oracle: 8 verts + 6 quads Ôćĺ 6 dual verts + 8 triangular dual faces (combinatorial octahedron), 0 irregular; 4├Ś4 torus (all valence-4) Ôćĺ 16 dual verts + 16 quad dual faces, 0 irregular; 2├Ś2 plane grid Ôćĺ 4 dual verts + 9 dual faces, boundary vertices counted irregular; cylinder barrel (open) Ôćĺ correct dual vertex/face count, boundary rings flagged irregular; all dual face indices valid; LLM tool `subd_compute_dual_mesh`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 28 oracle-asserted tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/dual_mesh.py`. HONEST: closed manifold meshes only for complete dual faces ÔÇö boundary primal edges produce INCOMPLETE (open) dual faces; angular sort (atan2) works on convex vertex stars but may mis-order concave or nearly co-planar stars; dual vertices are primal face centroids, NOT CC limit-surface points; non-manifold vertices produce topologically undefined dual faces. Refs: Bossen-Heckbert (1996) ┬ž3.1; Bommes-L├ęvy-Pietroni (2013) ┬ž3.2.
- **Architectural geometry** ÔÇö B-repÔćĺ2D tessellate, roof/curtain-wall/corridor generators, wall compound-layer offset, hatch/section-fill.
- **Oblique projection (cabinet + cavalier + general) per Bertoline ┬ž11 + ISO 5456-2** Ôťů ÔÇö 30┬░/45┬░/user-angle shear; 1:1:0.5 cabinet; 1:1:1 cavalier; isometric 120┬░-axis; hidden-line classification; LLM tool `drawing_oblique_projection` ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/oblique_projection.py`
- **Sketcher** ÔÇö collinear constraint, ellipse solver entity, G2 continuity.
- **Interop** ÔÇö 3DM write with readÔćĺwriteÔćĺread Hausdorff oracle.
- **Composite curve G2 audit + upgrade** Ôťů ÔÇö `composite_g2.py`: audit + auto-blend (cubic Hermite / quintic Bezier); LLM tools registered; 27 tests green.
- **NURBS composite tangent match (G1/G2)** Ôťů ÔÇö `composite_tangent_match.py`: `match_composite_tangents(curves, target="G1"|"G2")` ÔÇö Klass 1980 ┬ž3 / Farin ┬ž8.4 bisector construction for G1; Piegl-Tiller ┬ž7.3 second-derivative constraint for G2; returns `CompositeMatchResult` (adjusted_curves, max_cp_displacement, residual_tangent_error_per_seam, g2_converged); G2 non-convergence flag when curvature magnitudes differ by >10├Ś; `nurbs_match_composite_tangents` LLM tool registered; 19 tests green.
- **Precise NURBS arc-length (Gauss-Legendre + adaptive subdivision)** Ôťů ÔÇö `arc_length_precise` (5-pt GL + bounded-error recursive bisection, rel_tol/abs_tol contract); `arc_length_parametrize_gauss` (sÔćöt lookup via bisection on cumulative integral); `reparametrize_arclength_gauss`; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_arc_length`; 13 analytic-oracle tests (straight-line ÔëĄ1e-12, circle 2¤Ç ÔëĄ1e-9, bounded-error, round-trip ┬▒1e-6).
- **Multi-plane section + serial sections (ISO 128-30)** Ôťů ÔÇö `section_multi_plane.py`: `cut_body_with_planes` (parallel/perpendicular/arbitrary), `generate_serial_sections` (N evenly-spaced planes along axis), `generate_corner_detail_sections` (3 perpendicular planes at a corner), `combine_section_views_for_drawing` (grid/linear Bertoline layout); LLM tools `brep_multi_plane_section` + `brep_serial_sections` registered; 40 hermetic tests with analytic-oracle assertions (cube 10├Ś10 square sections, cylinder unit-circle radius within 5e-3).

### Mechanical / CAD

- **OCCT `.feature` Phase 2/3** Ôťů ÔÇö Pad/Pocket/Revolve/Hole/Fillet/Chamfer/Shell/Sweep/Loft/Push-Pull/Linear-Polar-Mirror patterns; face/edge gumball.
- **2D sketcher v1 + v2** Ôťů ÔÇö full constraint set, trim/extend, ellipse, B-spline, bezier, fillet, mirror, patterns.
- **Assembly model + 3D mates** Ôťů ÔÇö coincident/concentric/parallel/perp/distance/angle/tangent; gradient-descent solver.
- **Assembly clash detection UI** Ôťů ÔÇö OBB-SAT + BVH + tri-tri backend; Check Clashes side panel with pair list (part A / part B / severity / Jump-to); viewport highlight via `highlightFaces` hook ÔÇö parity with SOLIDWORKS Interference / Fusion / Onshape clash detection.
- **Assembly clash detection** Ôťů ÔÇö hard/clearance/coincident OBB-SAT + triangle-mesh narrow phase; cross-discipline `by_discipline_pair` summary; real OBB fallback Ôťů: when a component has no `bbox` but carries a `step_blob` / `step_blob_ref`, a tight PCA-OBB is computed from the STEP geometry and SHA-256 cached ÔÇö no more 1 mm┬│ approximation; unit-box fallback retained only when neither bbox nor STEP is available, with an explicit warning in `errors`.
- **Interference volume metric (Stroud-Nagy ┬ž10)** Ôťů ÔÇö exact/MC/voxel intersection volume; interference_severity score [0,1]; all-pairs assembly matrix; LLM tools `brep_interference_volume` + `brep_assembly_interference_matrix`.
- **Assembly mate inspector + validation** Ôťů ÔÇö validate joint geometries (concentric/coincident/distance/angle/tangent/parallel/perpendicular) between two B-rep bodies; residual + correction hints; auto-detect candidate mates by geometric similarity; full-assembly DOF accounting; `brep_validate_mate` + `brep_detect_mates` LLM tools; ASME Y14.5 ┬ž11 tolerance model. `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/mate_inspector.py`
- **Tolerance stack-up** Ôťů ÔÇö worst-case/RSS/Monte-Carlo + auto chain-walk.
- **GD&T frame validation (ASME Y14.5-2018)** Ôťů ÔÇö structural well-formedness per ┬ž3.4/┬ž6/┬ž9/┬ž10/┬ž12: symbolÔÇômodifier compatibility, datum requirements by tolerance category, duplicate-datum detection, bonus tolerance (MMC/LMC ┬ž6.3), canonical string round-trip; `gdt_validate_frame` + `gdt_parse_frame` LLM tools.
- **2D drawings** Ôťů ÔÇö multi-sheet, dimensions, GD&T frames, section hatching, leaders/balloons, centerlines.
- **3D PMI + GD&T annotation UI** Ôťů ÔÇö ISO 1101 GD&T toolbar (DrawingToolbar + GdntToolbar) with all 14 characteristics; datum A/B/C placement; FCF click-to-place modal with tolerance value, diameter zone, material-condition modifier, datum refs; SVG FCF glyphs (FcfGlyph/DatumGlyph) rendered inline per standard; 3D PMI overlay (Pmi3DOverlay) projects FCF labels into the three.js viewport; annotations persist via addFcf/addDatumLabel in the drawing data model.
- **Auto-dim ISO 129-1:2018** Ôťů ÔÇö chain / baseline / mixed dimensioning (┬ž5.1); extension-line gap + overshoot (┬ž5.4); 10 mm line spacing; leader lines at preferred 15┬░ angles (┬ž10); symmetric / unilateral / limit tolerance formats (┬ž8); compliance validator; 2 LLM tools (`drawing_auto_dimension_iso`, `drawing_validate_iso`).
- **Auto 6-view + iso projection (ISO 128-30 / Bertoline 5e)** Ôťů ÔÇö `drawings/projections.py`: `generate_six_view_drawing` (front/back/top/bottom/left/right + iso); third-angle (ANSI/ASME Y14.3) and first-angle (ISO/DIN) layout; hidden-line removal per view via ray-cast depth test; `compute_projection_silhouette`; `drawing_auto_views` LLM tool; standard isometric 120┬░ axis property validated (ISO 5456-3).
- **Section view auto-cutaway + ISO 128-30 hatch** Ôťů ÔÇö `cut_body_with_plane` + `hatch_cross_section` + `section_view_for_drawing`; marching-triangles half-body clipping; iron/concrete/plastic material hatch patterns; cutting-plane marker + Bertoline ┬ž11 arrow indicators; LLM tool `brep_section_view`.
- **Measurement chain auto-extraction (ASME Y14.5 + ISO 129)** Ôťů ÔÇö `extract_measurement_chain` generates a complete inspection dimension chain for a B-rep body: A/B/C datum-frame inference (┬ž3.4), per-feature DOF coverage (holes: diameter + depth + 2 position dims), redundancy detection (ISO 129-1 ┬ž6 no-closed-chain rule), `generate_inspection_report` in ISO129 or ASME14.5 format; LLM tools `drawing_measurement_chain` + `drawing_inspection_report` wired.
- **2D drawings** Ôťů ÔÇö multi-sheet, dimensions, GD&T frames, section hatching, leaders/balloons, centerlines. NURBS silhouette projection to plane (Hertzmann 2000) Ôťů ÔÇö sign-change grid locus, NURBS curve fit, visible/hidden layer output.
- **NURBS surfacing (Phase 4)** Ôťů ÔÇö sweep1/2/network/blend/loft + `surface_continuity` (C0ÔÇôC2/G0ÔÇôG2); surface-direct boolean; trim-by-curve; curvature-comb viz; zebra/reflection-line viewport toggle. G3 *enforcement* on the OCCT side is structurally impossible (absent from OCCT's type system); pure-Python is the G3 path.
- **NURBS surfacing (Phase 4a ÔÇö jewelry priority)** Ôťů ÔÇö `opSweep2` (two-rail sweep via `BRepFill_PipeShell`-style RMF midline, `sweep2_to_body` in `brep_build.py`), `opNetworkSrf` (Gordon/Coons-Gordon four-curve network, `network_srf_to_body`), `opBlendSrf` (G1/G2 Bezier blend strip, `blend_srf_to_body`); all three registered as LLM tools (`feature_sweep2`, `feature_network_srf`, `feature_blend_srf` in `surfacing.py`); 33 hermetic `validate_body`-clean tests in `test_phase4a_jewelry_surfacing.py`; scenario fixtures in `tests/fixtures/`.
- **Trim-loop auto-heal (T-junctions, dead loops, orientation)** Ôťů ÔÇö UV-domain repair pass: T-junction vertex merge (Sederberg-Zheng-Bakenov-Nasri 2003), dead-loop removal, CCW/CW orientation fix (Eberly shoelace), self-intersection detection; `nurbs_trim_loop_heal` LLM tool; 11 analytic-oracle tests.
- **Elliptic SSI trim (oblique plane ├Ś cylinder, GK-40 pure-Python)** Ôťů ÔÇö `_build_elliptic_face` in `trim_curve.py`: when a plane cuts a cylinder at an oblique angle the SSI curve is an ellipse; semi-minor = r, semi-major = r/cos(╬Ş) where ╬Ş = angle between plane normal and cylinder axis; ellipse centre = projection of cylinder axis onto plane; orientation axes (axis_a_dir = tilt direction in plane, axis_b_dir = n ├Ś A) stored in `AnalyticTrimLoop`; ellipse sampled as closed `_PolylineCurve3` polyline (64ÔÇô1024 pts, chord-error-adaptive); valid `Face` produced for both `keep_side='inside'` and `keep_side='outside'`; replaces the previous `BuildError` in the else-branch of `_build_ssi_trimmed_face`; 11 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (45┬░ unit cylinder semi_a=ÔłÜ2/semi_b=1, 30┬░ R=5 semi_a=10/semi_b=5, ratio oracle, axis_dirs populated/None, no BuildError, trim_face_by_ssi inside+outside return Face, AnalyticTrimLoop fields, ellipse points on cutting plane, residual < 1e-10).
- **NURBS seam control for periodic surfaces** Ôťů ÔÇö `detect_seam` / `shift_seam` / `align_seam_to_curve` in `geom/seam_control.py`; `nurbs_shift_seam` LLM tool registered; Piegl-Tiller ┬ž5.2 cyclic CP-net rotation with uniform knot rebuild; 16 analytic-oracle tests green.
- **Far-offset numerical conditioning** Ôťů ÔÇö `offset_far_correction.py` (Maekawa 1999 ┬ž6; Hoschek-Lasser 1993 ┬ž17): curvature-aware safety-distance computation (`safe_offset_distance`), adaptive local-refinement clamp (`offset_with_local_refinement`), graceful degradation with flagged unsafe parametric regions (`graceful_offset`); LLM tool `nurbs_surface_offset_robust` registered.
- **Variable-section extrude / morphing sweep** Ôťů ÔÇö `extrude_variable_section` (profile morphs per path parameter; linear / cubic-Hermite / C2 interpolation; Wang 2008 RMF frames) + `extrude_with_scaling_curve` (1-D scale taper along path) + `extrude_morph_via_rail_pair` (rail-guided profile morph); `nurbs_extrude_variable` LLM tool registered; 17 analytic-oracle tests green (constant-section degenerate, circleÔćĺsquare morph, conical-surface oracle, C2 smoothness).
- **NURBS curve/surface split at parameter** Ôťů ÔÇö `split_curve_at`, `split_curve_at_multiple`, `split_surface_at_u/v`; PieglÔÇôTiller ┬ž5.3 full-multiplicity knot insertion; rational-NURBS correct; LLM tools `nurbs_split_curve` + `nurbs_split_surface` registered (GK-P06).
- **Rhino parity** Ôťů ÔÇö 3DM I/O, SubD (Catmull-Clark), quad remesh, mesh tools, layers/display, parametric `.graph`, render output.
- **Persistent face naming** Ôťů ÔÇö sketch-anchored + topo-hash (frontend T1ÔÇôT7) plus kernel-side `feature_id::role::fingerprint` selector in the pure-Python DAG.
- **Assembly interference detection (M├Âller 1997)** Ôťů ÔÇö `detect_interference_pair` / `detect_interference_assembly` / `compute_assembly_aabb`; AABB broad-phase + M├Âller 1997 triangle-triangle narrow phase + GK-18 boolean intersection volume; severity classification (none/touch/overlap/major_overlap); LLM tools `brep_assembly_interference` + `brep_check_clearance` ÔÇö `kerf_cad_core/geom/assembly_interference.py`.

### Simulation / manufacturing

- **FEM** Ôťů ÔÇö FEniCSx + CalculiX: linear-static + modal + steady thermal + bonded contact; linear eigenvalue buckling + harmonic frequency response + random-vibration PSD; MITC4 plate/shell; acoustics FEM/BEM; high-frequency EM; electrostatics + magnetostatics; multi-axial fatigue; 2-D projection NS solver. Reference-value suite with Roark/Blevins/Incropera oracles (42 of 43 green).
- **CFD foundation** Ôťů ÔÇö 2-D laminar: potential flow (`Cp(╬Ş)=1Ôłĺ4sin┬▓╬Ş` oracle) + lid-driven cavity (Ghia Re=100 reference); 61 hermetic tests.
- **Topology optimization** Ôťů ÔÇö SIMP via FEniCSx; NURBS surface fit; multi-body.
- **CAM** Ôťů ÔÇö 2.5D + 3D parallel/waterline + lathe + 5-axis constant-tilt + 3+2 indexed; tool DB; LinuxCNC/GRBL/Fanuc posts.
- **CAM toolpath collision verifier** Ôťů ÔÇö `cam_toolpath_collision.py`: segment-by-segment holder/spindle capsule-vs-AABB (Ericson 2005 ┬ž5.5) + capsule-vs-triangle-mesh (M├Âller 1997 ┬ž6) minimum-distance checks at 1 mm sampling resolution; configurable safety margin; fixture mesh support; `cam_verify_toolpath_collision` LLM tool. Known limit: worst-case missed gap ÔëĄ step_mm ├Ś ÔłÜ2 Ôëł 1.41 mm at default 1 mm step.
- **CAM feedrate lookahead optimizer** Ôťů ÔÇö `cam_feedrate_lookahead.py`: two-pass corner lookahead (Erkorkmaz-Altintas 2001 / Altintas 2012 ┬ž5.7); V_corner = sqrt(a_max ├Ś r_blend / sin(╬Ş/2)); forward-pass acceleration + backward-pass deceleration; per-waypoint feedrate schedule + corner angles + cycle time. `cam_optimize_feedrate_lookahead` LLM tool. Supports two profile types: `"trapezoid"` (constant-accel, default, backward-compatible) and `"s-curve"` (jerk-limited, opt-in). S-curve scheduling Ôťů ÔÇö `schedule_s_curve()` implements the full 7-segment constant-jerk profile (Lambrechts-Boerlage-Steinbuch 2005 IEEE TCST / Erkorkmaz-Altintas ┬ž3.3): jerk-on accel Ôćĺ constant accel Ôćĺ jerk-off accel Ôćĺ constant velocity Ôćĺ jerk-on decel Ôćĺ constant decel Ôćĺ jerk-off decel; triangular fallback when distance too short; `SCurveProfile` dataclass; `profile_type="s-curve"` param on `optimize_feedrate` produces jerk-accurate cycle times (10ÔÇô30% longer than trapezoidal at same A_max). 16 new hermetic tests.
- **5-axis CAM UI** Ôťů ÔÇö `CAMView.jsx` mode switch (3-axis / 5-axis-indexed / 5-axis-continuous); tilt axis (A/B/C) + angle; strategy (swarf / contour-on-tilted-plane / indexed-rough); spindle vector preview; dispatches `cam_run` backend tool (`operation=5axis_finish` or `3plus2`).
- **Feed-rate optimizer** Ôťů ÔÇö Altintas 2012 chip-load model + machine acceleration cap (┬ž3.6) + tool deflection (Euler-Bernoulli); per-material/tool Vc+fz database (9 materials ├Ś 5 tool classes); forwardÔÇôbackward feed smoothing; MRR + cycle-time estimator. LLM tools: `manufacturing_optimize_feed`, `manufacturing_cycle_time`. (Altintas reference data ÔÇö NOT cutting-tool-manufacturer-certified.)
- **MANUFACTURING-TOLERANCE-COST** Ôťů ÔÇö Tolerance-cost estimation (Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž11.2 / Figure 11.4 exponential curve): `compute_tolerance_cost(tolerance_mm, process, base_cost_usd, dimension_mm)` Ôćĺ `ToleranceCostResult`; multiplier = exp(k ├Ś log10(t_max/t)); processes: turning (k=1.80, ┬▒0.012ÔÇô0.5 mm), milling (k=1.60, ┬▒0.025ÔÇô0.5 mm), grinding (k=2.50, ┬▒0.002ÔÇô0.02 mm), lapping (k=3.20, ┬▒0.0005ÔÇô0.005 mm); auto-upgrade chain (turningÔćĺgrindingÔćĺlapping) when tolerance tightens beyond process capability; ISO 286-1:2010 IT-grade mapping (`tolerance_to_IT_grade`) for IT1ÔÇôIT16; `manufacturing_tolerance_cost` LLM tool registered; 46 hermetic tests covering 4 tolerance bands ├Ś 2 processes, process-upgrade chain, IT-grade monotonicity, oracle B-D Fig 11.4 ratios, near-limit advisories, and LLM tool error paths. Honest-flag: simplified exponential fit; real cost depends on shop equipment, batch size, material hardness, and feature geometry ÔÇö treat as ┬▒30% estimate. References: Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž11.2 + Fig 11.4 (2010); ASME B89.1.5-1998; ISO 286-1:2010 ┬ž4.
- **MANUFACTURING-MATERIAL-COST-ROLLUP** Ôťů ÔÇö Multi-cavity BOM material cost roll-up: `compute_material_cost_rollup(parts, material_db, waste_factor)` Ôćĺ `MaterialCostReport`; mass = volume_mm┬│ ├Ś density ├Ś 1e-6 [kg]; gross_mass = net ├Ś (1 + waste_factor); cost = gross_mass ├Ś price_per_kg; aggregation by material type, finishing operation, and cavity supplier; 2025 H1 spot-price baseline DB (LME + Plastics News) for 17 materials (ABS/PP/PC/PA66/PEEK/PLA/Al6061/Al7075/Steel304/316/1018/4140/Cu/Ti6Al4V/GrayIron/CFRP/GFRP); honest advisory: prices fluctuate ÔÇö treat as H1 2025 baseline only; unknown materials zero-costed + flagged; `manufacturing_compute_material_cost_rollup` LLM tool; 26 oracle-asserted tests including Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž8.3 depth-bar oracle (1000├ŚABS@100cm┬│ Ôćĺ $286.00 USD) and Al6061 cross-check ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/costing/material_cost_rollup.py` + `material_prices_2025.py`. References: Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬ž8.3 (2010); ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬ž1.3; Tappi T 220 SP-08 (advisory).
- **3-2-1 Auto-fixture layout** Ôťů ÔÇö Asada-By (1985) ┬ž5 form-closure rank analysis; 6-locator placement (P1-P3 primary, P4-P5 secondary, P6 tertiary) on AABB workpiece; constraint matrix rank-6 validation; clamp-force estimates (material ├Ś operation); ASME B5.18-2018 compliant. `manufacturing_auto_fixture_layout` LLM tool. **Asada-By ┬ž6 form-closure / force-closure** Ôťů ÔÇö `check_form_closure(contacts) -> FormClosureReport` and `check_force_closure_with_friction(contacts, mu) -> ForceClosureReport`; `ContactPoint` dataclass (position_xyz_mm, normal_xyz, is_friction); frictionless wrench-set LP span test (12 canonical disturbance wrenches, revised-simplex Phase I / big-M solver); Coulomb 4-edge friction-cone expansion (n ┬▒ ╬╝┬Ět1, n ┬▒ ╬╝┬Ět2); margin = min LP slack over all 12 directions; missing_dof_directions list when not closed. Classical results: 3 parallel-normal contacts Ôćĺ NOT closed (missing Ôëą 3 DoF including ÔłĺFz); 6 orthogonal opposing contacts Ôćĺ form-closed; 4 frictional contacts ╬╝=0.3 on 4 faces Ôćĺ force-closed; ╬╝=0 degenerates to frictionless. References: Asada & By (1985) IEEE J. Robot. Autom. ┬ž6; Reuleaux (1875) ┬ž2; Murray, Li & Sastry (1994) Ch. 5; Mishra et al. IJRR (1987).
- **CAM G-code emitter** Ôťů ÔÇö `cam_gcode_emit.py`: emit Fanuc-compatible RS-274 G-code from a waypoint toolpath (G00 rapid / G01 linear / G02 CW arc / G03 CCW arc / M03 spindle-on / M05 spindle-off / M06 tool change; I/J centre offsets; F feedrate modal; S spindle modal); `GcodeProgram` dataclass; `emit_gcode()` pure-Python function; `cam_emit_gcode` LLM tool. Round-trips through `parse_gcode`. Dialect: Fanuc 0i/18i/Haas/GRBL Ôëą 1.1. Honest limit: XY-plane arcs only (G17); LinuxCNC %, Heidenhain TCPM, Siemens TRAORI out of scope. References: NIST RS-274/NGC (Kramer et al. 2000) ┬ž3.4ÔÇô3.8; Smid CNC Programming Handbook (2008) ┬ž3. 44 tests.
- **CAM lathe profile G-code emitter** Ôťů ÔÇö `cam_lathe_profile.py`: emit complete Fanuc RS-274 lathe program from a 2-D axis-symmetric profile (XZ polyline); G71 rough turning cycle (P/Q/U/W/D/F/S words), G70 finish turning cycle, G96 constant surface speed, G97 constant RPM, M03/M05 spindle on/off, M06 tool change; `LatheProgram` dataclass; `emit_lathe_gcode(profile, stock, tool_id, sfm=600, ipr=0.25)` pure-Python; `cam_emit_lathe_gcode` LLM tool registered. Depth bar: cylinder ├ś20Ôćĺ├ś10 step + tapered profile emit valid G71+G70 with stock allowance, 600 SFM steel, 0.25 mm/rev IPR; diameter programming (X = 2├Śradius); G18 ZX-plane preamble. Honest flag: Fanuc 0i-TF/30i dialect ONLY ÔÇö Heidenhain TURN PLUS, Siemens ShopTurn CYCLE95, Mazak SmoothTurn, Okuma OSP lathe codes out of scope; G71 Type I only (monotone-decreasing X; concave features warned). References: NIST RS-274/NGC (Kramer et al. 2000) ┬ž3.4ÔÇô3.9; Smid CNC Programming Handbook (2008) ┬ž6; Fanuc 0i-TF OM ┬ž14.2/14.3. 47 tests.
- **CAM wire-EDM path** Ôťů ÔÇö `cam_wire_edm_path.py`: Fanuc wire-EDM G-code from a 2-D profile (line + arc segments); G41/G42 cutter compensation (D-register = wire_radius + spark_gap; typical 0.135ÔÇô0.150 mm); M50/M51 wire feed on/off; G01/G02/G03 with I/J; straight lead-in for safe compensation activation; `WireEDMProgram` dataclass; `square_profile` + `circle_profile` convenience builders; `cam_emit_wire_edm_gcode` LLM tool. Depth bar: 50├Ś50 mm square Ôćĺ D=0.1500 mm (wire 0.25 mm, gap 0.025 mm); circle Ôćĺ G03 I/J=-25./I/J=+25.; all 46 tests green. Honest limits: 2-axis (XY) only ÔÇö no wire taper (4-axis U/V), no threading hole automation, no skim passes, no variable-feed corners. Refs: Tlusty 2000 ┬ž13; Fanuc B-59064EN/01; Rajurkar et al. CIRP Annals 62(2):779-801.
- **CAM lead-in / lead-out arc segments** Ôťů ÔÇö `lead_in_out.py`: tangent-arc, line, and perpendicular lead-in/lead-out G-code segments for 2D contour milling; eliminates witness marks at cutter entry/exit (MH 31e ┬ž1131); `LeadSpec` + `LeadResult` dataclasses; `generate_lead_in_out(spec, cutter_comp)` ÔÇö arc type: G02/G03 with I/J offsets (Fanuc incremental arc-centre convention), lead-in angle ╬▒ (1ÔÇô90┬░, 90┬░ = classic perpendicular tangent entry), lead-in length = R┬Ě╬▒_rad; line type: G01 approach along contour tangent; perpendicular type: G01 from normal offset; G41/G42 cutter compensation activated in lead-in block, G40 cancel in lead-out; `cam_generate_lead_in_out` LLM tool registered; 54 tests green. Honest limits: **2D contours only (XY plane, constant Z)** ÔÇö 3D ramp entry and helical entry are NOT implemented; no gouge/collision checking (use `cam_verify_toolpath_collision`); I/J offsets are incremental/Fanuc convention (verify if using absolute arc-centre mode). Refs: MH 31e ┬ž1131; Fanuc Operator Manual ┬žG41/G42.
- **CAM 3D parallel-offset surface milling** Ôťů ÔÇö `offset_3d_path.py`: `Offset3DSpec` + `Offset3DResult` + `generate_offset_3d_path(spec)` ÔÇö raster (zig-zag parallel passes) toolpath at constant tool_radius Z-offset above a sampled z(x,y) surface grid; scallop height h = R Ôłĺ sqrt(R┬▓ Ôłĺ (ae/2)┬▓) (Chuang & Yang 1995; Held & Klingenstein 1991 ┬ž3.1); bilinear z(x,y) interpolation; G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5 G-code; `cam_generate_offset_3d_path` LLM tool registered; 71 tests green. **Honest limits: 3-axis Z-axis-aligned only** (spindle always +Z vertical ÔÇö no 5-axis tool-axis tilt; steep walls >45┬░ receive slightly less than one tool_radius offset Ôćĺ potential micro-gouge on steep flanks per MH 31e ┬ž1139); **no gouge checking** (use `cam_verify_toolpath_collision`); **no z-level contouring / waterline passes** (raster only); no arc-fitting post-processor (all G01 linear segments); scallop formula is flat-surface approximation only (curved surface deviation not modelled). Time estimate constant-feed only (add 5ÔÇô15 % per MH 31e ┬ž1109). Refs: MH 31e ┬ž1139 (3-axis surface offset); Held & Klingenstein (1991) Computers & Graphics 15(3):333ÔÇô341; Chuang & Yang (1995) Intl J Mach Tools 35(2):261ÔÇô267; NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5.
- **CAM-DRESS-CYCLE-WHEEL** Ôťů ÔÇö `dress_cycle.py`: `DressSpec` + `DressCycleResult` + `generate_dress_cycle(spec)` ÔÇö open-loop grinding wheel dressing cycle G-code generator (traverse dressing); num_passes = ceil(total_dress_amount / depth_per_pass); per pass: G01 infeed X by depth_per_pass Ôćĺ G01 traverse Z across wheel_width at traverse_rate Ôćĺ G00 rapid-retract Z to start; G28 G91 Z0.0 reference return after final pass; G21/G90/G94/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC preamble; `cam_generate_dress_cycle` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 58 tests green. Dresser types: "single_point_diamond" (traverse 50ÔÇô300 mm/min, depth 0.002ÔÇô0.025 mm/pass) + "rotary_diamond" (traverse 100ÔÇô800 mm/min, depth 0.005ÔÇô0.050 mm/pass). HONEST: **open-loop only** ÔÇö no in-process wheel diameter measurement or closed-loop correction (AE sensor, power monitoring, roundness gauging NOT implemented); uni-directional traverse only (+Z per pass, bi-directional oscillation NOT generated); no wheel-spindle synchronisation G-code for rotary roll speed; time estimate constant traverse + 3000 mm/min rapid Z retract only (acceleration ramps excluded, add 10ÔÇô20%); G-code is RS-274/NGC / Fanuc 0i-PD compatible ÔÇö controller-specific dress cycles (Siemens CYCLE12x, ANCA DressPro) NOT emitted; out-of-band advisory if traverse rate or depth outside MH 31e ┬ž1145 safe bands. Refs: MH 31e ┬ž1145 (Wheel dressing); Sandvik Coromant CoroGrind Grinding Handbook ┬ž5 (Wheel conditioning) ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dress_cycle.py`.
- **CAM-MILLING-DWELL-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö `dwell_audit.py`: `DwellAuditSpec` + `DwellAuditReport` + `audit_milling_dwells(spec)` ÔÇö G-code G04 dwell analysis for milling programs; parses every `G04 X<seconds>` (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5) and `G04 P<ms>` (Fanuc/Haas) command; estimates G01 cutting time from line-by-line distance / modal feed rate (G94 mm/min); `total_dwell_time_ms`, `num_dwells`, `dwell_per_op_ms`, `total_program_time_estimate_s`, `dwell_ratio_pct`, `excessive` flag (ratio > `max_total_dwell_ratio_pct`, default 5 %), `suspicious_long_dwells` (> `max_recommended_dwell_per_op_ms`, default 500 ms); modal G20/G21, G90/G91, G94/G95 state tracked; `cam_audit_milling_dwells` LLM tool registered; 45 tests green. HONEST: heuristic only ÔÇö some dwells are deliberate (G89 boring spindle-settle, machine warm-up, coolant-pressure build); `excessive=True` is NOT proof of a programming error; G02/G03 arc moves excluded from cutting-time estimate (inflates dwell_ratio_pct for arc-heavy programs); G95 feed-per-rev blocks contribute 0 to cutting time; rapid rate assumed 10 000 mm/min (generic constant); acceleration ramps add 15ÔÇô30 % to wall-clock time (Altintas 2012 ┬ž5.7). Refs: MH 31e ┬ž1140 (Dwell commands); NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dwell_audit.py`.
- **CAM-G-CODE-ARC-LINEARIZE** Ôťů ÔÇö `arc_linearize.py`: `ArcLinearizeSpec` + `ArcLinearizeResult` + `linearize_arcs(spec)` ÔÇö converts G02/G03 arc commands to G01 linear segments for legacy CNC controllers that do not support circular interpolation (older Mach3 setups, plasma tables, laser cutters, some wire EDM). Supports both I/J centre-offset format and R radius format (R > 0 minor arc, R < 0 major arc per RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5.3); full-circle I/J arcs detected and handled; helical arcs (Z travel on G02/G03) linearised with linear Z interpolation. Segment angle ╬ö╬Ş = 2┬Ěacos(1 Ôłĺ ╬Á/R) per MH 31e ┬ž1130; N = ceil(╬Ş_arc / ╬ö╬Ş); minimum-segment-length floor (default 0.05 mm) prevents degenerate micro-moves on tiny arcs. Returns `linearized_gcode`, `num_arcs_processed`, `total_segments_emitted`, `max_actual_chord_error_mm`, `expansion_ratio`; `cam_linearize_arcs` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 42 tests green. HONEST: **modal G-codes not preserved** ÔÇö each emitted segment carries an explicit `G01`; downstream code must not assume modal state after a linearised arc block; **XY-plane (G17) arcs only** ÔÇö G18/G19 plane selection is passed through but arc maths does NOT adapt (G18/G19 arcs will linearise incorrectly); **full-circle R-format arcs** (start == end) are ambiguous per RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5.3 and are passed through unchanged with a warning comment; feed rate F is copied from the original arc line to every G01 segment (no arc-length-proportional feed correction); helical arcs linearised with linear Z interpolation (geometrically correct for uniform-pitch helices only). Refs: NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5.3; MH 31e ┬ž1130 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/arc_linearize.py`.
- **CAM-MILL-PROFILE-ROUGHING** Ôťů ÔÇö `profile_roughing.py`: `ProfileMillSpec` + `ProfileRoughingResult` + `generate_profile_roughing(spec)` ÔÇö multi-pass 2D profile roughing toolpath that progressively removes material from a closed CCW polygon boundary with adjustable stock offset, leaving a finish allowance for the final pass. Strategy: `num_axial = ceil(total_depth / depth_per_pass)` axial levels; per level, successive radial inward passes from `stock_offset_mm` down to `finish_allowance_mm` (step = cutter_radius = D/2 per pass, outermost Ôćĺ finish-spring pass); polygon offset via vertex bisector / Minkowski-sum approximation (Preparata & Shamos 1985 ┬ž8.4); G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5 G-code; `cam_generate_profile_roughing` LLM tool registered; 76 tests green. HONEST: **2D polygon profile only** ÔÇö no pocket-with-islands (island/internal boundaries not supported); no climb/conventional milling differentiation (all passes use same direction); no helical or ramping entry (plunges at feed rate); no cutter compensation G41/G42 (offsets pre-computed in software); polygon offset is bisector approximation ÔÇö exact for convex profiles, may self-intersect on highly non-convex geometries (use Clipper library for production); time estimate constant-feed only (add 5ÔÇô15 % per MH 31e ┬ž1109). MRR = (stock_polygon_area Ôłĺ finish_polygon_area) ├Ś total_depth. Refs: MH 31e ┬ž1131 (profile milling); Sandvik CoroPlus Contour Roughing (2024); NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/profile_roughing.py`.
- **CAM-DRY-MACHINING-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö `dry_machining_check.py`: `DryMachiningSpec` + `DryMachiningReport` + `check_dry_machining(spec)` ÔÇö dry-machining feasibility checker per Sandvik Coromant Dry/Near-Dry Machining Application Guide (2024) and ISO 8688-1 tool-wear standards. Inputs: `workpiece_material` (8 classes: steel-low-carbon, steel-medium-carbon, steel-stainless-austenitic, cast-iron-grey, aluminum-wrought, aluminum-cast, titanium-Ti6Al4V, nickel-inconel-718), `tool_coating` (uncoated | TiN | TiAlN | AlCrN | diamond-CVD), `vc_m_per_min`, `fz_mm_per_tooth`, `ae_mm`, `ap_mm`, `tool_diameter_mm`, `operation` (milling-roughing | milling-finishing | drilling | turning). Returns: `feasible` (bool), `recommendation` (str), `tool_life_reduction_factor` (1.0 = same as flood; 0.5 = half ÔÇö Sandvik mid-range Taylor-model values), `min_coating_required` (str), `max_vc_dry_m_per_min` (Sandvik catalogue absolute upper limit), `warnings` (list), `honest_caveat`. Rules (Sandvik Coromant 2024 + ISO 8688-1 + Klocke & Eisenbl├Ątter CIRP 1997): cast-iron-grey + carbide Ôćĺ FEASIBLE (factor 0.90ÔÇô1.00; graphite solid lubrication; uncoated acceptable; TiAlN preferred); steel-low-carbon + TiAlN/AlCrN Ôćĺ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.70ÔÇô0.85; max vc 180 m/min dry); steel-medium-carbon Ôćĺ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.65ÔÇô0.80; max vc 150 m/min; AlCrN preferred for hot hardness >900 ┬░C); steel-stainless-austenitic + AlCrN/TiAlN Ôćĺ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.50ÔÇô0.65; max vc 120 m/min; uncoated/TiN NOT acceptable ÔÇö BUE + crater wear); aluminum-wrought / aluminum-cast Ôćĺ NOT FEASIBLE (BUE / chip welding; flood or MQL + diamond-CVD); titanium-Ti6Al4V Ôćĺ CHALLENGING (factor 0.30ÔÇô0.50; MQL minimum required; combustion risk above 60 m/min fully dry per Biermann 2020 ┬ž4); nickel-inconel-718 Ôćĺ NOT FEASIBLE (extreme work-hardening; flood mandatory). Coating adequacy matrix (coating ├Ś material, 40 entries). `cam_check_dry_machining` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_cam/__init__.py`; 59 tests green. HONEST: rules are heuristic averages from Sandvik catalogue + CIRP literature ÔÇö NOT a substitute for chip-form testing; tool_life_reduction_factor uses mid-range Sandvik Taylor-model values, uncertainty ┬▒40 %; actual feasibility depends on machine rigidity, spindle thermal compensation, chip-air evacuation, insert geometry, exact alloy composition, BUE tendency, and surface finish requirement ÔÇö verify against Sandvik CoroPlus ToolGuide before production. Ti6Al4V tool combustion risk above 60 m/min flagged but NOT modelled (physical testing required). Grey cast iron dust/fume hazard requires machine enclosure and extraction. Module does NOT model thermal FEA, chip-evacuation dynamics, or machine-specific spindle temperature behaviour. Refs: Sandvik Coromant Dry/Near-Dry Machining Application Guide (2024); ISO 8688-1:1989; Klocke F. & Eisenbl├Ątter G. CIRP Ann. 46(2) 1997; Biermann D. et al. "Dry and Near-Dry Machining" Springer 2020 ┬ž4 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dry_machining_check.py`.
- **CAM-COOLANT-FLOW-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö `coolant_flow_check.py`: `MachiningOpForCoolant` + `CoolantFlowReport` + `check_coolant_flow(spec)` ÔÇö recommends minimum coolant flow rate [L/min] and pressure [bar] for a CNC machining operation; verifies whether the spindle/through-tool coolant system can deliver them. Flow heuristic: `required_flow = flow_factor ├Ś MRR`; material factors (Sandvik CoroPlus ┬ž3): steel=0.50, stainless=0.60, aluminum=0.30, titanium=0.50, composite=0.20 L/min per cm┬│/min. Pressure thresholds (Sandvik CoroPlus ┬ž3): titanium any coolant Ôëą70 bar; through-tool d>8mm Ôëą20 bar; through-tool dÔëĄ8mm Ôëą10 bar; flood Ôëą2 bar; mist Ôëą4 bar; MQL Ôëą5 bar. Material-specific recommended coolant type: titanium Ôćĺ through_tool (mandatory high-pressure); stainless Ôćĺ through_tool (chip-breaking + heat); steel Ôćĺ flood; aluminum Ôćĺ flood; composite Ôćĺ MQL. `cam_check_coolant_flow` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 41 tests green. HONEST: flow factors are heuristic averages ÔÇö actual requirements depend on ae/ap ratio, specific alloy thermal conductivity, insert grade, and chip volume; coolant chemistry (concentration, pH, biocide), chip-evacuation effectiveness, and nozzle positioning are NOT modelled; high-pressure through-tool channels require spindle + toolholder physically rated for that pressure (seal integrity not checked); MQL/mist flow is lubricant volumetric flow, not flood coolant; composite CFRP/GFRP may require dry or MQL-only machining regardless of flow rate. Refs: Sandvik CoroPlus Coolant Application Guide ┬ž3 (2024); MH 31e ┬ž1140 (Coolant application) ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/coolant_flow_check.py`.
- **CAM chip-load + chip-thinning calculator** Ôťů ÔÇö `chip_load_calc.py`: `MillingOpSpec` + `ChipLoadReport` + `compute_chip_load(spec)` ÔÇö fz = Vf/(n├Śz) (MH 31e ┬ž1136); radial chip-thinning Krad = D/(2┬Ěsqrt(D┬Ěae Ôłĺ ae┬▓)) when ae < D/2 else 1.0 (Sandvik CoroPlus 2024; Stephenson-Agapiou ┬ž6); actual_chip_load = fz ├Ś Krad; MRR = ae ├Ś ap ├Ś Vf / 1000 cm┬│/min; Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 recommended fz ranges (carbide/aluminium 0.05ÔÇô0.15, carbide/steel 0.05ÔÇô0.20, HSS/aluminium 0.03ÔÇô0.10, HSS/steel 0.03ÔÇô0.12, ceramic 0.10ÔÇô0.30 mm/tooth); compliant flag; work_material lookup supports aluminium/aluminum/steel/stainless_303/aluminum_6061; `cam_compute_chip_load` LLM tool registered; 32 tests green. Honest caveats: thinning formula assumes circular arc-of-engagement (flat workpiece, peripheral end-mill only) ÔÇö ball-nose tools, curved workpieces, profiling passes change engagement geometry; no climb/conventional distinction (both use same Krad); tool deflection NOT modelled (see Altintas 2012 ┬ž3.6); recommended ranges are material-class averages ÔÇö verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production. References: MH 31e ┬ž1136; Sandvik CoroPlus Milling/feed-per-tooth (2024); Stephenson-Agapiou ┬ž6.
- **CAM-CHIP-LOAD-VALIDATE** Ôťů ÔÇö `chip_load_validate.py`: `ChipLoadSpec` + `ChipLoadReport` + `validate_chip_load(spec)` ÔÇö validates programmed fz against published Sandvik Coromant / Kennametal / Harvey Tool catalog ranges for 7 specific workpiece materials (steel-1018, steel-4140-soft, stainless-304, aluminum-6061, titanium-Ti6Al4V, cast-iron-grey, plastic-acetal) ├Ś 5 diameter buckets (xs ÔëĄ3 mm, sm 3ÔÇô6 mm, md 6ÔÇô12 mm, lg 12ÔÇô20 mm, xl >20 mm). Chip-thinning using Sandvik simplified formula fz_eff = fz_nom ├Ś D/(2┬Ěae) when ae < D/2 else 1.0. Derived spindle speed n = vc├Ś1000/(¤Ç├ŚD) and table feed = fz├Śflutes├Śn. Warnings: chip-thinning active (factor + effective value), OVER-FEED (effective_fz > fz_max Ôćĺ tool fracture risk), RUBBING/WORK-HARDENING (effective_fz < 60% fz_min), under-feed, high-engagement-at-upper-fz. `cam_validate_chip_load` LLM tool registered; 46 tests green. HONEST: ranges are catalog mid-field averages (Sandvik 2024 + Kennametal 2024 + Harvey Tool 2024) for carbide end-mills with TiAlN coating ÔÇö actual limits depend on insert grade, edge prep, alloy hardness, machine rigidity, holder runout (<5 ╬╝m), and coolant strategy; chip-thinning formula is simplified linear Sandvik approximation (not exact trigonometric form); tool deflection, regenerative chatter, and harmonic excitation NOT modelled (see Altintas 2012 ┬ž3); runout >5 ╬╝m effectively halves per-tooth chip load but is NOT corrected for; ranges apply to peripheral end-milling only (slot-drill, ball-nose, chamfer-mill require manufacturer-specific tables) ÔÇö verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production. References: Sandvik CoroPlus Milling Technical Guide (2024); Kennametal Milling Application Guide (2024); Harvey Tool Speeds & Feeds (2024); MH 31e ┬ž1136 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/chip_load_validate.py`.
- **CAM-DEEP-PECK-LIVE-TIME** Ôťů ÔÇö `peck_live_time.py`: `PeckCycleParams` + `PeckLiveTimeReport` + `compute_peck_live_time(params)` ÔÇö G83 peck-drill cycle live-time analytics: num_pecks = ceil(depth/peck_depth); per-peck model: rapid-down from R-plane to current bore top + feed drilling stroke + rapid-up to R-plane + optional dwell; live_time_fraction = cutting_s / total_cycle_s; adequate flag (threshold 0.50 per Sandvik CoroPlus 2024); separates cutting / retract / dwell times; `cam_compute_peck_live_time` LLM tool registered; 52 tests green. Use: chip-evacuation analysis (low live fraction Ôćĺ heat cycling Ôćĺ accelerated tool wear); tool-life budgeting (cutting-second accounting). Honest caveats: **ideal rigid rapid assumed** ÔÇö no acceleration ramps at peck reversal (real machines add 5ÔÇô20 % retract overhead per Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 ┬žAnnex C servo dynamics); full-retract G83 per NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4 ÔÇö partial-retract G73/Haas-chip-break controllers will yield higher actual live fractions; dwell reported separately (not charged to cutting or retract). References: MH 31e ┬ž1132; Sandvik CoroPlus Drill Cycle Analytics (2024); NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4.
- **CAM** Ôťů ÔÇö 2.5D + 3D parallel/waterline + lathe + 5-axis constant-tilt + 3+2 indexed; tool DB; LinuxCNC/GRBL/Fanuc posts; G83 peck-drilling canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4); G84/G74 rigid tapping canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4 + MH 31e ┬ž1934; `cam_generate_tap_cycle` LLM tool; honest caveat: rigid tap timing only ÔÇö floating tap holders not modelled); G85/G86/G89 boring canned cycles (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4 + MH 31e ┬ž1162; `cam_generate_boring_cycle` LLM tool; G85=feed-out Ra 0.8 ╬╝m, G86=spindle-stop-out Ra 1.6 ╬╝m, G89=dwell-out Ra 0.4 ╬╝m; honest caveat: single-point boring bar only ÔÇö no roughing/finishing pass differentiation; G89 P-word in ╬╝s per NIST vs ms Fanuc); **zig-zag face-mill toolpath** (`face_mill_path.py`): `FaceMillSpec` + `FaceMillResult` + `generate_face_mill_path(spec, climb_milling=True)` ÔÇö rectangular pocket bbox + tool diameter + 70 % stepover (MH 31e ┬ž1136) Ôćĺ full G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5 G-code; climb vs conventional milling; `cam_generate_face_mill_path` LLM tool; 71 tests. Honest limits: 2.5D only (single flat depth); no helical entry; no cutter comp G41/G42; no high-feed (HFC) strategies; no corner arcs at pass reversal; time estimate excludes acceleration ramps (add 5ÔÇô15 %, MH 31e ┬ž1109). **Rigid-tap pre-run check** (`rigid_tapping_check.py`): `RigidTapSpec` + `RigidTapReport` + `check_rigid_tap(spec)` ÔÇö validates a rigid-tap operation against machine spindle synchronisation capability and tap-strength limits; torque T = K┬ĚD┬│ (Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 + MH 31e ┬ž1934 empirical K coefficients: HSS-steel=0.35, cobalt-steel=0.30, carbide-steel=0.25, HSS-aluminum=0.10; 4 materials ├Ś 3 tool classes); feed F = pitch ├Ś rpm; sync_compliant = rpm ÔëĄ machine_max_sync_rpm; tap_breakage_risk (low/medium/high) heuristic: deep hole (>3├ŚD), rpm above material/tool limit, stainless+small+HSS combo; recommended_feed_override_pct; metric (M6x1.0, M10x1.5) + inch UNC/UNF (1/4-20, 3/8-16) thread parser; `cam_check_rigid_tap` LLM tool registered; 58 tests green. Honest caveat: K coefficients ┬▒35 % ÔÇö coolant effects, tap geometry (spiral-flute vs spiral-point), thread-fit class, and worn tool state NOT modelled. References: Sandvik CoroPlus Technical Guide 2024; MH 31e ┬ž1934; NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.8.4.
- **CAM-G-CODE-ARC-LINEARIZE** Ôťů ÔÇö `arc_linearize.py`: `ArcLinearizeSpec` + `ArcLinearizeResult` + `linearize_arcs(spec)` ÔÇö converts G02/G03 arc commands to G01 linear segments for legacy CNC controllers that do not support circular interpolation. Supports I/J centre-offset + R radius formats; full-circle I/J arcs handled; helical arcs linearised with linear Z interpolation. ╬ö╬Ş = 2┬Ěacos(1 Ôłĺ ╬Á/R) per MH 31e ┬ž1130; min_segment_length_mm floor prevents micro-moves; `cam_linearize_arcs` LLM tool registered; 42 tests green. HONEST: modal G-codes not preserved (explicit G01 each segment); XY-plane (G17) arcs only; full-circle R-format arcs ambiguous ÔÇö passed through with warning comment. Refs: NIST RS-274/NGC ┬ž3.5.3; MH 31e ┬ž1130 ÔÇö `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/arc_linearize.py`.
- **Slicing** Ôťů ÔÇö plane-section, CNC layered, 3D-print G-code (Cura, Tier 1).
- **HVAC duct pressure loss ÔÇö ASHRAE ┬ž35 fittings** Ôťů ÔÇö ASHRAE Handbook of Fundamentals 2021 ┬ž35 (Ch. 21) Table 21-1 fitting loss coefficients: 10 fitting kinds (smooth/segmented elbows, 45┬░ elbow, tee branch/through, gradual/abrupt transitions, butterfly damper, gradual reducer/expander); `fitting_pressure_loss()` + `compute_duct_run_pressure_drop()` (straight-duct + fittings combined); `build_loss_table()` with full ASHRAE citations; 2 new LLM tools (`hvac.fitting_pressure_loss`, `hvac.compute_run_pressure_drop`).
- **Slicing** Ôťů ÔÇö plane-section, CNC layered, 3D-print G-code (Cura, Tier 1); infill pattern library (gyroid TPMS, honeycomb, triangular grid, concentric) Ôťů.
- **1D system simulation (kerf-1dsim)** Ôťů ÔÇö Modelica-compatible equation-based DAE solver (BDF-1); R/L/C/MassSpring/Damper/ThermalConductor/FluidResistor components; **Modelica .mo import** Ôťů ÔÇö recursive-descent subset parser: `model/end`, `parameter Real`, `Real`, `equation`, `der()`, `connect()`, `package` wrapping; `modelica_to_kerf_components` mapper; `load_modelica_library` directory scan; `sim_import_modelica` LLM tool registered. *Modelica subset support ÔÇö NOT certified Modelica compliance.*
- **1DSim** Ôťů ÔÇö Modelica-compatible equation-based DAE solver (BDF-1); Modelica import; FMI export; **SPICE 3F5 netlist import + MNA DC analysis** (R/C/L/V/I/Q/M parsing, `sim_import_spice` + `sim_dc_analysis` LLM tools; SPICE subset ÔÇö NOT SPICE-certified, BSIM models out of scope).

### Electronics

- **KiCad-class PCB design** Ôťů ÔÇö ERC, hier-schematic, buses/diff-pairs, net classes/rules, length tuning, via stitching/teardrops, shove router, copper pour, DRC.

- **KiCad-class PCB design** Ôťů ÔÇö ERC, hier-schematic, buses/diff-pairs, net classes/rules, length tuning, via stitching/teardrops, shove router, copper pour, DRC, netlist-vs-layout consistency DRC (IPC-7351B) Ôťů.

- **Wiring/harness** Ôťů ÔÇö WireViz YAMLÔćĺSVG (2D; 3D in flight at P1-7).
- **PLC** Ôťů ÔÇö MATIEC lint Tier 1; PLCopen XML (IEC TR 61131-10) reader/writer (T-220); `import_plcopen_xml` + `export_plcopen_xml` LLM tools; LadderEditor Import/Export buttons wired.
- **Wiring/harness** Ôťů ÔÇö WireViz YAMLÔćĺSVG (2D) + 3D polyline harness routing + formboard-flatten 2D manufacturing output (T-37, P1-7 complete).
- **PLC** Ôťů ÔÇö MATIEC lint Tier 1.
- **Silicon / IC layout** Ôťů ÔÇö VHDL + Verilog parsers; GHDL + Yosys + ngspice bridges; GDS II / OASIS I/O; SKY130 PDK; LEF/Liberty readers; OpenROAD place-and-route; DRC + LVS + parasitic extraction; mask fracturing. T-231..T-248.
- **Firmware / embedded** Ôťů ÔÇö board catalogue (Arduino/ESP32/STM32/RP2040/AVR); library cache; direct-gcc orchestrator (`avr-gcc`/`arm-none-eabi-gcc`/`xtensa-esp32-elf`); upload wrappers; serial monitor panel; LLM tools; cloud Flash via BYO worker Ôťů (esptool/avrdude/openocd dispatched to enrolled workshop machine). T-225..T-230.
- **FIRMWARE-PERIPHERAL-MAP-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö peripheral pin-mapping verifier against MCU hardware alt-function tables; detects: bad alt-function, pin conflict, missing required, peripheral pin-mux conflict, voltage incompatibility (5V tolerant check); embedded STM32F411 LQFP64 alt-function table (RM0383 ┬ž7.3, PA0..PC15) + ATmega328P PDIP-28 (datasheet ┬ž13, all 23 GPIOs); `firmware_verify_peripheral_map` LLM tool; `chip_specs.py` + `peripheral_map_verify.py`; 59 tests. NOT a substitute for ST CubeMX / Atmel Start.
- **Silicon / IC layout** Ôťů ÔÇö VHDL + Verilog parsers; GHDL + Yosys + ngspice bridges; GDS II / OASIS I/O; SKY130 PDK; LEF/Liberty readers; OpenROAD place-and-route; DRC + LVS + parasitic extraction; mask fracturing; SPICE waveform viewer UI Ôťů. T-231..T-248.
- **Silicon / IBIS 7.1 signal integrity** Ôťů ÔÇö IBIS 7.1 model import + eye-diagram estimation (`silicon_import_ibis`, `silicon_eye_diagram`); [Component]/[Pin]/[Model]/[Pulldown]/[Pullup]/[GND_clamp]/[POWER_clamp]/[Ramp]/[Voltage Range]; IV-curve interpolation; analytical eye opening height/width/jitter at arbitrary bit-rate + load. NOT IBIS-certified.
- **Firmware / embedded** Ôťů ÔÇö board catalogue (Arduino/ESP32/STM32/RP2040/AVR); library cache; direct-gcc orchestrator (`avr-gcc`/`arm-none-eabi-gcc`/`xtensa-esp32-elf`); upload wrappers; serial monitor panel; LLM tools. T-225..T-230.
- **FIRMWARE-PERIPHERAL-MAP-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö peripheral pin-mapping verifier; detects bad alt-function, pin conflict, missing required, peripheral mux conflict, voltage incompatibility; embedded STM32F411 LQFP64 (RM0383 ┬ž7.3) + ATmega328P PDIP-28 tables; `firmware_verify_peripheral_map` LLM tool; 59 tests.
- **FIRMWARE-CLOCK-TREE-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö STM32 clock-tree verifier; real PLL arithmetic (VCO = HSE/PLLM ├Ś PLLN; SYSCLK = VCO/PLLP; USB = VCO/PLLQ); detects VCO out of range, SYSCLK exceeded (100 MHz F411 / 168 MHz F407), APB1 > 42 MHz, APB2 > 84 MHz, USB Ôëá 48 MHz (┬▒500 ppm), ADC > 36 MHz; embedded RM0383 ┬ž6 (STM32F411) + RM0090 ┬ž6 (STM32F407) tables; `firmware_verify_clock_tree` LLM tool; `clock_tree_specs.py` + `clock_tree_verify.py`; 71 tests. LOOKUP-TABLE ONLY ÔÇö no jitter/phase-noise model.
- **FIRMWARE-DMA-CHANNEL-CONFLICT** Ôťů ÔÇö STM32 DMA controller channel-assignment verifier; detects: INVALID_ASSIGNMENT (peripheral not legal on stream/channel, with alternatives), STREAM_CONFLICT (two peripherals on same stream), UNKNOWN_CONTROLLER; embedded RM0383 ┬ž10.3.3 Tables 27ÔÇô28 (STM32F411) + RM0090 ┬ž10.3.3 Tables 42ÔÇô43 (STM32F407) stream-channel-peripheral matrices; `firmware_verify_dma_assignments` LLM tool; `dma_specs.py` + `dma_channel_conflict.py`; 64 tests. STATIC CONFLICT DETECTION ONLY ÔÇö no DMA throughput/priority/FIFO model.
- **FIRMWARE-INTERRUPT-PRIORITY-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö Cortex-M NVIC interrupt priority verifier; detects: OUT_OF_RANGE (priority outside [0,15] for STM32F4xx 4-bit field), SAME_PREEMPT_PRIORITY (two peripherals share a preemption level ÔÇö non-deterministic tie-break by IRQ number, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG ┬žB3.3), RT_IN_LOW_BAND (TIM/EXTI in LOW band, pre-empted by NORMAL), NON_RT_IN_RT_BAND (USB/ADC/RTC in RT band), UNKNOWN_PERIPHERAL, BASEPRI_MISCONFIGURED (BASEPRI=0 disables masking, ┬žB1.5.4); PRIGROUP-aware preemption-level extraction (CMSIS NVIC_EncodePriority formula); embedded RM0383 Rev 3 ┬ž10 STM32F411 + RM0090 Rev 19 ┬ž10 STM32F407 IRQ tables; `firmware_verify_interrupt_priorities` LLM tool; `interrupt_specs.py` + `interrupt_priority_verify.py`; 93 tests. STATIC CHECKS ONLY ÔÇö no WCET, RTOS priority-inheritance, or runtime latency model.
- **FIRMWARE-MEMORY-MAP-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö Cortex-M linker memory-layout verifier; detects: FLASH_OVERFLOW (sections exceed chip Flash capacity, RM0383 ┬ž3), SRAM_OVERFLOW (runtime sections exceed chip SRAM capacity), STACK_OVERFLOW_INTO_BSS (stack + .data + .bss > SRAM; conservative static check), VECTOR_TABLE_MISPLACED (vector table base not at Flash start and not in SRAM for VTOR remap, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG ┬žB3.2.4), ISR_COUNT_MISMATCH (vector table entry count != chip NVIC count, RM0383 ┬ž10); embedded memory maps for STM32F411 (512 KB Flash / 128 KB SRAM, RM0383 ┬ž3) + STM32F407 (1 MB Flash / 128 KB SRAM, RM0090 ┬ž3); `firmware_verify_memory_map` LLM tool; `memory_map_verify.py`; 63 tests. STATIC SECTION-SIZE CHECK ONLY ÔÇö does not run the linker; use arm-none-eabi-size + map-file for production audits.
- **FIRMWARE-SPI-TIMING-VERIFY** Ôťů ÔÇö SPI master/slave timing compatibility verifier; checks: master clock_hz ÔëĄ slave max_clk_hz, master setup_ns Ôëą slave min_setup_ns, master hold_ns Ôëą slave min_hold_ns, CPOL exact match, CPHA exact match (Motorola SPI spec canonical CPOL/CPHA definition + ARM Cortex-M Generic UG ┬žSPI Timing); reports clock_margin_pct, setup_margin_ns, hold_margin_ns, violation list; violation codes: CLOCK_TOO_FAST, SETUP_VIOLATION, HOLD_VIOLATION, CPOL_MISMATCH, CPHA_MISMATCH; edge case: MCP3008 ADC at 1.35 MHz max (DS21295D ┬ž1.0 Table 1-1) verified against STM32F411 SPI1 @ 1 MHz; `firmware_verify_spi_timing` LLM tool; `spi_timing_verify.py`; 41 tests. HONEST: assumes ideal square-wave signals; ignores PCB trace propagation delay and crosstalk; use a logic analyser on real hardware.
- **FIRMWARE-I2C-CLOCK-STRETCH-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö I┬▓C clock-stretch worst-case effective speed analyser; computes effective I┬▓C bus frequency when slaves exercise SCL clock stretching and verifies SCL low-timeout compliance; algorithm per NXP UM10204 Rev 7 ┬ž3.1.9: t_byte_effective = (9/f_nom) + stretch_us/1e6; f_effective = 9/t_byte_effective; timeout_compliant = (worst_stretch_us ├Ś bytes_per_txn) < scl_low_timeout_ms├Ś1000; reports effective_clock_hz, worst_case_stretch_per_byte_us, timeout_compliant, slowest_slave, throughput_degradation_pct; `firmware_check_i2c_clock_stretch` LLM tool; `i2c_clock_stretch_check.py`; 36 tests. HONEST: assumes synchronous single-master bus ÔÇö multi-master arbitration NOT modelled; stretch accumulated conservatively on every byte; rise/fall derating and t_BUF overhead not included; verify on target hardware with a logic analyser. Refs: NXP UM10204 Rev 7 ┬ž3.1.9; STM32F411 RM0383 ┬ž26.6 TIMEOUTB register.
- **FIRMWARE-UART-BAUD-DRIFT-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö UART baud-rate drift analyser; given MCU clock (Hz) and UBRR divisor register value, computes actual baud rate and percent drift vs nominal; flags unreliable links (|drift| Ôëą 2%, per RS-232 / IEEE Std 488 baud-rate tolerance); recommends closest standard baud + UBRR combinations that achieve < 0.5% drift with the same clock; ATmega normal mode: baud = clock / (16├Ś(UBRR+1)); double_speed (U2X): baud = clock / (8├Ś(UBRR+1)); standard bauds: [9600, 19200, 38400, 57600, 115200, 230400, 460800, 921600]; `UartConfigSpec` + `BaudDriftReport` dataclasses; `check_uart_baud_drift` function; `firmware_check_uart_baud_drift` LLM tool; `uart_baud_drift_check.py`; 24 tests. HONEST: ATmega integer-divisor model is exact for AVR; for STM32 (fractional BRR register, RM0383 ┬ž19) this model OVER-ESTIMATES drift ÔÇö the STM32 fractional generator typically achieves < 0.1% on standard bauds whereas this integer model reports ~0.94% at 80 MHz / 115200; clock-source tolerance (crystal ┬▒100 ppm, resonator ┬▒0.5%) not modelled; verify on target hardware with oscilloscope or logic analyser. Refs: ATmega328P ┬ž19 (USART); STM32F411 RM0383 ┬ž19; IEEE Std 488.
- **FIRMWARE-FLASH-WEAR-LEVEL** Ôťů ÔÇö MCU flash endurance and time-to-failure estimator for EEPROM-like wear-leveling; given sector layout, write rate, and N-sector wear-leveling pool: total_writes = writes_per_second ├Ś 31,557,600 s/yr ├Ś lifetime_years; sector_erase_events = ceil(total_writes / ceil(sector_size / bytes_per_write)); cycles_per_sector = sector_erase_events / N; adequate = cycles_per_sector ÔëĄ endurance_cycles; time_to_failure_years = endurance ├Ś N ├Ś WA / writes_per_sec / sec_per_yr; recommended_sectors = ceil(sector_erases / endurance); depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB sector (RM0383 ┬ž3, 10k cycles), 1 write/s, 10 yr, 1 sector Ôćĺ 3.15e8 cycles (31,558├Ś over limit, need ~31,558 sectors); same with 100 sectors Ôćĺ 3.15e6 (still 316├Ś over limit); ATmega328P EEPROM (┬ž11, 100k cycles), 0.0001 write/s, 10 yr Ôćĺ 31,558 cycles Ôćĺ adequate; `FlashSpec` + `WriteWorkload` + `FlashWearReport` dataclasses; `compute_flash_wear` function; `firmware_compute_flash_wear` LLM tool; `flash_wear_level.py`; 26 tests. HONEST: assumes perfect uniform wear distribution ÔÇö real algorithms (NuttX MTD, Zephyr NVS, ST EEPROM emulation AN2594) achieve ~80ÔÇô90% of ideal; divide time_to_failure_years by 0.85 for conservative estimate; write amplification is worst-case (one sector erase per logical write); streaming / buffered writes achieve lower WA; temperature derating not modelled (STM32F411 endurance halves at Tj = 125┬░C per RM0383 ┬ž3 Table 6). Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 ┬ž3; ATmega328P ┬ž11; JEDEC JESD47 ┬ž9.
- **FIRMWARE-FLASH-WEAR-LEVEL** Ôťů ÔÇö MCU flash endurance and time-to-failure estimator for EEPROM-like wear-leveling; total_writes = writes_per_second ├Ś 31,557,600 s/yr ├Ś lifetime_years; cycles_per_sector = ceil(total_writes / WA) / N; adequate = cycles_per_sector ÔëĄ endurance_cycles; recommended_sectors = ceil(sector_erases / endurance); depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB sector (RM0383 ┬ž3, 10k cycles), 1 write/s, 10 yr, 1 sector Ôćĺ 3.15e8 cycles (inadequate); ATmega328P EEPROM (┬ž11, 100k cycles), 0.0001 write/s, 10 yr Ôćĺ 31,558 cycles (adequate); `FlashSpec` + `WriteWorkload` + `FlashWearReport` dataclasses; `compute_flash_wear` function; `firmware_compute_flash_wear` LLM tool; `flash_wear_level.py`; 26 tests. HONEST: assumes perfect uniform wear distribution ÔÇö real algorithms (NuttX MTD, Zephyr NVS, ST AN2594) achieve ~80ÔÇô90% of ideal; WA model is worst-case; temperature derating not modelled. Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 ┬ž3; ATmega328P ┬ž11; JEDEC JESD47 ┬ž9.
- **FIRMWARE-RAM-USAGE-AUDIT** Ôťů ÔÇö MCU RAM utilisation auditor; given .data (initialised globals), .bss (zero-inited globals), heap_max_bytes (worst-case dynamic allocation estimate), stack_max_bytes (worst-case stack depth estimate), and total_ram_bytes: static_alloc = data + bss; dynamic_alloc = heap + stack; total_used = static_alloc + dynamic_alloc; free_bytes = max(0, total_ram Ôłĺ total_used); utilization_pct = total_used / total_ram ├Ś 100; within_budget = total_used ÔëĄ 80% of total_ram (10% safety guard for interrupt frames + malloc metadata); recommendation identifies largest contributor when over budget; depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB (RM0383 ┬ž2) data=8KB/bss=16KB/heap=24KB/stack=8KB Ôćĺ 56 KB used, 72 KB free, 43.75% util Ôćĺ adequate; ATmega328P 2 KB (┬ž8) data=500B/bss=1200B/heap=200B/stack=100B Ôćĺ 2000 B used, 48 B free, 97.66% Ôćĺ over budget; `MemorySectionSizes` + `RamUsageReport` dataclasses; `audit_ram_usage` function; `firmware_audit_ram_usage` LLM tool; `ram_usage_audit.py`; 46 tests. HONEST: static estimate only ÔÇö does not account for malloc fragmentation (budget 20ÔÇô30% overhead for general-purpose allocators) or interrupt-driven stack growth (each Cortex-M interrupt frame = 32 B; nested ISRs multiply this); RTOS task stacks not counted unless included in heap_max_bytes / stack_max_bytes; validate stack peak with stack-painting or RTOS uxTaskGetStackHighWaterMark(). Refs: RM0383 Rev 3 ┬ž2 (STM32F411 SRAM map); ATmega328P ┬ž8 (SRAM organisation).
- **FIRMWARE-STACK-DEPTH-ESTIMATE** Ôťů ÔÇö static worst-case stack depth estimator for Cortex-M / ATmega firmware; DFS through the function call graph accumulating per-function frame sizes; detects recursive cycles (back-edges); adds ISR preemption overhead once (default 32 B = Cortex-M3/M4/M7 exception frame: 8 registers ├Ś 4 B, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG ┬žB1.5.6); depth-bar: main(100 B) Ôćĺ A(200 B) Ôćĺ B(50 B) + ISR 32 B = 382 B total; cycle AÔćĺBÔćĺA flagged as has_cycles=True; ATmega variant passes isr_overhead_bytes=3 (PC save only); multiple-callee branching takes deepest path; `FunctionFrame` + `StackDepthReport` dataclasses; `estimate_stack_depth` function; `firmware_estimate_stack_depth` LLM tool; `stack_depth_estimate.py`; 38 tests. HONEST: STATIC ESTIMATE ONLY ÔÇö does not account for VLA (variable-length arrays; makes exact depth undecidable), alloca(), longjmp/setjmp, or indirect calls (function pointers, callbacks); frame sizes must come from arm-none-eabi-gcc / avr-gcc -fstack-usage (*.su files), not guesses; RTOS tasks each have their own stack ÔÇö analyse each task independently; recursive cycles report a per-iteration lower bound only. Refs: ARM IHI 0042F AAPCS ┬ž5.2/┬ž6.1; ARM Cortex-M Generic UG ┬žB1.5.6; Greenwood (2011) "Static Stack Analysis for Embedded Systems" ┬ž3; Brylow et al. (2001) LCTES/OM.
- **FIRMWARE-RTOS-PRIORITY-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö FreeRTOS / Zephyr / ChibiOS task priority assignment verifier; Liu-Layland (1973) rate-monotonic schedulability bound: U = ╬ú CßÁó/TßÁó ÔëĄ n┬Ě(2^(1/n)Ôłĺ1); also evaluates Bini-Buttazzo (2001) tighter hyperbolic bound ╬á(UßÁó+1) ÔëĄ 2; verifies RM priority assignment (shorter period Ôćĺ higher priority integer, FreeRTOS/Zephyr/ChibiOS convention); depth-bar: 2 tasks T1 period=10ms WCET=4ms (P2), T2 period=20ms WCET=8ms (P1) Ôćĺ U=80%, bound=82.84%, schedulable, assignment correct; overload detection with recommendation to reduce WCET or lengthen periods; high-utilisation (>90%) headroom warning; largest contributor advisory; `RtosTaskSpec` + `RtosPriorityReport` dataclasses; `check_rtos_priorities` function; `firmware_check_rtos_priorities` LLM tool; `rtos_priority_check.py`; 43 tests. HONEST: sufficient condition only for independent periodic tasks ÔÇö does NOT model shared resources (PCP/PIP, requires Sha-Rajkumar-Lehoczky 1990 blocking-time response-time analysis), aperiodic/sporadic tasks (Deferrable/Sporadic Server algorithms), interrupt latency, context-switch overhead, or deadlines Ôëá periods (use EDF/DM for DßÁó Ôëá TßÁó). Refs: Liu-Layland (1973) J. ACM 20(1); Bini-Buttazzo (2001) ECRTS; ARM FreeRTOS Kernel Developer Docs; Renesas R01AN5545; Zephyr Scheduling Docs.
- **FIRMWARE-CRC-COMPUTE** Ôťů ÔÇö table-driven CRC checksum engine for embedded protocol verification; 5 algorithms: CRC-8 (poly 0x07, init 0x00), CRC-16/CCITT-FALSE (poly 0x1021, init 0xFFFF, no reflection ÔÇö ITU-T V.41), CRC-16/MODBUS (reflected poly 0xA001, init 0xFFFF ÔÇö Modbus RTU spec ┬ž2.5.1), CRC-32/ISO-HDLC (reflected poly 0xEDB88320, init 0xFFFFFFFF, XOR-out 0xFFFFFFFF ÔÇö IEEE 802.3 Ethernet FCS), CRC-32C/Castagnoli (reflected poly 0x82F63B78, init 0xFFFFFFFF, XOR-out 0xFFFFFFFF ÔÇö iSCSI RFC 3720 / SCTP RFC 4960); official check-vector "123456789" verified: CRC-16/CCITT=0x29B1, CRC-32=0xCBF43926, CRC-32C=0xE3069283; returns crc_hex + crc_int + crc_binary (zero-padded bit-string) + polynomial_hex + honest_caveat; `CRCSpec` + `CRCResult` dataclasses; `compute_crc` function; `firmware_compute_crc` LLM tool; `crc_compute.py`; 66 tests. HONEST: 5 standard algorithms only ÔÇö CRC-64 (ECMA-182, XZ), CRC-16/CCITT-TRUE (init=0), CRC-32/BZIP2 (big-endian), CRC-32/JAMCRC (no output XOR), and bitwise-reflection variants require a separate tool; Modbus CRC register value uses Williams LSB-first convention (low byte transmitted first on wire). Refs: Koopman (2002) FTCS-32; Koopman & Chakravarty (2004) DSN; ITU-T V.41; IEEE 802.3-2018 ┬ž3.2.8; IETF RFC 3720 ┬žB.4; Williams (1993) "A Painless Guide to CRC Error Detection Algorithms."
- **FIRMWARE-PWM-RESOLUTION** Ôťů ÔÇö MCU PWM resolution and frequency-error analyser; given timer clock (Hz), desired PWM frequency (Hz), and counter bit-width (8/10/16/32), searches integer prescaler P Ôłł [1..65536] to find (P, ARR) that maximises achievable resolution_bits = log2(ARR+1) while keeping |freq_error| < 1%; algorithm: ARR = round(clock/(P├Śfreq)Ôłĺ1) clamped to [1, 2^bitsÔłĺ1]; f_actual = clock/(P├Ś(ARR+1)); freq_error_pct = (actualÔłĺtarget)/target├Ś100; oracle: 16 MHz / 1 kHz / 16-bit Ôćĺ P=1, ARR=15999, 13.97 bits; 16 MHz / 20 kHz / 16-bit Ôćĺ P=1, ARR=799, 9.64 bits; STM32F411 100 MHz / 20 kHz / 16-bit Ôćĺ P=1, ARR=4999, 12.29 bits; 100 MHz / 50 Hz / 32-bit Ôćĺ >20 bits; `PWMConfigSpec` + `PWMResolutionReport` dataclasses; `check_pwm_resolution` function; `firmware_check_pwm_resolution` LLM tool; `pwm_resolution_check.py`; 25 tests. HONEST: integer-prescaler model is exact for STM32F411 (PSC Ôłł [0..65535], RM0383 ┬ž13) ÔÇö ATmega328P Timer1 prescaler is discrete {1,8,64,256,1024} (┬ž15), so only those 5 values are legal on ATmega; interrupt latency, dead-time insertion (TIM1/TIM8 BDTR), complementary PWM, and centre-aligned ARR alignment constraints NOT modelled. Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 ┬ž13 (TIM2ÔÇôTIM5); ATmega328P ┬ž15 (Timer/Counter1 Fast PWM, ICR1 mode).
- **FIRMWARE-ADC-EFFECTIVE-BITS** Ôťů ÔÇö ADC Effective Number of Bits (ENOB) calculator with oversampling improvement; base ENOB from SINAD: ENOB = (SINAD_dB Ôłĺ 1.76) / 6.02 (ADI MT-003 Rev. B Eq. 1); or from directly-specified datasheet ENOB; oversampling gain: ENOB_after = ENOB + log2(OSR)/2 (TI SBAA221 ┬ž2.1 ÔÇö each 4├Ś OSR adds 1 bit via ÔłÜOSR noise reduction); voltage resolution: signal_full_scale_V / 2^ENOB_after; recommended OSR for target bits: 4^(target Ôłĺ ENOB) rounded up to next power-of-4; SNR estimate: 6.02 ├Ś ENOB_after + 1.76 (inverse ADI MT-003); depth-bars: SINAD=68 dB Ôćĺ ENOB = (68Ôłĺ1.76)/6.02 Ôëł 11.00 bits; OSR=16 Ôćĺ gain=2.0 bits Ôćĺ 13.00 bits; target 14 bits from ENOB 11 Ôćĺ recommend OSR=64; `ADCSpec` + `OversamplingSpec` + `ADCEffectiveBitsReport` dataclasses; `compute_adc_enob` function; `firmware_compute_adc_enob` LLM tool; `adc_effective_bits.py`; 58 tests. HONEST: oversampling gain assumes white (uncorrelated) noise ONLY ÔÇö correlated noise sources (50/60 Hz mains hum, PSU switching ripple, reference noise, quantisation plateaux on slowly-varying DC signals) DO NOT average out; real-world improvement is typically 0.5ÔÇô1.5 bits per decade of OSR, not the full theoretical log2(OSR)/2; thermal (kT/C) noise of the sample-and-hold capacitor sets an absolute floor; dither injection (low-level white noise added before the ADC) can partially recover theoretical gain by breaking quantisation plateaux. Refs: ADI MT-003 Rev. B; TI SBAA221; Maxim AN2861.
- **FIRMWARE-CONST-ALLOCATION** Ôťů ÔÇö Flash (.rodata, .text) vs RAM (.data initialised constants) allocation analyser for tight MCUs (STM32F411, ATmega328P); input: GCC linker-map symbol list (name, section, size_bytes); Flash sections: .text + .rodata + .init_array + .ARM.exidx; RAM sections: .data + .bss; key metrics: rodata_bytes (Flash constants ÔÇö correct placement), data_init_bytes (RAM-stored constants ÔÇö wasteful, both Flash LMA + RAM VMA consumed); suspect_data_consts: top-10 .data symbols matching ALL_CAPS naming convention (^_*[A-Z][A-Z0-9_]*$) and >= 4 bytes, sorted by size ÔÇö heuristic for likely-constant arrays misplaced in RAM; top_rodata_consumers: top-10 .rodata symbols by size; flash_utilization_pct + ram_utilization_pct; recommendations: data_init_bytes > 1 KB Ôćĺ "move large const arrays from RAM to flash via const-qualifier / section attribute"; flash > 80% Ôćĺ "enable -Os"; depth-bar: STM32F411 (512 KB Flash / 128 KB RAM) LOOKUP_TABLE 2 KB in .data Ôćĺ suspect flagged + const-migration recommendation; 4 KB .rodata on 4 KiB MCU Ôćĺ -Os triggered; `SymbolEntry` + `ConstAllocationReport` dataclasses; `analyze_const_allocation` function; `firmware_analyze_const_allocation` LLM tool; `const_allocation.py`; 41 tests. HONEST: HEURISTIC ANALYSIS ONLY ÔÇö detection based on ELF section placement and ALL_CAPS naming convention, NOT on C/C++ source AST or DWARF type info; a mutable global named 'MAX_SPEED' will be flagged; a const array named 'lookup' will not; .data LMA Flash cost is not separately reported from the symbol map; ARM Thumb literal pools in .text are not included in rodata_bytes. Refs: GCC Internals ┬ž18; ARM IHI 0044F AAPCS ┬ž5.4; RM0383 Rev 3 ┬ž3 (STM32F411 512 KB Flash / 128 KB SRAM); ATmega328P ┬ž8 (SRAM) + ┬ž28 (Flash).
- **FIRMWARE-WATCHDOG-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö firmware watchdog-kick gap analyser; given a task schedule (list of FirmwareTask with period_ms, wcet_ms, priority, kicks_watchdog) and a WatchdogSpec (IWDG or WWDG, timeout_ms, optional window_min_ms), verifies that the independent watchdog is kicked frequently enough across ALL execution paths to never time out ÔÇö even under worst-case latency; algorithm: (1) find slowest kicker (max period), (2) add WCET of all higher-priority non-kicker tasks (blocking time), (3) max_gap = slowest_kicker.period_ms + blocking_time_ms, (4) is_safe = max_gap < timeout_ms; WWDG: also flags kicks earlier than window_min_ms (early-kick reset risk, RM0383 ┬ž20); depth-bar: kicker period=100 ms + blocker WCET=0 ms vs IWDG 250 ms Ôćĺ max_gap=100 ms, margin=150 ms, safe; kicker period=1000 ms vs IWDG 500 ms Ôćĺ violated; WWDG kick=50 ms in window 60ÔÇô100 ms Ôćĺ window violation; `FirmwareTask` + `WatchdogSpec` + `WatchdogCheckReport` dataclasses; `check_watchdog` function; `firmware_check_watchdog` LLM tool; `watchdog_check.py`; 29 tests. HONEST: STATIC SCHEDULE ONLY ÔÇö no IRQ latency, DMA burst, or scheduling-jitter model; assumes ideal fixed-priority preemptive scheduler; shared-resource blocking (PCP/PIP) NOT modelled; WWDG window-minimum uses kicker period as proxy ÔÇö verify on hardware with logic analyser; IEC 61508 SIL-2+ requires challenge-response watchdog in addition to this check. Refs: STM32F4 RM0383 ┬ž19 (IWDG), ┬ž20 (WWDG); IEC 61508:2010 Part 2 ┬ž7.4.3.7; ARM Keil AN259.

### Architecture / BIM

- **`.bim` text-DSL Ôćĺ IFC4** Ôťů ÔÇö walls/slabs/spaces/openings/levels/site.
- **IFC import Tier 1 + 2** Ôťů ÔÇö walls/slabs/spaces/levels/sites + openings/MEP/families/schedules.
- **IFC 4 fa├žade parser + thermal summary** Ôťů ÔÇö extract walls/curtain walls/windows/doors with U-value, R-value, fire rating, structural class; weighted building-envelope U-value; WWR; continuity validation. `kerf-bim/ifc_facade_parser.py`. IFC 4 subset parser ÔÇö NOT buildingSMART certified.
- **Revit parity** Ôťů ÔÇö `.family`/`.schedule`/`.view`/`.sheet`, categories, type-vs-instance, phasing/filters, stairs/railings, MEP, curtain wall.

### Aerospace / composites

- **Applied aerodynamics** Ôťů ÔÇö ISA atmosphere, VLM/thin-airfoil, flight mechanics, propulsion, Breguet range/endurance; 6-DOF; orbital mechanics (Kepler/Lambert/Hohmann); rocket propulsion (CEA-lite); ADCS (quaternion + reaction wheels + magnetorquers); spacecraft thermal network.
- **Composites (CLT)** Ôťů ÔÇö ABD matrix, per-ply stress/strain, Tsai-Wu/max-stress/Hashin failure indices, first-ply-failure, laminate moduli.
- **Composites manufacturing UI** Ôťů ÔÇö `LaminateStackup` (drag-to-reorder ply table, balance/symmetry check, areal-weight + cost rollup, CLT stiffness matrix preview); `AFPToolpathView` (AFP 2D tape-path canvas, cure cycle plot, path-plan dispatch, **Export CNC dropdown Ôćĺ G-code / APT**); `FiberOrientationContour` (HSL contour heatmap, angle tooltip, exploded ply stack, drape sim dispatch). File kinds: `.layup` / `.afp_plan` / `.fiber_map`. Backend routes: `POST /api/composites/clt`, `POST /api/composites/afp` (+ `?format=gcode|apt`), `POST /api/composites/fiber_map`; auth-gated. **AFP CNC export Ôťů** ÔÇö `afp_export.py` (`afp_to_gcode` 5-axis G-code with M200/M201/M202/M203/M204/M205 fibre M-codes; `afp_to_apt` APT/CL ISO 3592 GOTO/FEDRAT/AUXFUN); `composites_afp_export` LLM tool; Fibersim + VeriFiber AFP rows Ôćĺ yes; 79 tests green.
- **Layup angle optimizer (Tsai-Hahn 1980 + Daniel-Ishai 2006)** Ôťů ÔÇö minimize weight subject to Tsai-Wu FPF margin constraint; simulated-annealing search over discrete angles; symmetric + balanced constraint enforced.
- **Aeroelasticity** Ôťů ÔÇö flutter boundary (Theodorsen + p-k method), doublet-lattice.

- **Cross-project parts** Ôťů ÔÇö external_ref, lockfile, derived-artifact cache; derived-cache hit response includes `last_accessed_at` + `cache_key` Ôťů.
- **Cross-project parts** Ôťů ÔÇö external_ref, lockfile, derived-artifact cache; DerivedCacheOverlay mounted (dev-only).
- **kerf-partsgen** Ôťů ÔÇö 5 ISO/DIN family generators shipped.

Standard dimensions from public DIN tables ÔÇö NOT DIN-certified.

| **ELEC-PCB-TRACE-CURRENT-CHECK** | **IPC-2221B simplified PCB trace maximum current** ÔÇö IPC-2221B Eq. 6-4 empirical power-law: I [A] = k ┬Ě ╬öT^0.44 ┬Ě A^0.725 where A [mil┬▓] = trace_width_mils ├Ś (copper_oz ├Ś 1.37); k_external=0.048, k_internal=0.024; copper weights 0.5ÔÇô3 oz/ft┬▓; allowed temperature rise (default 10 ┬░C); `PcbTraceSpec` + `PcbTraceCurrentReport` dataclasses; `electronics_compute_pcb_trace_current` LLM tool. Honest: IPC-2221B simplified formula only; IPC-2152 (2009) has more detailed thermal curves with copper-weight correction (cf_cw), board thermal-conductivity correction (cf_th), and plane-proximity correction (cf_pl) NOT modelled here ÔÇö use `tracecurrent_ipc2152` for the full IPC-2152 model; no temperature-coefficient-of-resistivity correction; worst-case steady-state (no heat spreading from adjacent copper, vias, or pads). | Instant PCB trace ampacity check at design time without needing a full IPC-2152 calculator; catches undersized signal/power traces early. | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö `kerf-electronics/pcb_trace_current.py`, `kerf-electronics/tools/pcb_trace_current.py`; 27 tests |
| **ELEC-PCB-VIA-CURRENT** | **IPC-2152 ┬ž6.3 + IPC-2221A ┬ž6 PCB via current-carrying capacity** ÔÇö barrel cross-section A_barrel [┬Ám┬▓] = ¤Ç ├Ś D_drill_┬Ám ├Ś t_plating_┬Ám (thin-wall annulus, IPC-2152 ┬ž6.3); capacity I_via [A] = 0.048 ├Ś ╬öT^0.44 ├Ś A_mil┬▓^0.725 (IPC-2221B Eq. 6-4, external copper, k=0.048); equivalent 1 oz trace width = A_barrel_┬Ám┬▓ / (34.8 ┬Ám/oz ├Ś 1000); N_vias = ceil(target_current_A / I_per_via) (IPC-2152 ┬ž6.3 Note 2). Dataclasses: `PcbViaSpec` (drill_diameter_mm, plating_thickness_um, via_length_mm, temp_rise_C=10.0, copper_pad_size_mm=1.0); `PcbViaCurrentReport` (max_current_A, via_cross_section_um2, equivalent_trace_width_mm, recommended_via_count_for_target_current, honest_caveat). `electronics_compute_pcb_via_current` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 27 tests green. HONEST: IPC EMPIRICAL MODEL ONLY ÔÇö actual via thermal capacity depends strongly on adjacent copper plane proximity (IPC-2152 cf_pl adds 10ÔÇô30%, NOT modelled ÔÇö result is conservative when a plane is present); resin/copper-filled vias conduct heat better than air-filled (air-filled assumed); dense via arrays suffer mutual heating ÔÇö apply 0.80ÔÇô0.90 derating factor per IPC-7093 ┬ž4.1 for clusters; via barrel length (board thickness) does not enter the IPC-2221B formula (cross-section + ╬öT only). Reference values: 0.3 mm drill / 25 ┬Ám plating / 10 ┬░C Ôćĺ AÔëł23562 ┬Ám┬▓, IÔëł1.80 A/via; 0.5 mm drill Ôćĺ IÔëł2.60 A/via; 5 A target at 0.3 mm/25 ┬Ám Ôćĺ 3 vias needed. Refs: IPC-2152 (2009) ┬ž6.3; IPC-2221A (1998) ┬ž6; IPC-6012 (2020) plating specs; IPC-7093 ┬ž4.1 thermal-via derating ÔÇö `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/pcb_via_current.py`. | Via-count calculation for power delivery and thermal vias without opening a Saturn PCB Calculator tab; catches single-via overloads on high-current power pads. | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö `kerf-electronics/pcb_via_current.py`, `kerf-electronics/tools/pcb_via_current.py`; 27 tests |

HONEST: SQUARE-WAVE FAULT CURRENT ONLY ÔÇö sinusoidal AC or exponentially decaying DC NOT modelled; for AC apply I_rms┬▓ ├Ś t with IEC 60909 asymmetry correction (X/R ratio); arcing I┬▓t NOT included in applied I┬▓t ÔÇö total clearing I┬▓t > pre-arcing I┬▓t; downstream equipment must also survive arcing phase (add 20ÔÇô50% per Bussmann ┬ž3.6); pre-arcing I┬▓t is 25┬░C rated value ÔÇö derate for ambient > 25┬░C per manufacturer temperature correction curve (typically Ôłĺ3% to Ôłĺ8%/10┬░C for silver-element fuses); fuse co-ordination / selectivity between series fuses NOT checked; breaking capacity is rated rms symmetrical AC ÔÇö apply asymmetry factor for DC or high X/R systems (IEC 60909-0 ┬ž11).
