| G-6b | **SUBD-SYMMETRY-DETECT: mirror + rotational + spherical symmetry detection** | Rhino 8 SubD / Blender | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö PCA-based mirror planes (Podolak 2006), n-fold rotational axes (Mitra-Guibas-Pauly 2006), spherical flag; `detect_symmetry(cage) -> SymmetryReport`; continuous-symmetry honest-flag via eigenvalue equality; `subd_detect_symmetry` + `subd_enforce_symmetry` LLM tools; 39 oracle tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_symmetry.py`, `subd_symmetry_tools.py` |
| G-7 | **Render: caustics + dispersion** ÔÇö in-browser path-tracer + Blender Cycles spectral | Cycles / V-Ray / KeyShot | ­čö┤ not started ÔÇö Cycles translator stashes Sellmeier/Abbe coefficients for downstream use but no caustic solver is wired; in-browser path-tracer not started |
| G-8 | **Direct + parametric history coexistence** | Fusion / Inventor / Onshape | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö history mode (direct edit promoted to DAG feature node, replays on upstream changes) + in-place mode; 30+ tests ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/direct_edit.py`, `geom/history/direct_edit.py` |
| G-9 | **Full joint system** ÔÇö rigid/revolute/slider/cam/gear/pin-slot | Inventor / SolidWorks | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö all six joint types with analytic kinematics and drive support ÔÇö `kerf-mates/joints.py` |
| G-10 | **BIM parametric family authoring UX** | Revit | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö `FamilyTemplate` schema + expression evaluator + cycle detection + `generate_body` ÔÇö `kerf-bim/family_authoring.py` |
| G-11 | **BIM family library** ÔÇö curated catalog | Revit | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö 40+ entries across Doors / Windows / Walls / Columns / MEP / Furniture categories ÔÇö `kerf-bim/family_library.py`, `family_library_data.py` |
| G-12 | **BIM walls / doors / windows / slabs full parametric** | Revit | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö `Door` + `Window` + `JambProfile` hosted in walls with IFC mapping; walls/slabs already in core BIM ÔÇö `kerf-bim/openings.py` |
| G-13 | **BIM stairs / ramps full** | Revit | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö multi-flight stairs + winder geometry + code-compliance (IBC/BS/SANS) + ramps + handrails + IFC export ÔÇö `kerf-bim/stairs.py` |

| G-15 | **BIM site / earthwork (toposolids)** | Revit / Civil 3D | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö toposolid B-rep grading + IFC site export ÔÇö `kerf-bim/tools/site_geometry.py`, `kerf-bim/site_ifc.py` |
| G-16 | **BIM material catalogue with render appearance** | Revit / Enscape | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö 40+ materials with PBR properties (`base_color`, `metallic`, `roughness`, `ior`, `transmission`) wired to Cycles translator ÔÇö `kerf-bim/material_catalogue.py` |

### Long-tail verticals

Everything committed, lowest priority. Ordered roughly by near-term readiness.

**Mechanical / product:** cams generators ┬Ě woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist ┬Ě power one-line / switchgear ┬Ě lighting / photometric ┬Ě interior / space-planning / FF&E *(IFC 4 export (ISO 16739-1:2018) Ôťů ÔÇö subset export, NOT buildingSMART certified; `kerf-interior/ifc_export.py`)* ┬Ě kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork ┬Ě landscape ┬Ě scaffolding / formwork.

| Woodworking | Capability | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Joinery geometry validator (Hammer-Krenov) | Validate dovetail (7┬░ÔÇô14┬░ pin angle, Ôëą1/3 board pin width, Ôëą2 pins), mortise-and-tenon (1/3-rule, cheek check, tenon length), box joint (Ôëą3 fingers, equal widths, depth==thickness), finger joint (angle 15┬▒3┬░); strength estimate via FPL Wood Handbook shear values ├Ś joint efficiency for oak/pine/cherry/maple/walnut in kN; `woodworking_validate_joinery` + `woodworking_joinery_strength` LLM tools | Ôťů shipped ÔÇö `kerf-woodworking/joinery_validate.py` |
**Mechanical / product:** cams generators ┬Ě woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist ┬Ě power one-line / switchgear ┬Ě lighting / photometric ┬Ě interior / space-planning / FF&E ┬Ě kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork ┬Ě landscape (plant catalog with USDA + Dirr references, 101 species Ôťů) ┬Ě scaffolding / formwork.

**Vehicles:** composites ply/layup authoring (draping / fiber-steering / Fibersim class) ┬Ě hull fairing (NURBS-reachable) ┬Ě 3D harness routing.

**Civil / infrastructure (distinct engines):** plan-and-profile sheet engine ┬Ě IFC-4.3-infra I/O ┬Ě bridge/tunnel ┬Ě mining ┬Ě marine/dredging ┬Ě rail signaling. *(CRS engine, horizontal/vertical alignment, corridor, earthworks, geotechnical, LandXML 1.2 I/O, pressurized water-distribution networks (Todini GGA + Hazen-Williams/Darcy-Weisbach), gravity sewer (Manning), storm rational method + HDS-5 culverts already shipped; TINView / PipeNetworkView / GradingPlanView / LandscapeView UIs Ôťů 2026-05-29.)*

**Body-worn / medical / craft:** watchmaking / horology ┬Ě eyewear / frames ┬Ě footwear / last design ┬Ě dental CAD (crowns/aligners) ┬Ě orthopedic / prosthetics ┬Ě hearing aids.

**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape ┬Ě technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile ┬Ě upholstery / leather. *(ARAP/LSCM pattern flattening for non-developable surfaces (Bo-Wang 2007 / L├ęvy 2002) Ôťů ÔÇö `kerf-apparel/pattern_flatten.py`, `apparel_flatten_pattern` LLM tool wired.)*
**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape ┬Ě technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile ┬Ě upholstery / leather. *(ASTM D5219 + ISO 8559 grading rules Ôťů ÔÇö `GradingRule`, `build_grading_table`, `apply_grading`, `grade_check_iso_8559` shipped; `apparel_apply_grading` + `apparel_grade_check` LLM tools registered ÔÇö `packages/kerf-apparel/src/kerf_apparel/grading.py`.)*

**Scientific / niche:** microfluidics / MEMS ┬Ě signage / large-format.

**Silicon next:** verification depth + post-silicon (cocotb testbench harness, power analysis, STA, clock-tree synthesis, formal equivalence, Tiny Tapeout / Efabless harnesses). T-249..T-258.

**Firmware next:** RTOS primitives, OTA, RTOS-aware debugger, power profiling, pin-map cross-check vs PCB, USB-class drivers. T-259..T-265. **T-274 Ôťů** ÔÇö Build / Flash / Monitor UI wired: `FirmwareProjectPanel`, `BuildOutput`, `SerialMonitor` in `src/components/firmware/`; `firmware_project` kind renders in Editor; PlatformIO + Arduino IDE compare rows added.

**Aerospace next:** XFOIL-class viscous solver, aircraft conceptual sizing (Raymer/Roskam), stability derivatives, aero-acoustics (FW-H), heat-shield/ablation, aerospace fasteners. T-266..T-272.

**Platform (demand-gated post-launch):** fully-local / offline / no-account desktop app ÔÇö committed but not a launch pillar. Portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the launch answer.

### Strategic AI-native capabilities

These are roadmap-level moats that span every sector simultaneously and compound leverage instead of adding it linearly.

| **PLM depth** ÔÇö configurator, 150% / effectivity BOM, where-used, ECR/ECO, digital thread, MBSE/SysML traceability. File revisions + cloud git + configurations + BOM rollup shipped (partial PLM). **Change Notification Distribution (ISO 10007 ┬ž6.2 + APQP PPAP ┬ž3) Ôťů** ÔÇö `packages/kerf-plm/src/kerf_plm/change_notification.py`; LLM tool: `plm_compute_change_notification`. Stakeholder matrix: engineering (every line), supplier (Class A/B ÔÇö PPAP renewal flagged for dimension/material/process/finish changes), manufacturing_lead (process-spec or part has routes), quality (Class A always; Class B functional triggers), document_control (every line). | **PLM depth** ÔÇö configurator, 150% / effectivity BOM, where-used, ECR/ECO, digital thread, MBSE/SysML traceability. File revisions + cloud git + configurations + BOM rollup shipped. **BOM Cost Roll-up (ISO 10303-44 + APICS "rolled-up cost") Ôťů** ÔÇö `packages/kerf-plm/src/kerf_plm/bom_cost_rollup.py`; LLM tool: `plm_rollup_bom_cost`. Recursive depth-first post-order rollup: `rolled_cost(node) = internal_cost + ╬ú(qty_i ├Ś rolled_cost(child_i))`; `BomNode` dataclass (part_number, name, unit_cost, currency, children, internal_cost); `RollupReport` (total_cost, currency, num_unique_parts, depth, cost_breakdown_by_node, honest_caveat); FX conversion via caller-supplied `fx_rates` dict (default 2025 baseline: USD/EUR/GBP/ZAR/JPY/CAD/AUD/CHF/CNY/INR); cycle detection (ValueError with full path); fractional quantities; multi-currency trees. Honest-flagged: static unit costs only ÔÇö no scrap, overhead absorption, yield-based costing, learning-curve amortisation, or activity-based costing. References: ISO 10303-44:2021 ┬ž5.3; APICS Dictionary 16th ed.; Horngren et al. ┬ž7. 20 hermetic tests green. | Ôťů shipped |
| **PLM depth** ÔÇö configurator, 150% / effectivity BOM, where-used, ECR/ECO, digital thread, MBSE/SysML traceability. File revisions + cloud git + configurations + BOM rollup shipped. **Component Where-Used (ISO 10303-44 + APICS "where-used") Ôťů** ÔÇö `packages/kerf-plm/src/kerf_plm/component_whereused.py`; LLM tool: `plm_component_whereused`. Given a flat list of `BomRelationship(parent_pn, child_pn, qty)` records, performs BFS upward from the queried component to root assemblies; returns `WhereUsedReport` (component_pn, num_unique_parents, num_total_usages, max_depth, entries, honest_caveat) and per-entry `WhereUsedEntry` (parent_pn, parent_name, qty, level); qty aggregation: multiple rows for the same (parent, child) pair are summed; BFS first-visit ensures shallowest level wins for diamond BOMs; cycle detection raises ValueError with full cycle path. Honest-flagged: in-memory traversal only ÔÇö no DB pagination, live PDM sync, effectivity filtering, or path-multiplied extended-qty. References: ISO 10303-44:2021 ┬ž5.3 (next_assembly_usage_occurrence); APICS Dictionary 16th ed. "where-used"; PROSTEP-iViP SIG ┬ž5.2. 17 hermetic tests green. | Ôťů shipped |
| **PLM depth** ÔÇö **ECN Cascading Impact Analysis (ISO 10007 ┬ž6 + APICS "ECN") Ôťů** ÔÇö `packages/kerf-plm/src/kerf_plm/ecn_impact_analysis.py`; LLM tool: `plm_analyze_ecn_impact`. Given an `EcnInput` (ecn_id, affected_components, change_description, urgency) + flat BOM relationships, performs BFS upward from every ECN-affected component to find all transitively affected parent assemblies (deduplicated across components); counts distinct drawings and open work orders linked to affected parents; heuristic cost estimate: `parents├Ś$50 + drawings├Ścost_per_rev + work_orders├Ś$200` (default $150/drawing); ISO 10007 ┬ž6.3.2 implementation class assignment: `Class_I_immediate` (emergency urgency OR Ôëą 20 parents), `Class_II_rev` (normal, 1ÔÇô19 parents), `Class_III_drawing_only` (deferred or zero parents). Honest-flagged: cost formula is heuristic ÔÇö real-world ECN costs vary widely by industry; aerospace/defence drawing revisions can exceed $10 000; consumer electronics may be <$50; use for initial prioritisation only. Class assignment is heuristic; real ECN classification requires change-board review per ISO 10007 ┬ž6.5. 23 hermetic tests green. | Ôťů shipped |
| **PLM depth** ÔÇö **ECN Change-Log Export (ISO 10007 ┬ž6 + PMI PMBOK ┬ž4.6) Ôťů** ÔÇö `packages/kerf-plm/src/kerf_plm/change_log_export.py`; LLM tool: `plm_export_change_log`. `EcnLogEntry` dataclass (ecn_id, summary, approval_date ISO 8601, status draft/approved/in_progress/closed/cancelled, affected_components, urgency emergency/normal/deferred, requester, approver); `ChangeLogExportResult` (csv_content RFC 4180, html_content table with thead/tbody, num_entries, date_range_start, date_range_end, summary_stats {total, by_status, by_urgency}, honest_caveat); `export_change_log(entries, start_date, end_date, sort_by)` ÔÇö optional date-range filter (ISO 8601 bounds, entries with empty approval_date excluded when bounds set); sort by approval_date (default ascending), urgency (emergency first), status, or ecn_id; CSV uses csv.QUOTE_ALL (RFC 4180-compliant; commas in summary safely quoted); HTML table with status/urgency CSS colour cues. ## Genuinely outstanding

*Last verified: 2026-05-26 (status verify-pass against live codebase).* Items that are actually `­čö┤ not started` or meaningfully incomplete after the pass above.

### Tractable soon (weeks, well-scoped)

- **P0-5 viewport integration** ÔÇö LOD planner and lazy-load ordering are implemented in `assembly/perf.py` but not yet wired to the 3D viewport renderer.
- **P0-7 bulk import endpoint** ÔÇö `POST /api/projects/import` (ZIP archive upload); workaround (file-by-file) exists; bulk path not yet implemented.
- **P0-5 real-part catalogue** ÔÇö LOD planner heuristics use synthetic triangle / bbox estimates; wiring to real tessellated part geometry (via `mesh_url` pre-baked buffers) would sharpen tier boundaries for production DMU use.

### Multi-month epics

- **GK-P foundational kernel** ÔÇö general solid boolean for NURBS-faced bodies; Stam limit-tangents Ôťů + G1 at extraordinary SubD points; fractional creases; MatchSrf G3; analytic surface derivatives.
- **GK-P foundational kernel** ÔÇö Ôťů general solid boolean shipped (GK-P-A); remaining: Stam limit-tangents + G1 at extraordinary SubD points; fractional creases; MatchSrf G3; analytic surface derivatives.
- **GK-P Bezier extraction** Ôťů ÔÇö B-spline Ôćĺ multi-Bezier patch decomposition (Piegl & Tiller ┬ž5.6); foundational for FEA tet-mesh handoff, GPU-friendly rendering, IGES export. (`bezier_extract.py`, LLM tool `bezier_extract` registered.)
- **NURBS-CONVERT-TO-IGES-144** Ôťů ÔÇö full IGES 5.3 ┬ž4.27 entity-144 (Trimmed Parametric Surface) writer + reader: `write_iges_trimmed_surface(srf, outer_loop, inner_loops) -> bytes` serialises entity 128 (┬ž4.26 NURBS surface) wrapped by entity 142 (┬ž4.23 Curve on Parametric Surface) outer + optional inner (hole) loops, each referencing entity-126 (┬ž4.22) UV-space B-spline curves. `read_iges_trimmed_surface` returns `TrimmedSurfaceRecord` with `outer_loop`, `inner_loops`, `has_3d_outer/inner` flags and `form` (Form 0). Field-count oracle verified against ┬ž4.27 Table 1 (4 + N2 fields). Hausdorff round-trip oracle ÔëĄ 1e-6 for trimmed plane + circular-hole case. LLM tool `nurbs_export_iges_144` registered (`geom/io/iges_144_tool.py`); 32 tests green.
- **GK-P reparametrisation** ÔÇö Reparametrization (chord-length + centripetal + Foley-Nielsen) Ôťů ÔÇö `geom/reparam.py`; `fit_curve`/`fit_surface` accept `parameterisation` kwarg; LLM tool `nurbs_reparametrize` registered (Piegl-Tiller ┬ž9.2.2).
- **GK-P non-manifold detection + repair** Ôťů ÔÇö `detect_non_manifold` / `repair_non_manifold` for B-rep bodies (T-junction edges, touching-cone vertices, self-intersecting loops) and mesh equivalents; `brep_non_manifold_check` + `brep_non_manifold_repair` LLM tools; `heal_body(repair_non_manifold=True)` integration. (Weiler 1985 / Sheffer-Hart 2002.)
- **GK-P curve lifting** ÔÇö Curve lifting (2D-loop Ôćĺ 3D-on-surface + inverse) Ôťů ÔÇö `geom/curve_lifting.py`: `lift_curve_to_surface`, `lift_curve_with_arc_length`, `project_3d_curve_to_surface_uv`; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_lift_to_surface`; 14 analytic-oracle tests (P&T ┬ž10.3.1).
- **GK-P shell-offset operator** Ôťů ÔÇö shell-offset operator (constant thickness + fillet propagation): `shell_offset_body`, `detect_shell_self_intersection`, `shell_with_open_face`; `brep_shell_body` LLM tool; 47 tests green.
- **GK-P curvature heatmap export** Ôťů ÔÇö `render_curvature_heatmap` / `export_heatmap_png` / `export_heatmap_svg` / `generate_curvature_legend`; viridis + diverging_blue_red palettes; pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_export_curvature_png`, `nurbs_export_curvature_svg`) registered ÔÇö `geom/curvature_heatmap.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CURVATURE-PROFILE-EXPORT** Ôťů ÔÇö ╬║(t) sampled along a NurbsCurve at configurable resolution; exports (1) CSV (t, ╬║, arc_length, x, y, z, high_kappa_risk), (2) SVG plot of ╬║ vs arc-length (inflection markers, high-risk bands), (3) PNG plot (pure-Python encoder, no Pillow); `CurvatureProfileResult` dataclass; `export_curvature_profile` / `export_curvature_profile_result`; LLM tool `nurbs_export_curvature_profile` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; honest-flag `high_kappa_risk` per sample where |d╬║/dt| > 5├Ś mean; **adaptive curvature-weighted sampling** Ôťů ÔÇö `export_curvature_profile_csv(curve, num_samples, adaptive=True, output_path)` implements de Boor ┬žVI / Hoschek-Lasser ┬ž5 curvature-weighted resampling: seed N├Ś10 uniform samples Ôćĺ compute w(t)=|╬║(t)|┬ĚÔÇľC'(t)ÔÇľ Ôćĺ integrate W(t) cumulatively (trapz) Ôćĺ invert at equal-spaced W targets Ôćĺ dense samples in high-╬║ regions; straight-line (╬║Ôëí0) falls back to arc-length uniform; CSV WARNING header suppressed when adaptive=True; 43 hermetic tests (35 original + 8 adaptive: straight-line uniform fallback, kappa-zero on line, denser corner samples, S-curve non-uniform t-spacing, exact count preservation, circle accuracy, no-WARNING header, adaptive max error < uniform) ÔÇö Farin ┬ž11.6, Sapidis ┬ž3, de Boor ┬žVI, Hoschek-Lasser ┬ž5 ÔÇö `geom/curvature_profile_export.py`.
- **GK-P17 SHEET-METAL-FLAT-PATTERN** Ôťů ÔÇö `compute_flat_pattern(part: SheetMetalPart) Ôćĺ FlatPatternResult`; parametric sheet-metal flanges, bends, and unfold-to-flat-pattern with K-factor interpolation from r/t per DIN 6935 / Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" ┬ž3 / ANSI Y14.5M. `SheetMetalPart` dataclass: `material` (steel-cold-rolled|stainless-304|aluminum-5052|copper + aliases), `thickness_mm`, `length_mm`, `width_mm`, `bend_radius_mm`, `bend_angle_deg`, `flange_lengths_mm` (ordered straight segments; bends = lenÔłĺ1). `FlatPatternResult`: `flat_length_mm`, `flat_width_mm`, `bend_allowances_mm` (per-bend BA list), `k_factor`, `total_bend_deduction_mm`, `num_bends`, `honest_caveat`. K-factor interpolation: r/t < 1 Ôćĺ K = k_min (0.33 steel / 0.31 SS / 0.40 Al/Cu); r/t Ôëą 3 Ôćĺ K = k_max (0.44 steel / 0.38 SS / 0.50 Al/Cu); 1 ÔëĄ r/t < 3 Ôćĺ linear. BA = (¤Ç┬Ě╬Ş/180)┬Ě(r + K┬Ět); OSSB = (r+t)┬Ětan(╬Ş/2); BD = 2┬ĚOSSB Ôłĺ BA; flat_length = ╬úflange_lengths Ôłĺ ╬úBD. LLM tool `sheetmetal_compute_flat_pattern` registered via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 33 hermetic tests (K-factor at r/t<1/1/2/3/>3; material alias resolution; single 90┬░ L-bracket KÔëł0.385; BA formula oracle; flat-length formula oracle; flat-width passthrough; 180┬░ hem fold no-raise; stainless thicker bend K; stainless K < mild steel; U-channel 2 bends; U-channel flat-length formula; zero bends single panel; aluminum K_max; copper alias; unknown material / zero thickness / negative radius / angle>180 / empty flanges Ôćĺ ValueError; dataclass field types; honest caveat content; re-export from __init__). HONEST CAVEATS: K-factor is empirical (tabulated DIN 6935 interpolation) ÔÇö measured press-brake data should be used when available; bend-deduction formula assumes inside-set air-bend geometry; bottoming/coining process shifts the neutral axis (see sheet_metal_bend_table.py); spring-back NOT modelled ÔÇö apply overbend to compensate (typically 1ÔÇô3┬░ for mild steel per DIN 6935 ┬ž4); multi-bend interaction for closely-spaced bends (< 4├Śt apart) not captured; flat_width_mm passed through unchanged (no notch/relief geometry modelled). Refs: Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" ┬ž3; DIN 6935:1990; ANSI Y14.5M-2018 ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/sheetmetal_features.py`.
- **GK-P16 NURBS-LOFT-WITH-GUIDE-RAILS** Ôťů ÔÇö `loft_with_guide_rails(spec: GuideRailLoftSpec) Ôćĺ GuideRailLoftReport`; skinning loft through cross-section curves while following N guide rail curves that constrain the surface's intermediate shape (Rhino/Fusion 360 guide-rail loft pattern). `GuideRailLoftSpec`: `cross_section_curves` (Ôëą 2 NurbsCurves), `guide_rail_curves` (Ôëą 1), `num_v_samples` (default 20), `degree_v` (default 3), `closed_v` Ôťů. `GuideRailLoftReport`: `loft_surface` (NurbsSurface), `num_cross_sections`, `num_guide_rails`, `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `num_self_intersections`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm: (1) sample v uniformly at `num_v_samples` stations; (2) interpolate cross-sections by lerp between bounding pair; (3) for each guide rail evaluate rail point at v, compute displacement from interpolated cross-section to guide; (4) blend displacement with Gaussian weight centred at the rail's U-parameter (¤â = 1/(2┬Ěn_rails)); (5) accumulate blended displacements; (6) fit interpolating NurbsSurface via row-then-column B-spline fitting (P&T ┬ž9.4.5). **closed_v=True Ôťů** (P&T ┬ž9.4.5 periodic skinning): samples num_v+1 stations with last==first, fits open surface on extended grid, clamps last degree_v CP columns to first degree_v columns (seam wrap), replaces knots_v with periodic open-uniform vector; warns if first/last cross-sections are not coincident (> 1e-3 mm). `_check_guide_endpoint_alignment` warns (UserWarning) when guide endpoints are > 0.5 mm from the first/last cross-section. LLM tool `nurbs_loft_with_guide_rails` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 39 hermetic tests (all previous + torus/vase circle loop closed_v, periodic knot uniformity, seam CP wrap, mismatched seam warning, coincident seam no warn, vase shape, tilted ellipse loop). HONEST: **approximate** guide-rail constraint ÔÇö Gaussian displacement blend, NOT an exact constrained-NURBS solver; `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm` and `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm` are reported for QC; guide endpoints mismatched from cross-sections trigger UserWarning; exact isogeometric constrained fitting (P&T ┬ž10.5) is out of scope. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž10.3 (skinning) + ┬ž10.4 (Gordon) + ┬ž9.4.5 (periodic skinning); Rhino 8 guide-curve loft docs; Fusion 360 guide-rail loft help ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/loft_guide_rails.py`.
- **GK-P15 NURBS-SURFACE-ANALYTIC-DERIVATIVES** Ôťů ÔÇö `compute_analytic_derivatives(surface, u, v) Ôćĺ SurfaceDerivativeResult`; closed-form ÔłéS/Ôłéu, ÔłéS/Ôłév, Ôłé┬▓S/Ôłéu┬▓, Ôłé┬▓S/ÔłéuÔłév, Ôłé┬▓S/Ôłév┬▓ via Piegl & Tiller Algorithm A3.6 (B-spline tensor-product derivative table) + rational quotient rule A4.4. `SurfaceDerivativeResult` dataclass: `dS_du`, `dS_dv`, `d2S_du2`, `d2S_dudv`, `d2S_dv2` (each a `tuple[float,float,float]`), `gauss_K` = (LNÔłĺM┬▓)/(EGÔłĺF┬▓), `mean_H` = (ENÔłĺ2FM+GL)/(2(EGÔłĺF┬▓)) (do Carmo ┬ž3.2; Mortenson ┬ž6.5), `honest_caveat`. `SSIHardenedMarcher` class: `march(surface_a, surface_b, seed_uv_a, seed_uv_b, step_mm=0.5, max_steps=1000)` ÔÇö differential-geometry SSI marcher (Patrikalakis & Maekawa ┬ž5) with bisection fallback when |n╠é_A├Śn╠é_B| < tangent_threshold (near-tangent robustness). LLM tool `nurbs_surface_derivatives_analytic` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 19 hermetic tests (plane K=H=0, cylinder K=0/H=1/(2R), sphere K=1/R┬▓/H=1/R, Ôłé┬▓S/Ôłéu┬▓ radially inward on cylinder, analytic vs Richardson FD < 1e-8 non-rational, analytic vs FD < 1e-6 rational cylinder, SSI two-cylinder Steinmetz curve, dataclass fields, rational/non-rational caveats, K=H┬▓ sphere identity, bilinear patch exact partials, parameter clamping, SSI cylinder├Śplane circle radius, near-tangent parallel-plane guard). HONEST: curvature NaN at degenerate points (poles, seams where |S_u├ŚS_v| < 1e-12); rational NURBS uses the correct quotient rule (P&T A4.4) but may have large condition number for near-zero weights; SSI marcher traces one branch per seed ÔÇö bifurcation points not handled; bisection fallback is O(step┬▓) accurate but uses more evaluations. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž3.3 (A3.6/A4.4); Patrikalakis & Maekawa ┬ž5; do Carmo ┬ž3.2 ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_analytic_derivatives.py`.
- **GK-P NURBS-DERIVATIVE-FIELD-VISUAL** Ôťů ÔÇö 1st partial-derivative vector-field arrow-plot on NURBS surfaces: `render_derivative_field_png` / `render_derivative_field_svg`; real analytic derivatives at a u/v sample grid (default 12├Ś12) via `surface_derivative`; two-colour encoding (red = ÔłéS/Ôłéu, blue = ÔłéS/Ôłév); proper arrow scaling (longest arrow ÔëĄ cell size); pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_derivative_field_png`, `nurbs_derivative_field_svg`) registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 19 hermetic tests (flat-plane parallel, sphere tangent, PNG magic bytes, SVG structure, scale bound) ÔÇö `geom/derivative_field_viz.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FIT-G2** Ôťů ÔÇö `fit_curve_g2(spec: G2FitSpec, degree=5) Ôćĺ G2FitResult`; fit a degree-5 B-spline curve to a set of 3-D data points with G2 (curvature-continuous) end conditions. `G2FitSpec` dataclass: `data_points` (list of xyz), `start_tangent_xyz`, `start_curvature_xyz`, `end_tangent_xyz`, `end_curvature_xyz`. `G2FitResult`: `fitted_curve` (NurbsCurve), `max_residual_mm`, `mean_residual_mm`, `start_g2_residual`, `end_g2_residual`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm (Piegl & Tiller ┬ž9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10): (1) chord-length parameterisation; (2) clamped knot vector via P&T ┬ž9.2 averaging rule; (3) first three and last three control points fixed analytically from the G1/G2 endpoint formulas (P&T Eqs 9.26ÔÇô9.29: C'(0)=p┬Ě(P_1ÔłĺP_0)/╬ż_{p+1}, C''(0)=p(p-1)┬Ě[(P_2ÔłĺP_1)/╬ż_{p+2}Ôłĺ(P_1ÔłĺP_0)/╬ż_{p+1}]/╬ż_{p+1}; symmetrically at t=1); (4) interior CPs solved by least-squares collocation. Degree Ôëą 2 required for G2; default degree=5. LLM tool `nurbs_fit_curve_g2` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 22 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (straight line residual < 1e-9, circle arc residual < 1e-6, G2 start/end constraints < 1e-9, G1 start/end constraints < 1e-9, 8-point freeform, 12-point 3D, degree-2/3/5, knot clamping, endpoint interpolation, residual non-negativity, residual field parity). HONEST: chord-length parameterisation used throughout ÔÇö centripetal parameterisation (Lee 1989; Foley-Nielsen 1989) may give smaller oscillations for high-aspect-ratio data with large spacing variation and is NOT implemented here. Curvature vectors are *parametric* second derivatives C''(t), NOT the Frenet curvature ╬║(s)┬Ěn╠é ÔÇö for surface-blending use cases, pass the adjacent curve's C''(t) evaluated at the join parameter ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_fit_g2.py`. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10; Lee (1989) CAD 21(6).
- **NURBS-SURFACE-SHEAR-OFFSET** Ôťů ÔÇö `apply_shear_offset(surface, shear: ShearMatrix) Ôćĺ SurfaceShearOffsetResult`; apply a global linear shear-transform (I+S) to all control points of a NurbsSurface: P'_x = x + s_xy┬Ěy + s_xz┬Ěz, P'_y = y + s_yx┬Ěx + s_yz┬Ěz, P'_z = z + s_zx┬Ěx + s_zy┬Ěy (Mortenson ┬ž4.8; Piegl & Tiller ┬ž6.1 Theorem 6.1). `ShearMatrix` dataclass: six off-diagonal shear coefficients (s_xy, s_xz, s_yx, s_yz, s_zx, s_zy; all default 0.0). `SurfaceShearOffsetResult`: sheared_surface, max_displacement_mm, mean_displacement_mm, honest_caveat. Knots and weights preserved exactly. LLM tool `nurbs_apply_surface_shear_offset` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests (identity unchanged, zero displacement, single-axis oracles for all 6 coefficients, combined superposition, knot/weight preservation, rational weight copy, max/mean displacement formulas, maxÔëąmean invariant, ValueError for non-3D CPs, ShearMatrix defaults, input not mutated, honest caveat content). HONEST: global linear shear only ÔÇö non-uniform warp (thermal distortion, springback, gravity sag) requires per-point deformation field, not a single ShearMatrix; displacement stats are control-point displacements, not evaluated-surface deviations ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_shear_offset.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FOOTPRINT-ON-PLANE** Ôťů ÔÇö `project_curve_to_plane(curve, plane_point, plane_normal) Ôćĺ FootprintResult`; orthographic projection of a 3-D NurbsCurve onto an arbitrary plane, producing a planar 2-D NurbsCurve in plane-local UV coordinates. `FootprintResult` dataclass: `footprint_curve_2d`, `projection_axis`, `max_orig_depth`, `honest_caveat`. Each control point projected via P' = P Ôłĺ ((PÔłĺO)┬Ěn╠é) n╠é; degree, knot vector and weights preserved exactly (Piegl & Tiller ┬ž6.1 Theorem 6.1). Degenerate flag when curve is perpendicular to the plane (footprint collapses to a point). `lift_footprint_to_3d` inverse helper. LLM tool `nurbs_curve_project_to_plane` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 17 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (helixÔćĺXY circle radius exact, already-planar identity, vertical-line degenerate, skewed-normal unit-axis, knot/weight/degree preservation, non-rational weights=None, max_orig_depth, projection-formula depth, 45┬░-tilt analytic, make_circle_nurbs round-trip, lift round-trip, ValueError zero-normal, multi-turn helix, YZ-plane analytic). HONEST: orthographic (linear) projection only ÔÇö no perspective; for rational NURBS the footprint is a correct rational NURBS but the Euclidean evaluated curve may differ from a naive point-by-point projection. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬ž6.1; Mortenson ┬ž4.4 ÔÇö `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_footprint_on_plane.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CURVATURE-OSCULATING-CIRCLE** Ôťů ÔÇö osculating circle at any parameter t: `osculating_circle(curve, t) Ôćĺ OsculatingCircle` (center, radius, tangent, curvature, normal_plane_normal, is_degenerate) + `osculating_circles_along(curve, samples)`; ╬║ = |CÔÇ▓├ŚCÔÇ│|/|CÔÇ▓|┬│ (do Carmo ┬ž1.5); degenerate sentinel (╬║=0 Ôćĺ radius=None, is_degenerate=True); LLM tool `nurbs_osculating_circle` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 18 hermetic tests ÔÇö circle oracle (╬║=1/R ┬▒1e-6, center=origin), line oracle (╬║=0, degenerate), helix ╬║=0.5/radius=2.0, parabola vertex ╬║=2/radius=0.5, sample-grid ÔÇö `geom/osculating_circle.py`.
- **NURBS-NORMAL-CURVATURE-AT-POINT** Ôťů ÔÇö normal curvature ╬║_n = II(t,t)/I(t,t) via Meusnier's theorem (do Carmo ┬ž3.2 / Mortenson ┬ž10.4); `normal_curvature_at(srf, u, v, direction_uv) Ôćĺ NormalCurvatureReport` (╬║_n, ╬║_1, ╬║_2, K, H, principal_dirs, is_umbilic, is_degenerate); principal curvatures from characteristic equation of shape operator; Euler's formula ╬║_n(╬Ş)=╬║_1cos┬▓(╬Ş-¤ć)+╬║_2sin┬▓(╬Ş-¤ć) verified; umbilic honest-flag (╬║_1=╬║_2 Ôćĺ principal_dirs=None); LLM tool `nurbs_normal_curvature_at_point` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 32 hermetic analytic-oracle tests ÔÇö sphere K=1/|╬║_n|=1 in 12 dirs, cylinder ╬║_along=0/|╬║_across|=1/R/K=0, saddle K<0/mixed-sign principals, Euler formula bounded in all dirs ÔÇö `geom/normal_curvature.py`.
- **NURBS-FAIR-COMPOSITE-CURVE** Ôťů ÔÇö `composite_fair.py`: `fair_composite(curves, max_iter=50, lambda_smoothness=1.0)` ÔÇö global curvature-variance fairing for poly-NURBS chains; minimises ╬úÔÇľD┬▓PÔÇľ┬▓ (discrete bending energy, Greiner-Hormann 1996 ┬ž3.2) over all segments with per-iteration G1 seam re-imposition (Klass 1980 ┬ž3 bisector) and hard-pinned global endpoints (ÔëĄ1e-6); honest `converged=False` flag for anti-parallel seams or stalled descent; returns `CompositeFairResult` (faired_curves, curvature_variance_before/after, iterations, converged, endpoint_error); `nurbs_fair_composite` LLM tool; 10 hermetic tests ÔÇö 3-segment kink Ôëą50% variance reduction, smooth arc not degraded, endpoints within 1e-6.
- **BREP-CURVE-ON-SURFACE-PROJECTION** Ôťů ÔÇö `geom/curve_on_surface_robust.py`; `project_curve_to_surface(curve, surface, tol, samples) -> CurveOnSurfaceResult`; Newton-Raphson with full 2├Ś2 closest-point Jacobian (second-partial terms, Piegl-Tiller ┬ž6.1 / PM ┬ž3.3); warm-start + coarse-grid seed; near-singular fallback to lstsq; boundary-exit failure detection; UV-trace output as degree-3 NurbsCurve; LLM tool `nurbs_project_curve_to_surface`; 7 hermetic analytic-oracle tests. Honest: no silhouette branch-tracking; Newton stops at local minima; documented.
- **BREP-WIRE-CLOSED-CHECK** Ôťů ÔÇö `geom/wire_closed_check.py`; given an ordered list of B-rep edges forming a wire, verify it forms a closed loop (last vertex connects back to first) and check planarity; used as a pre-condition for face creation. `EdgeSegment` dataclass: `start_xyz`, `end_xyz`, `edge_id`; `WireCheckReport` dataclass: `closed`, `planar`, `max_endpoint_gap_mm`, `num_edges`, `plane_normal_xyz`, `max_out_of_plane_deviation_mm`, `honest_caveat`; `check_wire_closed(edges, tolerance_mm=1e-6)` ÔÇö closed if last.end Ôëł first.start within tol AND every consecutive pair connected; planar via SVD best-fit plane over all endpoints (least singular vector = normal, Pratt 1987; Eberly ┬ž6.6). LLM tool `brep_check_wire_closed` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py _TOOL_MODULES`. 26 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (closed square closed=True/planar=True/normal=(0,0,1), open 3-of-4 closed=False, 3-D zig-zag planar=False/max_oop>tol, triangle closed+planar, hexagon closed+planar, square-at-Z5 planar, collinear degenerate, tetrahedron-outline non-planar, lifted vertex non-planar, tolerance sensitivity, empty ValueError, re-export). HONEST: edge order-dependent ÔÇö scrambled/unordered edge lists are NOT automatically sorted (pass pre-ordered edges only); planarity is endpoint-only (curve interiors are NOT sampled). SubD USD export (USDA ASCII + USDC binary crate) Ôťů ÔÇö `subd_export_usd.py`; `export_subd_to_usda` + `parse_usda_subd` USDA round-trip; `export_subd_to_usdc` minimal-conforming USDC crate writer (header magic PXR-USDC, version 0.6.0, TOKENS/STRINGS/FIELDS/FIELDSETS/PATHS/SPECS TOC sections, uncompressed passthrough payload); `write_subd_usd` auto-dispatches by extension; `parse_usdc_header` round-trip oracle; LLM tool `subd_export_to_usd`; targets HdStorm/Houdini/Maya USD workflows; 24 tests; note: full Pixar usdcat interop requires Pixar C++ library (minimal-conforming subset only). **SUBD-LIMIT-MESH-EXPORT-OBJ** Ôťů ÔÇö `subd_export_obj.py`; `export_limit_to_obj(cage, levels=2, include_normals=True) -> str` + `parse_obj` round-trip; LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_obj`; cube cage 2 levels Ôćĺ 96 quads; face count scales 4├Ś per level; bounding-box convergence verified. Geometry only ÔÇö no MTL; vertex normals via area-weighted cross-product (not Stam exact eigenbasis); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** ÔÇö multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). **SUBD-EXPORT-PLY** Ôťů ÔÇö `subd_export_ply.py`; `export_limit_to_ply(cage, levels=2, format="ascii") -> bytes` + `parse_ply` round-trip; LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_ply`; ASCII and binary_little_endian; valid PLY header (ply, format, element vertex N, property float x/y/z, element face F, property list uchar int vertex_indices, end_header); cube cage 2 levels Ôćĺ 96 faces; binary body compact vs ASCII; sphere cage bounding-box convergence. Honest (v1): geometry only ÔÇö no colour, normals, texture coords; no big-endian; pure-Python struct module. 36 tests. Ref: Turk (1994) Stanford PLY spec. **SUBD-EXPORT-GLTF** Ôťů ÔÇö `subd_export_gltf.py`; `export_limit_to_gltf(cage, levels=2, format="gltf") -> bytes` + `parse_gltf` round-trip; both `.gltf` (JSON + base64 buffer) and `.glb` (binary GLB container) formats; valid `asset.version="2.0"`; POSITION (VEC3 FLOAT) + SCALAR UNSIGNED_INT indices; quads fan-triangulated; GLB magic b"glTF" + version 2; cube cage 2 levels Ôćĺ 192 triangles; vertex/face counts round-trip; sphere cage bounding-box convergence. Honest (v1): geometry only ÔÇö no materials, normals attribute, textures, animations, skinning; no Draco compression; pure-Python (json + struct). 39 tests. LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_gltf`. Ref: Khronos glTF 2.0 https://www.khronos.org/gltf/ **SUBD-EXPORT-STEP** Ôťů ÔÇö `subd_export_step.py`; `export_limit_to_step(cage, levels=2) -> str` + `parse_step_subd` round-trip; valid ISO 10303-21 STEP AP242 ASCII file; FILE_DESCRIPTION + FILE_NAME + FILE_SCHEMA + DATA section; CARTESIAN_POINT / VERTEX_POINT / EDGE_CURVE / EDGE_LOOP / FACE_OUTER_BOUND / ADVANCED_FACE on PLANE surfaces / OPEN_SHELL / SHELL_BASED_SURFACE_MODEL / SHAPE_REPRESENTATION; minimal SI unit context (millimetres); cube cage 2 levels Ôćĺ 96 ADVANCED_FACEs; face count scales 4├Ś per level; sphere cage bounding-box convergence; structural validity verified (header + DATA + ENDSEC). Honest: faceted B-rep ÔÇö each subdivided polygon is a flat PLANE face (STEP has no native SubD primitive); not smooth NURBS. Pure-Python. 38 tests. LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_step`. Ref: ISO 10303-242:2020, ISO 10303-42:2022, ISO 10303-21:2016.
- **GK-P architectural geometry** ÔÇö B-repÔćĺ2D tessellate; roof/curtain-wall/corridor generators; wall compound-layer offset; hatch/section-fill.
- **GK-P sketcher** ÔÇö collinear constraint; ellipse solver entity; G2 continuity. **Parametric sketch constraint solver (Sutherland 1963 / Hoffmann 2001) Ôťů** ÔÇö Newton-Raphson DOF solver with Jacobian numerical differentiation, 10 constraint kinds (coincident/horizontal/vertical/parallel/perpendicular/tangent/distance/angle/equal/on_curve), `check_consistency` (over/under detection via rank), `drag_entity` interactive re-solve, 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_sketch_solver`, `nurbs_sketch_drag`) ÔÇö `geom/sketch_solver.py`.
- **GK-P interop** ÔÇö 3DM write with Hausdorff readÔćĺwriteÔćĺread oracle.
- **T-100 FEM depth** ÔÇö explicit dynamics Ôťů shipped (`kerf_fem/explicit_dynamics.py`); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-╬Á turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue, explicit dynamics are now all shipped.)
- **T-100 FEM depth** Ôťů EPIC CLOSED ÔÇö all sub-tasks shipped: explicit dynamics, full nonlinear static (geometric + material + contact + arc-length), k-╬Á turbulence CFD, coupled-field probabilistic FEA (LHS + Karhunen-Lo├Ęve), plus acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue.
- **Composite curve G2 audit + upgrade** Ôťů ÔÇö `composite_g2.py`: `audit_composite_g2` (per-joint G0/G1/G2 residuals), `upgrade_to_g2` (cubic Hermite / quintic Bezier blend insertion), `composite_curvature_profile` (╬║(s) statistics + jump detection); LLM tools `nurbs_composite_g2_audit` + `nurbs_composite_g2_upgrade` registered; 4 validation test classes (27 tests green).
- **GK-P rational conic detection** Ôťů ÔÇö `detect_conic` / `extract_canonical_circle` / `simplify_curve`; Lee 1987 algebraic LS fit + Piegl-Tiller ┬ž7.2 classification; returns `ConicInfo` (center, axes, radii, eccentricity, focus, plane_normal) for circle / ellipse / parabola / hyperbola; 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_detect_conic`, `nurbs_simplify_conic`); 24 hermetic analytic-oracle tests ÔÇö `geom/conic_detect.py`.
- **GK-P NURBSÔćömesh max deviation** ÔÇö NURBS surface Ôćö triangle mesh Hausdorff distance + per-region max + RMS (Aspert-Santa-Cruz-Ebrahimi 2002 / Cignoni-Rocchini-Scopigno 1998); critical for class-A reverse-engineering acceptance (point cloud Ôćĺ NURBS fit). LLM tool: `nurbs_max_deviation_to_mesh`. Ôťů
- **GK-P auto-lightweight** ÔÇö Auto-lightweight body (Lyche-M├Şrken knot removal + rational simplification) Ôťů ÔÇö `geom/auto_lightweight.py`; `brep_auto_lightweight` LLM tool; 4 hermetic oracle tests.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CIRCLE-FIT** Ôťů ÔÇö fit a circle to a 2D NurbsCurve by least-squares (Kasa 1976 + Taubin 1991); reports center, radius, RMS and max residual; `nurbs_fit_circle_to_curve` LLM tool wired. Caveats: 2D only ÔÇö for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; short arcs (< 30┬░) prefer Taubin. Ref: Taubin (1991) IEEE TPAMI 13(11):1115ÔÇô1138; Kasa (1976) IEEE TIM 25(1):8ÔÇô14.
- **NURBS-CURVE-LINE-FIT** Ôťů ÔÇö fit a straight line to a 2D NurbsCurve via total-least-squares (TLS) / SVD; `LineFitResult(origin_xy, direction_xy, rms_residual_mm, max_residual_mm, is_planar_line, honest_caveat)`; `fit_line_to_curve` + `nurbs_fit_line_to_curve` LLM tool wired; 35 hermetic tests. Algorithm: centroid subtraction + thin SVD; principal right-singular vector = least-squares line direction; perpendicular residuals computed orthogonally. Use cases: linear-segment detection in imported STEP/IGES profiles, snap-to-line in 2D sketcher, near-straight edge classification. HONEST: 2D only ÔÇö for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; for 3D principal-axis fit use 3D SVD separately; direction is undirected (unit vector, sign-canonicalised); sampling is parameter-uniform, not arc-length-uniform. Refs: Press ┬ž15.7 (TLS); Lawson-Hanson ┬ž6 (SVD geometric fitting). `geom/curve_line_fit.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CONIC-DETECT** Ôťů ÔÇö `detect_conic_type(curve_or_points, num_samples=100, residual_threshold_mm=0.01)` returns `ConicDetectResult(conic_type, conic_coefficients, eccentricity, rms_residual_mm, honest_caveat)`; classifies a 2-D NurbsCurve or raw point set as one of: `circle` | `ellipse` | `parabola` | `hyperbola` | `line` | `free_form`. Algorithm: (1) sample `num_samples` 2-D points; (2) line gate ÔÇö if TLS perpendicular-distance RMS < `residual_threshold_mm` Ôćĺ `"line"`; (3) fit the general conic Ax┬▓+Bxy+Cy┬▓+Dx+Ey+F=0 via SVD null-space (smallest right-singular vector), normalised so Frobenius norm of the quadratic block [[A, B/2],[B/2, C]] = 1; (4) if RMS pseudo-geometric residual > `residual_threshold_mm` Ôćĺ `"free_form"`; (5) classify by discriminant ╬ö = B┬▓Ôłĺ4AC: ╬ö < Ôłĺ╬Á Ôćĺ ellipse-family (circle if additionally |B| < ╬Á_c and |AÔłĺC| < ╬Á_c┬Ěmax(|A|,|C|)), |╬ö| ÔëĄ ╬Á Ôćĺ parabola, ╬ö > ╬Á Ôćĺ hyperbola. Eccentricity: 0 for circle, sqrt(1Ôłĺb┬▓/a┬▓) for ellipse, 1 for parabola, sqrt(1+b┬▓/a┬▓) for hyperbola (axes extracted from 3├Ś3 homogeneous conic matrix eigendecomposition). LLM tool `nurbs_detect_conic_type` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 32 hermetic tests (circle r=1, circle r=5, ellipse a=3/b=1 eÔëł0.9428, parabola y=x┬▓/2, horizontal line, tilted line, sinusoid free_form, random free_form, rectangular hyperbola xy=1, coefficient round-trip, raw-point array, threshold gate, degenerate < 5 points). **HONEST CAVEATS**: (1) Algebraic least-squares fit is biased by gradient magnitude ÔÇö for production-quality circle detection use Pratt (1987) or Taubin (1991) in `curve_circle_fit.py`. (2) Parabola detection via discriminant thresholding is fragile near the parabolic boundary for noisy data ÔÇö the ╬ö=0 locus is a measure-zero set. (3) The `rms_residual_mm` is a *pseudo-geometric* residual (algebraic value / gradient magnitude), not the true Euclidean distance to the conic. (4) Line detection uses TLS perpendicular RMS exclusively (degenerate conic Bxy+Dx+Ey+F=0 has nonzero quadratic-block norm, so a separate geometric test is needed). Refs: Pratt, V. (1987) "Direct least-squares fitting of algebraic surfaces." SIGGRAPH ┬ž3; Fitzgibbon, A., Pilu, M., & Fisher, R.B. (1999) "Direct least-square fitting of ellipses." IEEE TPAMI 21(5):476ÔÇô480. `geom/curve_conic_detect.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **BREP-EDGE-FACE-NORMAL-FLIP** Ôťů ÔÇö detect and fix B-rep faces whose outward normals are inconsistently oriented (some inverted) via iterative neighbour-consensus BFS voting. `FaceNormalFlipResult` dataclass: `face_normals_after`, `num_faces_flipped`, `flipped_face_indices`, `consensus_score`, `honest_caveat`. `detect_and_flip_face_normals(faces_with_normals, max_iter=10, threshold=0.15)`: for each BFS edge (AÔćĺB), if dot(n_A, n_B) < -threshold (anti-parallel, indicating face B is inverted relative to the expected co-oriented outward direction of a convex surface) Ôćĺ flip face B. Iterates until convergence. LLM tool `brep_detect_and_flip_face_normals` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 16 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: (1) PERPENDICULAR-FACE LIMITATION ÔÇö adjacent faces with orthogonal normals (|dot|ÔëĄthreshold, e.g. unit cube) produce no flip signal; a cube cannot be corrected from normals alone. (2) Algorithm assumes CONVEX surface convention (adjacent outward normals co-oriented, dot>0); NOT valid for concave surfaces or open flat meshes where inversion produces co-oriented pairs. (3) Isolated faces (no neighbour_face_indices) are returned unchanged. (4) Absolute orientation is seeded from the first face per connected component ÔÇö all-inward input is internally consistent but absolutely wrong. (5) Not a geometric B-rep heal: does not recompute normals from surface derivatives; for production use OCCT BRepLib::OrientClosedSolid. Refs: Mantyla ┬ž6.4; Hoffmann ┬ž3; Weiler 1985 ┬ž3. `geom/face_normal_flip.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **T-100 FEM depth** ÔÇö explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-╬Á turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)
- **T-101 CFD depth** ÔÇö RANS turbulence models; 3-D unstructured meshing; OpenFOAM bridge.

- **T-101 CFD depth** ÔÇö k-╬Á RANS shipped (T-101-A Ôťů); 3-D unstructured meshing (T-101-B, 4L); OpenFOAM bridge depth (T-101-C, 4M).
- **T-100 FEM depth** ÔÇö explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-╬Á turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)

---

## Deliberately not building

This list is only AI-redundant *authoring/UX interaction paradigms* ÔÇö not skipped domains or correctness features.

| Not building | Why |
|---|---|
| Visual node programming (Grasshopper / Dynamo / Sverchok) | The LLM writing a parametric script *is* the graph. `.script.py` + SDKs + JSCAD + `.graph` cover the value. |
| Ribbon / toolbar maximalism | The LLM is the command palette ÔÇö discovery is a chat sentence, not a menu hunt. |
| Macro recorders / scripting-GUI builders | The LLM is the macro author; it writes `.script.py` directly. |
| Gumball / direct-modeling maximalism | Keep a basic gumball; the LLM edits the feature tree. |
| In-app wizards / tutorials / onboarding tours | The chat is the wizard ÔÇö context-specific guidance on demand. |

---

## How to contribute

Pick a task from [`tasks.md`](./tasks.md) (sized for a single isolated agent run), or open an issue proposing a new long-tail sector line. The roadmap states *why* and *in what order*; `tasks.md` is the *how*. Keep them in sync: when a priority moves here, move the corresponding tasks there.
